aſſayed pacyēs lyued c xl yere ꝑ ang greg lix ¶moyſes aboute tyme borne chyldrē iſrael ī grete trybulacyō bondage moyſes put water drowned ¶aron aboute tyme borne ¶dafrus kyng babylon xiiii kynge moyſes borne vnder hym egypt ¶cycrops fyrſt kynge athene ſaynt auſtyn tyme many leſyng • wryten hyſtoryes grekis whiche comynly leſſe comyn fame fa • lytell thynge wrote grete • ere bycauſe ſhewe theyr connynge vnyuerſyte grekys ¶anno mūdi iiimviclxxviii et ante xp̄i natiuitatē mvcxi amynadab ſon̄e aron cryſtes lyne tyme thys amynadab fyrſt moyſes full fayth entred reed ſee dredde whan many hondreth ferde leſte ſholde drowned therfore deſerued brynge forthe kynges lygnage whome deſcended lorde iheſu cryſt moyſes fyrſt iſrael euer iuge xl yere moyſes moſt excellent prophete euer god made mooſt notable wryter ſtoryes louynge heuen erthe ſpekethe ſawe almyghty god clerely face face whiche frayl lyf neuer foū den ſcrypture hym poul thapoſtle ¶aron ye fyrſt byſſhop lyued cxxiii yere aron called god ye dignyte hye preeſt byſſhop ordened ye eternal teſtamēt himſelf al come hym gret power preſthode whā cxxiii yere aege deceſſed buryed hylle hor ſone heleazarus ſucceded hym ye byſſhopryche ¶pharao boccaris tyme kynge egypt pharao wolde cō maūdement god ne delyuer childern iſrael wherfore punyſſhed ten plage vt patꝫ exo hooſt drowned ī ye red ſee naſon ſone amynadab prynce trybe iudas deſerte tyme lawe god gyuen hylle synay boke leuicici wryte another booke called numerū tabernacle ordeyned boke deuteromanū made balaam prophete ſlayne ¶anno mundi iii mviicxxxv et ante xp̄i natiuitatē miiiiclxxiiii salmen lyne cryſt aboute thꝭ tyme wyfe hyght reab moyſes thys tyme deceſſed water frome iordan drye ierico take ſon̄e ſtode fyrmament inmeuable hiſtoria li ioſue fyrſt hyghe byſſhop ab • achar laſte ¶ebaſſam iuge iſrael vii yere xii iuge named wyſe boo ye whiche wedded ruth ¶abialon xii • iuge iſrael iuge x yere vnder theſe tymes ye chyldren iſrael quyete therfore none notable thynges done theſe dayes ¶abdon ye xiiii iuge gouerned iſraell viii yeres aboute tyme hyſtorye ruth wryten ¶authamanis tyme kynge aſſeri • priamꝰ kyng troy ſon̄e lamido • ye buylded cyte agayne merueylouſly ſtrōge began batayl grekes vnto owne hurte ſon̄e called hector leyffull gentyl ſon̄e wyfe eccuba man faythfull wyſe incōparable ſtrēgth noblenes priamus ſon̄e called parys ye whiche toke away fro ye lōde grekes helena wyf nelaiꝰ ye kyng ¶agamenon ye kyng brother menelaius leder al grekes hoſte faught agaynſt troy laſte wanne cyte falſly grekes mooſte ſhame ſclaunder myght certaynly myght called vnhappy batayll man gyueth louynge ye grekes euery man reporteth ſhame ¶eneas kynge ytaly thre yere eneas troye deſtroyed grekes came īto ytaly xx ſhyppes dyde myghty batayles man wedded priamus doughter elinſaram made god thrughe errour comyn people man came iulius cezar octauianꝰ auguſtꝰ ¶vlixes eloquent man amonge ye grekes many perylles ſee wente home hys penelopem mooſte faythfull mooſte chaſte woman radde grekes peryſſhed wretchedly deſtroyed troy bothe water londe wēte home warde ayen ¶and ye pryncypal date theyr wrytynge victory wrote theyr hyſtoryes wrytynges ſic āno primo vel ſecūdo c̄ poſt troiam captam thyrde yere abdon iuge iſraell ¶circa annū mundi iiiimxxv et ante xp̄i natiuitatem mclxxiiii obeth cryſtes lyne ſone boosis reherced ¶sampſon xv iuge regned xx yere ſampſon ye mooſt ſtrongeſt man euer delyuered iſraell ye philiſtiens fro meruaylous ſtrengthe men trowed ben hercules et rius mirabilia oꝑa vide iudicū xiii ¶anno mundi ·iiiimlx • v et ante xp̄i natiuitatem mcxiiii ieſſe ſone obeth lyne cryſte otherwyſe called yſay fad dauyd tyme lyued notable man ī honeſte kyng • egrete gouernour hym many time made mēcyon ī holy ſcrypture hym deſcēded cryſt ſauyour ¶this tyme ely iuge byſſhop iſrael whiche two ſones ophni phinees corrected thē ſuffycyently punyſſhed lorde ſlayne philiſtiens ely felle ſete brake necke ely iuge nexte ſampſon ye lygnage aran fyrſt byſſhop god electe ythamar ye lygnage dured hundred xx yere whiche lygnage ely fyrſte byſſhop abiathar laſt vide plura primo regum thys tyme saul kynge iſraell ye mayſter hyſtoryes ioſephꝰ ·viii boke saul fyrſte kynge iſrael regned xx yere whiche kyng good mā electe god warde wretchedly fayled ſlayne thre ſones hylles gylboy ¶in tyme saull samuel iuge prophete iſrael holy man borne barayne moder many daye mynyſtred afore lorde chylde aege hyghe byſſhop iuged iſrael al dayes lyfe prophete god two kynges anoynted saul fyrſt dauyd ſamuel alone moyſes radde prayed theyr enemyes al ye olde teſtamēt ſamuel saul dyuers oppynyons ¶iſyder ſayth samuel saul ruled iſrael xl yere ¶and ioſepus viii boke ye mayſter ſtoryes ſayth samuel iuge xii yere alone hym saul regne xx yere plura vide primo regū ascanius vii kynge ytaly ſonne eneas buylded cyte alby • n called ye kynge albano rū aſcanius gate siluius viii kynge ytaly whiche siluius fader vnto brute kynge brytayne nowe called englōde leue ye kynges ytaly dyd lytell noble thynges tyll comen romulus remus yt buylded rome ſhall thoſe kynges come agayne nowe procede ye cronycles englonde whiche namely boke made ¶and venes padua buylded aboute tyme reſydue troyans ¶homere grete poete aboute tyme whiche wrote fayned gloryouſly many leſynge ¶incipit regnū britanie nūc dicit ur anglia ¶here may ye ſe london fyrſte began albyon albyon ¶afore wyll ſpeke brute ſhall ſhewed howe londe englonde fyrſt named albyon encheſon ſo named noble londe sirrie ryal kynge myghty man grete renowne called dyocleſyā wel worthely hym gouerned ruled thrugh hys noble cheualry soo conquered londes aboute hym ſo almooſt al kynges ye worlde hym attendaūt ¶it befell thus dyocleſyā ſpowſed gentyl damoyſell wōder fayre vncles doughter labana ſhe loued hym reaſon wolde ſo gate vpō xxxiii daughter whiche ye eldeſt called bine theſe damoyſelles whā came vnto aege became ſo fayre wonder wherof dyocleſyan anone lete make ſomonynge cōmaunded letter ye kynges helde hym ſholde come certayne daye letter conteyned make feeſt ryall whiche daye thyther came brought theym admyralles prynces duke noble chyualry feeſt ryally arayed lyued ioye myrth ynough wonder wyte befell thus dyocleſyan thought mary doughters amonge al tho kynges ſolempnyte ¶and ſo ſpake dyd albine eldeſt doughter al ſyſters rychely maryed vnto xxxiii kynges lordes grete honour power ſolempnyte whā ſolempnyte doone euery kynge toke wyfe ladde theyr owne coūtre made quenes befell thus afterwarde dame albine became ſo ſtoute ſo ſterne ſhe tolde lytell pryce lorde hym ſcorne dyſpyte wolde wyll ſhe wolde haue owne wyl dyuers mater al ſyſters euery chone bare ſo euyl agaynſt theyr lordes wonder wyte moche thē thought theyr huſbondes ſo hyghe parentage come theyr fad thoſe kyngꝭ theyr lordes wolde haue chaſtyſen fayre manere vpō al loue frendſhyp ſholde amende theyr ſelfwylled condycyons noughte dyd theyr owne wyl al thynge thē lyked power wherfore thoſe xxxiii kynges vpon tyme ofte tymes bete theyr wyues wē de wolde amende theyr tatches theyr wyckedneſſe ſuche condycyons fayre ſpeche warnynge dyd ye wors betynges ofte tymes moche wors wherfore kynge wedded albine wrote tatches condycyons wyfe albine ſente lettre dyocleſyan fader whan kynges herde albines lorde hadde ſente lettre dyocleſyan anone ſente letter ſealed theyr ſeales condycyons tatches theyr wyues whan kynge dyocleſyan ſawe herde ſo many playntes doughters ſore aſhamed • became wonder angry wrothe towarde doughters thought howe then̄e myght amende ſo myſdyde anone ſente letter vnto xxxiii kynges ſholde come hym brynge theym theyr wyues euerychone certayne daye wolde chaſtyſe theym theyr wyckedneſſe yf myght ony maner wyſe kynges came tyme day ſette bytwene hym kynges dyocleſyan receyued moche honoure made ſolempne feeſt vnderneth lordſhyp thyrde day ſolempnyte kynge dyocleſyan ſente xxxiii doughters ſholde come ſpeke hym chābre whan come ſpake theyr wyckednes theyr cruelte ſpytefully repreued blamed ſayde yf wolde chaſtyſed ſholde loue loſe euermore whan ladyes herde al became abaſſhed gretly aſhamed theyr fader ſayde wolde make al amendes ſo departed theyr faders chābre dame albine eldeſt ſyſter ladde theym alto chambre made voyde therin ſo perſone amonge theym ſhe ſyſters togyder ¶then ſayd albine fayre ſyſters wel know ye kynge fader v hath reproued ſhame dyſpyſed bycauſe make v obedyen • vnto huſbondes certes ſhall neuer whyles lyue ſythe come hygher kyngꝭ bloode myn huſbonde whan ſhe thus ſayde alle ſyſters ſayd ſame thē ſayd albine well wote fayre ſyſters huſbondes haue cōplayned vnto fader vpō v wherfore hath v thus foule reproued diſpiſed wherfore ſyſter counſell nyghte whan huſbondes ben bede one aſſente kytte theyr throtes thenne may pea beter thynge vnder faders power elles anone ladyes conſented graunted counſell whan nyght comen lordes ladyes went bedde anone theyr lordes ſlepe kette theyr huſbō de throtes ſo ſlewe whan dyocleſyan theyr fader herd thinge became furyouſly wrothe agaynſte hys doughters anone wolde alle haue brente baron lordes sirrie coūſeyled ſo ſuche ſtreytneſſe owne doughters ſholde voyde londe euer ſo neuer ſholde come ayen ſo dyde dyocleſyan theyr fader anone cōmaunded go ſhyppe deliuered thē vytaylles half yere· whan done ſyſters went ſhyppe ſaylled forthe ſee betoke theyr frendes apolin theyr god ſo long ſaylled ſee tyll laſt came arryued yle wylderneſſe whan dame albion come londe ſyſters albyne went fyrſte forth ſhyppe ſayd ſyſters moche ſayde ſhe eldeſt ſyſter company fyrſt londe hathe taken moche myn name albine wyll thys londe called albion myn owne name anone al ſyſters graunted wyth good wyll tho wente oute ſyſters ſhyppe toke londe albyon ther ſyſter called wente vp downe foūde neyther manne woman ne childe wylde beeſtes dyuerſe kyndes whan vytaylle dyſpended fayled fedde herbes fruites ſeaſon yere ſo lyued beſt myghte toke fleſſhe dyuerſe beeſtes became wonder fatte ſo deſyred mannes company mannes kynde thē fayled hete waxed wō der courageous kynde ſo deſyred mānes company ony ſolace myrthe whā deuyll perceyued wē te dyuerſe countrees toke body ye ayre lykynge nature ſhed men cam londe albyon laye tho wym̄en ſhadde tho nature vpon conceyued brought forth gyaūtes ye whiche one called gogmagog longherigam ſo named dyuers name maner came forth borne horryble gyaūtes albyon dwelled caues hylles atte ther wylle hadde londe albyon lykyd vnto ye tyme brute arryued came tornes yle albyon brute cōquered dyſcomfyted gyauntes aboueſayde ¶explicit prima par ¶here begynneth brute goten ſlewe firſt moder fader conquered albyon named brytayne owne name callyd englonde ye name engyſt saxonie ¶this brute came brytayne aboute xviii yere hely knowen noble cytee grete troy noble knyght man grete power called eneas whan cyte troy loſte deſtroyed thrugh grece thys eneas wyth meyne fledde thēs came lombardy thē lorde gouernoure ye londe kyng called latyne kynge called turocelyne ſtrongely warred vpon kynge latyne oftentymes dyde hym moche harme whā kynge latyne herde eneas come receyued hym moche honour helde moche herde hym wyſt wel noble knyght worthy hys body dedes eneas helped kyng latyne ī warre ſhortely telle ſo well ſo worthely dyde ſlewe turocelyne diſcomfyted hym people whan done kynge latyne gaaf londe turocelynes thys noble man eneas maryage wyth lauyne doughter ye mooſt fayreſt creatue ony man wyſt ſo lyued togyder yoy • myrthe dayes ther lyftyme ¶and aſcanius ſone eneas wedded wyf vpon gate ſone called silueyne silueyne whan coude ſome reaſon man vnwetynge fader aenſt wyll aqueyted hym damoyſell coſyn lauyne kynge latynes doughter ye quene eneas wyf brought damayſell chylde whan aſcanius fader wyſt anone lete enqueyre ye wyſeſt mayſters ye gretteſt clerkes chylde domoyſell ſholde brynge forth anſwerde ſayd ſhe ſholde brynge forth ſone ſhalde kylle bothe fader alſo moder ſo dyde moder deyed berynge hym whan childe borne fader lete calle hī brute mayſters ſayd ſholde moche harme ſorowe many dyuers place ſholde come grete honour worſhyp kyng aſcanius deyed whan god wolde silueyne ſone receyued londe made hym wonderly well beloued amonge people ſo whā brute silueynes ſone xv yere olde wente vpon day fader play ſolace brute ſholde haue ſhot vnto herte arowe myſhappe glā ced ſo brute ſlewe hys fader ¶how brute dreuen londe helde hym grece whan myſchaūce befall ye people londe made ſorowe ynough ſore angred enche ſon droue brute lōde wolde ſuffre hym among whā ſawe myght abyde wē then grece founde vii thouſande men lygnage kynred troy come grete blood ſtory telleth men wymmen chyldern whyche hollde thraldome bondage kynge pandras grece dethe achilles betrayed ſlayne troy brute wonder fayre man ſtronge huge age gladde ſemblaunt alſo worthy body well beloued amonge people thys kyng pandras herde ſpeke goodnes condicions anone made hym dwelle wyth hym ſoo brute became wonder preuy moche beloued kynge ſoo longe tyme brute dwelled kynge laſte troy brute ſpake togyders kynred lygnage acquayntaunce playned vnto brute ther ſorowe ther bondage many ſhames kynge pandras done vnto brute ſayde vpon tyme ye lorde lygnage ſtrong man myghty • ye capytayne lorde gouernoure wyll become men cōmaundemē te doo maner thynges brynge v wretchedneſſe bondage wyll fyghte kynge trouthe ye grace grete god ſhal hym ouercome ſhall make kyng londe doo homage ſhall holde euer brute tho grete pyte theyr bōdage brought ī preu • ly wente kynges courte tho troy wente put woodes moūtaynes helde ſente vnto kynge pandras ſholde gyue leue ſauely wē de londe wolde noo l • nger dwelle bondage kynge pandras wexed tho ſore anoyed tho ſwore ſholde ſlee euerychone ordeyned grete power wente warde fyght brute men māly defended fyerfly fought ſlewe kynges men none eſcaped toke kynge helde hym pryſon ordeyned counſell bytwen myghte done ſome ſayde ſholde put dethe ſome ſayde ſholde exiled ye londe ſome ſayd ſholde brēte tho ſpake wyſe kynght called mempris ſayd brute alle tho troy yf kynge pandras wolde yelde hym haue lyf counſell gyue vnto brute duke ſouerayne doughter gennogen wyf maryage wyth hōdred ſhyppes well arayed treſoure golde ſyluer corne wyne moche nede haue • thyng then̄e go londe ordeyned v londe elles nenōe kynred come v ſhall neuer haue pea londe amōge theym grece haue ſlayne ſo many ther knyghtes frēdes euer warre contake ſholde among v brute tho folke conſented well counſeyll thynge tolde kyng pādras haue lyf graū ted moche axed anone gaf vnto brute gennogen doughter wyfe hondred ſhyppes aſmoche neded vytaylles afore ordeyned brute tho toke wyfe men forſoke londe grece went vnto ſee wynde weder theyr wyll came ye thyrde daye ile called lorgers thys brute anone ſente men londe eſpye maner countree founde olde cyte waſted forlet ther nother mā ne woman ne thynge dwellynge mydeell cyte founde olde temple fayre lady called dyana goddeſſe came ayen vnto brute tolde hym ſeen foūde counſelled hym goo doo ſacrefyce vnto dame dyana ſhe wōte yeue anſwere euer men prayed namely vnto honoured ſacrefyce brute wente vnto yamge ſayd dyana noble goddeſſe thynge haſte thy myght power wyndes water woodes felde thynge world manere beeſtes theryn ben make prayer ye counſeyll telle place ſhall haue couenable dwellynge people ſhal make honour well fayre temple noble wherin ye ſhall alwaye honoured whā done prayer dyana anſwerd maner brute ſayde ſhe go euen forth thy waye ouer ſee io frauce warde weſt ye ſhall fynde yle called albyon yle compaſſed wyth ſee noo man maye come ther ſhyppes londe wonte dwelle gyauntes ſoo wyldernes londe deſtenyed ordeyned people ¶how corin became brute man kynge goffar dyſcomfyted thenne whan brute anſwere dyana goddes anone lete ye ancres wynde vp ſayled hyghe ſee whan men ſaylled xx dayes moo foūde faſt beſyed coſt ye ſee thouſande men lygnage kynred troy ther ſouerayne ther mayſter called corin· whan brute wyſte whens tho toke wyth moche ioye hys ſhyppes ladde theym forth wiht hym thꝭ corin came brute man hym dyde homage ſo longe ſaylled forth ſee tyll cam vnto gaſcoyne anone arryued hauen lyegers dwlled viii dayes reſt ther ſaylles amēde nede tydynges ſoone came kynge goffar lorde lōde howe moche people ſtraūge londe arryued lōde ye hauen lyegres wherfore ſore angreged anoyed came arryued londe wythout lycence leue anone ordened hym gret power dryue brute deſtroye hym people ſo kyng goffar dyſcomfyted peple hym ſelf fledde fraūce helpe ſocour tyme regned fraunce ·xii kynges xi aſſembled grete power helpe goffar fight ayeſt brute goffar dwelled thē fraū ce halfe yere meane tyme whan goffar fraūce brute company deſtroyed londe gaſcoyne lete take treſour kyng goffar lete brynge ſhyppes brute founde londe fayry place couenable brute made fayre caſtel ſtronge ¶whan done kyng goffar came fraunce xi kynges hym brought wyth hym xxm men fyghte brute company brute viim ccc men neuertheles whanne two hoſtes mette togyder brute folke thorugh helpe hymſelf turin coſen corin ye well manly hym defended fought ſo tyll lytell tyme hadde ſlayne frenſſhemen two thouſande mo anone alyue fledde awaye bataylle turin brute coſyn ſlayne brute lete entere hym worthely whan ſpace leyſer caſtell made tho lete calle ſame caſtell toures cauſe name turin entred yet vnto day noble cyte called toures kynge goffar wyſte turin deed came agayne men yaue ſtronge bataylle vnto brute brute men ſo wery fyghtynge myght noo lenger endure megre hym brute yede caſtell men made gate faſte ſaue take counſell amoage beſt brute corin gaaf counſell ordeyned pryuely corin ſholde go oute buſſhe ī wood tyll morne ſoo mornynge whan brute ſholde fyghte enemyes thenne corin ſhold come folke one ſyde ſlee harme myght mornynge dawnynge daye brute wē te caſtell fyerſely faughte enmyes manly deffended within lytell tyme brute folke ſlewe viii hondred kynge goffars men thenne came corin ye buſſhement ſmote grounde companye thoſe wolde ſtonde abyde kyng goffar cōpany dyſcōfyted faſte began flee brute corin ther cōpany fyerſely purſewed ſlewe mo ye fleynge dyd ye batayll ī maner brute victory neuertheles brute made moche ſorowe coſyn turī ſlayne alſo haded loſt men ſaye vii· hondred xv whiche nobly entered ſame caſtell toures entered turin coſyn ¶how brute arryued totneſſe yle thenne called albyon bataylle betwixt corin gogmagog whan done brute wolde lenger dwell fyghte leſe moo people kynge goffars people myghte euery daye encreace mo moo brute loſſened therfore toke men wente vnto ſee wende weder theyr wyll fyfth daye arryued hauen totneſſe came yle albyon neyther man woman ſtory telleth founde gyaūtes dwelled hylles caues brute ſawe londe fayre lykynge good alſo hym people dyan goddeſſe hadde hym behyght therfore brute wonder gladde lette aſſembled vpon daye • ol • e make ſolempne ſacrefyce grete feeſt honour reuerence dyana goddeſſe whiche hadde counſeyll fyrſte come londe thenne whan hadde ther ſolempnyte done vpon daye ſate ther meete came vpon xxx gyauntes ſlewe brute men xxx brute men anone ſtrete vp faught gyauntes ſlewe euerychone excepte one called gogmagog mayſter gyauntes ſtrō ger hygher ony brute kepte hym cauſe ſholde wreſtyll wherfore corin ſore angry toke gogmagog betwixt armes caſt hym downe vpon aroche ſoo gogmagog brake peces ſoo deyed euell deth therfore place called vnto daythe ſaute gogmagog ¶and thenne brute yaue alle contree vnto corin corin called name cornewayl • men called cornewaylles ſo ſholde men tha countree called euermore contree dwelled corin hys men made townes howſes enhabyted londe theyr owne wyth moche ſolempnyte glorye londe brytayne whan crowned kynge albanak cambar two brethern wente agayne theyr owne countree lyued moche honour worſhyp lotrī theyr brother regned kynge gouerned well wyſely good man wonderly well beloued londe befell ſo albanak dwelled owne londe moche honoure worſhyp thenne came kynge humbar hunlonde grate power aryued albyne wolde haue conquered londe began hanemos erle cornewayle ordened ſpake bytwene thē ye ſholde departe reame bytwene two dethe kynge leyr theyr fader soo cordeill yongeſt doughter ſholde nothynge haue londe cordeill wonder fayre good condicyons maners kynge fraunce agampe herde fame ſente kynge leyr fader haue vnto wyf prayed hym therof kynge leyr fader ſente hym worde departed londe gyuen hit al vnto two doughters ſayd ſayd lōde wherwith marye whan agampe kynge fraunce herde āſwere ſent anone agayne leyr ſayd axed nothyng oonly clothynge body anone kynge leyr ſente ouer ſee kynge fraunce receyued moche worſhyp ſolempnyte ſpowſed made quene fraunce ¶how kynge leyr dryuen lō de thrugh folke cordeill yongeſt doughter holpe hym nede thus befell afterwarde tho two eldeſt doughters wolde abyde tyll leyr theyr fader deed done laſte thought wolde go cornewayll rigan hys doughter whan come erle wyfe leyrs doughter hym welcomed hym made moche ioye dwelled xxx knyghtes ſquyres dwelled ſcarſly xii monethes doughter wery hym company lorde ſhe hym grete ſcorne deſpyte ſoo xxx knyghtes broughte vnto x afterwarde fyue ſo lefte hym moo thenne made ſorowe ynoughe ſayd ſore wepyng ala euer came londe ſayd yet ye better haue moche ſorowe ſayd ala haue longe lyued ſorowe myſcheyf nowe fallen poore ſomtyme ryche nowe haue noo frende ne kynne wyll ony good whan ryche men honoured worſhyped euery man • athe ſcorne dyſpyte well wote cordeill yongeſt doughter ſayde trouth whan ſhe ſayd moche ſoo moche ſholde loued ye whyle good ſo longe loued honoured ryches two doughters gloſed ſet lytell pryce ſoth tolde cordeil wolde byleue ne vnderſtonde therfore lete goo frome thynge ſette lytell pryce wote neuer ſyth two doughters haue thus dyſceyued ſo moche loued muſt nedes ſeke londe lyghtly lete go without ony rewarde gyftes ſhe ſayde ſhe loued moche ſhe ought loue fader maner reaſon ſholde haue • ed thoſe otherwiſe behoteth thrugh fals ſpeche haue deſceyued thys maner leyr lōge tyme begā make moone ye laſt ſhypped hym ye ſee paſſed ouer fraunce axed aſpyed ye quene myght foūde men tolde hym ſhe was▪ whan came ye cyte ſhe pryuely ſent ſquyre vnto quene tell fader come grete nede whan ſquyre came quene tolde euery deale ſyſters frome begynnynge vnto ende cordeil ye quene anone toke golde ſyluer plenty toke ſquyre coūſell ſholde go bere fader ſholde go certayne cyte hym aray waſſhe come agayne lete lende thrugh al ye realme cōmaunded al men ſholde entendaūt kynge leyr quenes fader maner thynges vnto hymſelfe whā kynge leyr dwelled moneth tolde kynge quene doughter two eldeſt doughters called cloten called kynge cornewayle cloten ſholde haue londe reſon cauſe man wyſte none ſo ryght heyre ſtrongeſt ſette lytel leſſe eſtate therfore cloten hadde noo londe amonge cornewaylle ¶of kynge donebant clotens ſone wanne londe cloten ſone called donebant dethe hys fader became hardy man fayr curteis ſo paſſed al ye kīges fayreneſſe worthyneſſe anōe knyghte wyſte well whā hys fader lyued tyme loued kynge called gutlagh hym ſhe tolde coūſel bren̄e ſholde haue lede hym euer ſo ſholde leſe ſhe myght ſake brenne whan gutlagh herde tydynges lay aſpye bren̄e many ſhyppes myght haue soo two fletes mette togyder longe tyme faught ſoo brennes men tourned ayen dyſcomfyted kynge gutlagh toke samie put ſhyppe brēne ſhamefully fledde then man dyſcomfyted kyng gutlagh wold haue gone owene coūtree came vpon hym ſuche grete tempeſt fyue dayes laſted ſoo thorugh tempeſt dryuen brytayne thre ſhyppes moo tho kepte coſtes ſee toke gutlagh samie folke preſented belin belin put pryſon ¶how belin droue londe kyng gutlagh denmerk samie longe brenne came agayne grete nauy ſent brother belin ſhold yeld ayen londe wyfe folke caſtelles alſo elles wolde deſtroye londe ¶belin dradde noo thyng tarquinꝰ vii kynges ſone aforeſayde came vnto ladyes hous abſente huſbonde ſupper lodgyng whan ſlepe roſe ſwerde hys honde ſtrengthe fere rauyſſhed woman whan gone ye nere daye ſhe ſende vnto fader coude ſayd noo vylany vnto ayenſt wyll anſwered ſayd yet ſhall ther neuer woman excuſe lucre though ſhe cōſented thys dyde yet ſhall ſhe dye without payne dede worde ſhe knyf redy vnder mantell whiche ſhe ſmote herſelf cruelnes pyteous deth peple rome aroſe exiled ye king euer progenye thus ſeaſed theſe kynges rome neuer none gouernaunce rome tyll emperours beganne thys tyraunte deed romayns two choſen ony thē wolde make ony yf exceſſe ſholde gouerne hym theyr thynge obeyed yf conſented bothe alſo ſholde ſtonde ther dygnyte paſſynge one yere thys cauſe domynacyon longe tyme ſholde vſurpe vpon ryght alle thys tyme empyre rome dylated poſſynge xii myle fyrſt conſules made called lucium brutū theſe two men dyde grete thynges theyr time yet ye peple bare heuy theyr domynacyon wherfore brytons ſlewe hym wyckedneſſe gracian whan began regne became ſo wycked ſoo ſterne ſo moche ſorowe dyde brytons yt ſlewe hym amonge ¶tho whan kynge gowan vnderſtode yt gracian ſlayne done dethe aſſembled grete power came ayen londe yf fyrſte done harme tho dyde moche tho deſtroyed londe cryſten peple moche brytayne ſo man ſo hardy name god ſo dyde anone put ſtrange deth ¶but ye byſſhop london called goſſelim ſcaped went then rome ſeke ſocour helpe dyſtroy ſarraſyns hadde deſtryed londe romayns ſayd ben ſo often enoyed ther ſendinge people brytayne helpe brytōs wolde nomore ſoo ſoo byſſhop goſſelin wente then wythout ony ſocoure helpe tho wente kynge lytell brytane called aldroye ye thyrde kynge gowan meryedok ſayde ¶the byſſhop prayed aldroye helpe ſocoure kynge pyte herte whan herde byſſhop fledde cryſten men ſoo ſlayne grete brytayne thrugh ye paynyms ſarraſyns graūted hym cōſtantyne broder helpe wyth power folke dyde arraye hors armour ſhyppes al thynges neded vyage whā al thinge redy called ye byſſhop hym ſayde take cōſtantyne broder vpon couenaū • yf god gyue hym grace paynems ſarraſins deſtroye yt ye make hym kynge byſſhop graūted wyth good wyll ¶conſtantyne byſſhop toke leue ye king aldroye betoke god toke men xii thouſande went ther ſhyppes ſaylled warde grete brytayne arryued totneſſe ¶whan brytons herde theſe tydyngꝭ thē came ſocoure ſtrongely holpen ordeyned thē huge nō bre people came receyued moche honoure ¶gowan anone wyſt theſe tydynges aſſēbled ye sarraſyns cam ayenſt yaue thē batayle • cōſtantyne ſlewe hym owne hō de anone ſpowſyd hys wyf thrugh coūſeyll ye brytōs begate thre ſones fyrſt called cōſtance aurilambros ye thyrde vter cō ſtance elder brother▪ whan cam aege made hym monke atte wyncheſtre conſtantyne ••• togyder ¶circa annū dm̄ ccccxlix¶how wardeyns thoſe chyldern kepe conſtanſtynes ladde theym lytell brytayne treaſon falſeneſſe vortiger hyre begynneth fyfth parte durynge comynge dane thys tyme came ye saxon pagan fyrſte brytane called englonde vnder vortiger whyche crowned kinge londe tyme thoſe yt theſe two childern kepinge ye whyche cō ſtantynes ſons ſaye aurilambros vter thrugh ordynance goſſelin byſſhop london faders deth ſaye conſtantyne durſt dwelle londe thoſe childern conueyed vnto kynge lytell brytayne moche tho wiſt treaſon vortiger tho made kynge thorugh conſtance elder brother ſlayne wherfore hondred knyghtꝭ pehites put dethe bore blame vortiger hadde wyſt ther ne conſented ſo kepers thoſe two chyldern dradde leſt vortiger ſholde put deth thrugh treaſon falſeneſſe done brother therfore ladde ouer lytell brytayn kyng receyued moche honour lete nouryſſhe dwelled tyll became fayre knyghtꝭ ſtronge fyers thourght auenged vpon conſtaunce theyr brother whan ſawe theyr tyme ſo dyde ye ſhalle telle warde ¶it longe warde ye tydynges came ouerſee ye kynred hondred knyghtꝭ pehites dampned put deth thrugh vortiger thys londe therfore wonderly wrothe ſwore wolde auenged theyr kynnes men deth came londe greate power robbed many place ſlewe dyde ye ſorowe myght whan vortiger wyſt made moche ſorowe ſore anoyed place alſo tydynges came hym aurilambros vter brother aſſembled grete hoſte came moche brytayne ſaye thys londe auenged vpon conſtance theyr brother deth soo one half brougho ſo moche ſorowe ne wyſt whether go ¶how engiſt xi thouſande mē came londe vortiger yaue place callde thongcaſtell ſoone ſorowe tydinges came vortyger grete nauy ſtraūgers arryued ye coūtree cent wyſt whēs ne wherfore come londe ¶the kynge ſent anone meſſager thyder ſome ſholde come ſpeke wyth hym wyte folke wert axed coūtree wolde ¶there two brethern mayſters prynces ſtronge company one called engiſt horne engiſt wente kynge tolde hym cauſe wherfore come londe ſayde syrewe ben countree called saxonne ye londe germayne wheryn y ſo moche ſorowe people ben ſoo many londe maye ſuſteynes mayſters prynces haue ye londe gouerne rule made come men wymmen boldeſt ben amonge theym fyghte beſte maye trauayll dyuerſe londes ſoo ſholde yeue horſe harnes armour thynge nedeth ſhall ſaye go countree mowelyue theyr cetrees dyde ¶and therfore ſyr kynge yf ye haue ought doo wyth company ben comen youre londe wyth good wylle wolde ſerue londe kepe helpe defende enmyes yf ye nede ¶whan vortyger herde theſe tydynges ſayde gladly wolde theym wyth holde vppon ſuche couenanuce yf myghte delyuer hys londe hys enmyes wolde yeue theym reſonable lōdes ſholde dwelle euer ¶engyſt thanked hym goodly thys maner cō pany xi thouſande ſholde dwelle wyth kynge vortiger moche dyde thrugh theyr boldeneſſe delyuered hys londe enmyes clene ¶tho prayed engyſt kynge ſo moche londe myghte make hym cyte hys meyne ¶the kynge anſwered doo wythoute coancell brytons ¶engiſt prayed hym eftſones moche plyce myghte compace thonge ſkyn̄e wherupon myghte make mancer hym dwelle kynge hym graunted freely ¶tho toke engiſt bulles ſkynne kytte ſma • e myghte oo thonge roūde ther compaced moche londe myght then̄e make vpon fayre caſtell ſo whan caſtell made lett calle thongcaſtell moche ye place marked thonge ¶of ronowen engiſtes douhter kynge voreiger ſpowſed beaute whan caſtell made full well arayed engiſt pryuely dyd ſende letter ī ye coūtree cam fro c ſhyppes fylled men ye ſtrong alſo well fyghtynge bataylles ye ſholde alſo brynge wyth ronowen hys doughter fayreſt creture man myghte ſee ¶and whan thoſe people come hadde ſente tooke caſtell wyth moche ioye hymſelf vpon daye went vnto kynge prayed hym worthely wolde come ſee hys newe maneer made place yt compaſſed wyth thonge ſkynne kynge anone graunted hym frely hym went thyder well apayed wyth caſtell wyth fayr werke togyder ete dranke wyth moche ioye whan nyght came kyng vortiger ſholde go hys chambre take hys nyghtes reſte ronowen yt engiſtes doughter came wyth cuppe golde honde kneled kynge ſayd hym waſſaylle kynge knewe meane ne ſhold anſwere vpon moche hymſelf ne none brytons coude noo englyſſhe ſpeſe ne vnderſtonde ſpake ſame langage brytons done yet neuertheles latiner tolde kynge full vnderſtandynge therof waſſayll ſholde drynke hayll fyrſte tyme waſſhayll drynkhall came vp londe frome ye tyme vnto thys tyme well vſed londe ¶the kynge vortiger ſawe fayrneſſe ronowen armes layde necke thryes ſwetely kyſſed anone ryght enamoured vpon yt deſyred haue wyf aſked engiſt fader engiſt graunted hym vpon couenaūt yt kyng ſholde yeue coūtree kent myghte dwelle hys people kynge hym graunted pryuely wyth good wylle anone ſpowſed ye damoyſell moche confuſyon hymſelfe therfore alle brytons became ſoo wrothe cauſe ſpowſed woman myſbyleue wherfore wente frome hym noo thynge hym tooke ne halpe hym thynge done ¶how vortimer vortigers ſone made kynge engiſt dryuen vortimer ſlayne engiſt wente kente ſeaſed ye londe honde hym men bycame lytyll whyle ſoo grete power ſo moche people hadde men wyſte lytell tyme whyche kyngꝭ men whyche engiſtes men wherfore brytons hadde hym dredde ſayd amōges theym yf ne toke counſeyll bytwene londe ſholde bytrayed thrugh engiſt people ¶vortiger kyng begoten fyrſt wyf thre ſones fyrſt called vortimer ſeconde catagien thyrde paſſent ¶the brytons euerychont one aſſent choſe vortimer theyr lod ſouerayne counſeyler euery batayll crowned hym made hym kynge wolde ſuffre vortiger lenger regne cauſe alyaunce betwixt engiſt hym ¶the brytons ordeyned grete hoſt dryue engiſt company londe yaue hym thre bataylles fyrſte kente lorde ſeconde tetforde thyrde ſhyre thys half colcheſtre batayll theym mette catagien horne engiſtes brother ſo eche thym ſlewe other· moche countree yeuen longe befor horne thrugh vortiger tho • e ſpowſed coſyn made fayr caſtell called horne caſtell owne name vortiger ſo anoyed brother dethe anone lete fell downe caſtell grounde ne lefte nyght ne daye tyll dryuen engiſt people londe then̄e ronowen doughter made ſorow ynogh quen • ely ſpake nexte kyng vortimer pryuyeſt hym ſo moche ſhe gaue hym gyftes enpoyſoned deyed london fourth yere hys regne lyeth ¶how brytons choſe tyme vortiger theyr kynge engiſt came londe fought togyders vortimers dethe brytons theyr comyn aſſēt eft ſones made vortiger theyr kynge vpon couenaunt ſholde neuer ſuffre engiſt ne none eft ſones come ī londe whā done ronowen quene pryuely ſente letter engiſt ſhe hadde en poyſoned vortimer vortiger lorde bare ayen ye crowne regned ſholde come ayen londe well arayed wyth moche people auenge hym vppon brytons wynne londe ayen ¶and whan engiſt herde theſe tydynges made grete ioy appareylled hym haſtely xv thouſande men yt deughty euery batayll came londe whan vortyger herde telle engyſt come ayen wyth grete power thys londe aſſembled hys brytons tho went ayenſt engyſt yeue hym batayll hys folke engiſt dradde hym ſore brytons dryuen hym diſcomfyted hym ſtrēgth wherfore engiſt prayed hym loue daye ſayd comen londe fyght haue hys lond ayen yf myght accorde brytons haue loue grace kynge vortiger thrugh counſeyll hys brytons graūted hym loue daye thus ordeyned thrugh brytons yt ſame daye ſholde holden faſt beſyde salyſbury vpon hylle engyſt ſholde come thyder four hordred kdnghtes without moo kyng many wyſeſt men hys londe· daye kynge came coūſeyll ordeyned engiſt warned hys knyghtes pryuely conmaunded euery one ſhold put longe knyf hys hoſe whan ſayde fayre ſyres y tyme ſpeke loue pea euery man anone ſhold drawe hys kynue ſlee bryton ſo ſlewe mlxi knyghtes wyth moche ſorowe many eſcaped kyng vortyger hymſelf tho taken ladde thongcaſtell put pryſon ſome engyſtes men wolde kynge brente alle quycke vortiger tho haue hys lyf graūted moche wolde yaue vp londe townes caſtelles cytees borughs engiſt folke brytons fledde thes waiys helde ſtyll engyſt wente thorugh londe ſeaſed londe wyth fraunchyles euery place lete caſt downe chyrches houſes relygyon waſted deſtroyed cryſtendome thrughout thys londe lete • aunge ye nam thys lond called brytayne noo man hys ſoo hardy tyme calle lōde brytayne calle engiſt londe ne departed londe hys men made vii kynges ſtrength londe brytons ſholde neuer come therem ¶the fyrſt kyngdome kent engiſt hymſelf regned lorde mayſter ouer al ye ¶the kyng southſex yt called chycheſtre ¶the thyrdet kyng weſtſex ¶the fourth eeſtſex fyfth eſtangill yt called northfolke southfolke merchemeryk y ſaye therldome nycholl ¶the ſixth leycheter ſhyre northampton ſhyre herforde huntyngdon ¶the ſeuenth hadde ox enforde gloucheſtre wyncheſtre wer wykeand derbyſhyre ¶how vortyger wente walys beganne caſtell yt wolde ſtande wyth morter tempred wyth blood engiſt departed lond thys maner bytwene hys men lyuerde vortyger pryſon ſuffred hym freely go whyther wolde toke waye wente walys brytons dwelled moche ye londe ſtronge wycked wynne engyſt • neuer came therene neuer knew londe ¶vortiger helde hym wyth hys bratons axed counſeyll hym beſt yaue hym counſeyll make ſtronge caſtell hym myghte hymſelf kepe defende yf nede • e ſons haſte tho fette began werke vpon ye hylle breigh certes thus befell werke maſons made daye downe felle nyght wyſte myght ther kynge ſore anoyed chaunce wyſte werfore lette ſende wyſeſt clerkes alſo lerned men thorugh walys myght foude ſholde tell wherfore ye foūdament ſo fayled vnder werke ſholde hym tell beſt doo whan theſe wyſe men longe tyme ſtudyed ſayde kynge ſholde doo ſeke chylde borne woman neuer man chylde ſholde ſlayne tempred blood morter werke ſoo ſholde werke euer endure withouten ende ¶how kynge lette ſeke merlyn thorugh walys ſpeke wyth hym kynge herde commaunded meſſagers anone go thrugh walys ſeke chylde yf myghte hym fynde ſholde hym brynge forthe vnto hym recorde wytneſſe thys kynge hadde take letter ne diſtroubled no▪ man ne lette tho meſſengers wente then ſpedde ſoo faſte came towne called carmardyne paſſed theyr waye founde two chyldern xxiiii· yere aege thydynge togyder haſty wordes one ſayde donebat ſayde ye wronge chyde ſtryue ye haue wytte ne reaſon haue certes merlyn ſayde wytte ne youre reſon make force men telle comynly ye haue thynge god myghty ſyth ye neuer fader euery man knoweth youre moder ¶the meſſengers kynge vortiger whan herde ſtryue betwixt two gromes axed ſtode beſyde whens that· marlyn borne alſo hym nouryſſhed folke tolde greate gentyll woman hym bare carmadyne called adhanr neuer myght noth man wyte fader ¶whan kynges meſſengers herde theſe tydynges wente anone hym wardeyne towne tolde hym kyngꝭ wyll ſhewed hym leter wherfore come thyder ¶merlyn moder fetched wardeyne towne commaunded ſholde go kynge ordeyned meſſagers merlyn moder wente then came vnto ye kynge receyued moche honour kynge axed lady yf ye chylde ſone whome hym gate lady anſwered full tenderly wepynge ſayde neuer hadde company worldly man ſyr ſayde ſhe yonge mayden faders chambre greate lygnage company oftentymes wente place ſolace belefte alone chambre wolde goo • orthe bernnynge ſonne • tyme came fayre bacheler entred chambre alone came wyſt neuer ne yet knowe doores faſt barred dyde game loue ne myght ne power hym defen often came vnto ye forſayd maner ſo begate childe neuer myght wyte ¶of anſwere merlyn wherfore kynge axed caſtel myght ſtonde begonne ne proue whan merlyn hadde herde moder hadde ſayd ſpake kynge maner ¶syre begoten axe ye falleth ne none wyte telle cauſe wherfore brought wherfore ye haue ſente ¶truely ſayd kyng wyſe couſeyllers haue done vnderſtode yt ye morter werke haue begonne behouety thempred blood foundament ſhall fayle euer ¶syr ſayd merlyn wyll ye ſlee blood tempre morter ye ſayd kyng elles caſtell ſhall neuer ſtande coūſeyllers vnderſtonde tho anſwerd merlyn kyng syr ſayd ſayd lete come thoſe wyſe coū ſeylles woll preu ſaye well ne truly whan ye wyſe men comen merlyn axed yf blod ye cauſe make werke ſtōde endure tho wyſe men abaſſhed coude anſwere merlyn tho ſayd kynge syr ſhall tell ye cauſe wherfore werke thus fayleth may • ſtande vnder moūtayne yt ye haue buylded youre toure grete ponde water ī ye botome ye ponde vnder ye water ben two dragon ye one whyte ye reede ye fyght togyd ayēſt werke ye myne depe eyll men come ye pond cauſe men take way ye water thenne ye ſhall ſee ye dragans haue tolde ye togyder fyght ayēſt werke cauſe wherfor foūdament fayleth kynge anone lete dygge vnder men came ponde lette doo waye water founde two dragon merlyn tolde egerly fought togyder whyte dragon egerly aſſayled reede lyadde hym ſo ſtrongely myght endure withdrewe hym reſted ſame caue whā whyle reſted hym wente aſſayled reede dragon angerly helde hym ſoo ſore yt myght ayenſte hym endure withdrewe hym reſted came ayen ye whyte dragon ſtrongly fought wyth reede dragon bote hym euyl ouercame fledde then nomore came agayne ¶of ſygnycacyon thoſe two dragon botome ponde fought togyder kynge vortyger hys men ſawe thys batayll grete meruayſle prayed merlyn tell myght betoken syr quod merlyn ſhall telle reede dragon betokeneth yourſelfe whyte betokeneth folke saxon fyrſte ye toke helde londe fyght ayenſt haue dryuen enchaced ¶but brytons ynure lygnage ouercame droue waye ſythen ye comynge ayen saxon recouered londe helde euer droue brytons dyde wyth londe wyll deſtroyed cryſtēdom thrugh thys londe ye fyrſte grete ioye wyth theyr comynge yt y torned grete damage ſorowe tho brethern conſtance kynge whiche ye lete ſlee ſhal come quīzeme paſſed grete power lytell brytayne ſhall auenge deth theyr brother ſhal brenne fyrſt wyth ſorowe ſhall ſlee grete parte saxon ſhall dryue remenaūt londe therfore abyde ye noo lenger make caſtell werke anone goo elles youre lyues alle ſaue god betake trouthe haue ſayde thynges ſhalle befalle ¶and vnderſtande ye welle aurilambros ſhalle kynge ſhalle enpoyſoned lytell tyme ſhall regne ¶of kynge aurilambros purſued vortiger engiſt deyed merlyn hys moder departed frome kynge torned agayne carmardyn ſoone tydynges came ye brytons aurilambros vter brother arryued totneſſe wyth greate hoſte anone brytons aſſembled thē wente receyue aurylambros vter wyth grete nobleſſe vnto london crowned aurylambros made hym kynge dyde vnto hym homage anone axed vortyger kynge myght founde wolde auenged brother dethe wolde warre vpon paynems tolde hym vortyger walys ſoo ladde hym thyther warde ¶vortiger wyſte welle tho brethern came hym conquere fledde then caſtell called gerneth ſtode vppon hyght mountayne hym helde aurilambros vter hys brother theyr folke beſyeged caſtell full long tyme cagell ſtronge well arrayed ¶so laſte caſted wylde fyre brente howſes men theyr araye moche wythin caſtell soo vortiger brente amonge ſoo deyde wyth moche ſorowe ¶tho engiſt kente regned ane herde thys tydynges anone fledde wolde haue gone scotlonde haue ſocoure aurilambros men mette hym north coū tre yane hym batayl engiſt men defended whyles myghte folke diſcomfyted ſlayne octa ſone fledde vnto yorke aurilambros hym folowed egerly octa lytell whyle withſtode hym warde put hym mercy aurilambros receyued hym hym hys men gaafthe countree galewaye scotlonde dwelled ¶the kyng aurilambros wente thorugh londe put awaye name englonde engiſt hys name called befoere tho lete calle agayne grete brytayne lete make ayen cherches houſes religyon caſtelles cytees broughs towones saxon hadde deſtroyed came london lete make walles cyte whyche engiſt folke hadde caſtedowne ¶the brytons ladde hym vnto mount ambrian ſomtyme hous relygyon tho deſtroyed thrughe paynems ¶wherof knyght called ambri ſometyme founder houſe therfore ſame hylle called mount ambrian called ambreſbury ſhall ſo euermore • ¶how aurilambros dyde redreſſe londe greate brytayne whyche deſtroyed thorugh saxon ſayde kynge aurilambros lete amende redreſſe houſe ambreſbury put monkes ben nonnes lytell fro place called salyſbury saxon ſlewe brytons engiſt ſhold haue made laue daye whyche tyme ſlayne thouſande knyghtes lxi thrugh treaſon engiſt· kynge therof grete pyte thoughte make mynde monument ſtone myght endure worldes ende thys thynge tooke ther counſeyll therof beſt ¶tho ſpake kynge byſſhop london called ternekyn ſholde requyre merlyn coude beſt telle thyng myght beſt made merlyn ſought founde came kyng kynge tolde hym hys wyll monumente wolde haue made merlyn anſwered kynge ſayd ben grete ſtones irlonde longe vpon hylle kyan men called gyauntes karoll yf place ben wolde endure eurer remembraunce thoſe knyghtes entyred ¶per may foy ſayd kynge harde ſtone ben londe irlonde ¶soth ſayde merlyn londe ben none ſuche gaūtes ſette grete good themſelf atte euery tyme woūde ony maner hurte wyſſhe ſtones hote water thenne wyſſhe ther anone hoole ¶how brytons wente ſeke grete ſtones irlonde ſoone brytons herde thynge yede ſwore amō ge wolde go ſeke thoſe ſtones toke vter kynges broder thyef capytayne v thouſande men merlyn counſelled go vnto irlonde ſoo thye dyde whan kynge irlonde culled guillomer herde tell ſtraungers arryued londe aſſē bled grete power fought ayenſt folke dyſcomfyted ¶the brytons went tyll came mount kyan clymmed vp vnto mounte whan ſawe ſtones maner ſtode grete meruaylle ſayde bytwene themſelf noo man ſholde remeue noo ſtrengthe ne engyne ſoo grete ſoo longe merlyn thrugh crafte remeued broughte theyr ſhyppes came ayen thys londe merlyn ſette ſtones kyng wolde haue ſette ſame manner ſtode irlonde whan ye kynge ſawe made thanked merlyn rychely hym rewarded owne wyll place lete calle stonhenge euer ¶how paſſent vortigers ſone kynge guillomer came thys londe traytour called cappa enpoyſoned ye kynge aurilambros men ſhall vnderſtonde paſſent vortigers ſone lyued ye ſame tyme came thys londe wyth grete power arryued north coūtre wolde auēged faders deth vortiger ſtrongely truſted vpon company brought wyth hym londe germayne conquered north countree vnto yorke ¶and whan kynge aurilambros herde aſſemled grete power brytons went fyght paſſēt dyſcomfyted paſſent peple paſſent eſcaped then ſome men fledde then irlonde come kynge guillomer prayed hym helpe ſocour kynge graūted hym good wyll ſayde wolde helpe hym vppon couenaunt ſelfe muſte go power brytayne wolde aduenge vpon broytons rather came londe toke ſtones ſtrength called gyauntes karoll ¶the kyng guillomer lete ordeyne ſhippes went ſee xv thouſāde men arryued walys began robbe moche ſorowe dyde ¶it befell ſo kynge aurilambros laye ſyke wyncheſtre myghte helpe hym ſelf ſente name vter brother power helpe walys thyther warde went moche myght ¶the kynge irlonde paſſente herde telle aurilambros ſyke hym came sarraſyn called cappa ſayde syre dwelle ye pea hoſt behyght thorugh quaynteſye ye ſhall ſlee kynge aurilambros ſyke thenne ſayd paſſent yf ye doo ſo ſhall rychely auaunce traytour cappa put vpon hym habyte relygyon lete ſhaue hym brode crowne came vnto kynges courte ſayde wolde help • kynge malady tho ſayd traytour cappa vnto kyng syr good comforte ſhall yeue ſuche medicyne ye ſhalle ſwete anōe ryght lyſte ſlepe haue good reſte traytour yaaf hym ſuche poyſon ſlepe anone ryghte deyed hys ſlepynge ye traytour ſayd yt wolde go felde tyll awaked ſo eſcaped awaye man hym ſuſpeccyon cauſe habyte clothed ī alſo hys brode ſhauen crowne whan kynges men wyſte deed became wonder ſory faſte ſoughte traytoure myghte fynde hym· ye cappa torned ayen vnto hoſte frem whes yt came ¶whan aurilambbros deyed ſterre morne ſeen wyth clere lyght bought beeme ſene heed horryble dragō whan kyng aurilambros deed enpoyſoned wincheſtre morne dede aboute tyme pryme ſene ſterre grete clere beeme ſterre brygheter thā ye ſonne bought ye beeme apperyd dragon heed hys mouth came two huge lyghtes bryght ony fyre brennynge one beeme warde fraunce ſtreyght ouer ſee thyther warde beeme came vii beemes full clere longe lyghte fyre ¶this •• erre ſeen many man none wyſte tokened ¶vter kynges brother walys wyth hys hoſte brytons ſawe ſterre grete lyght yaue wondred ther gretly myghte betoken lete calle merlyn prayed hym telle yt myhght betoken ¶of betokenynge ſterre merlyn ſawe ye ſterre behelde yt longe tyme ſythen quoke wepte tenderly ſayde· ala ala ſoo noble kyng worthy y deed iou vnderſtānde aurilambros brotherds poyſoned ſee well thys ſterre yourſelfe y betokened heed dragon ſeen bought beeme y ſelf ſhall kynge regne beeme ſtondeth warde eeſt y vnderſtonde ye ſhall gete ſone ſhall conquere fraunce londes belongeth crowne fraunce ſhalle wrothyer kynge honoure euer ony auncetours ¶and beeme ſtretched towarde irlonde betokened ye ſhalle gete doughter ſhalle quene irlonde ¶and ſeuen beemes betoken ye ſhall haue vii ſones euery one ſhall kyng regne wyth moche honoure abyde ye lenger goo yeue batayll enmyes fyghte wyth booldely ye ſhalle ouercome haue victory ¶vter thanked hertely merlyn toke men wente warde hys enmyes fought togyder mortally ſoo dyſcomfyted enmyes deſtroyed hym ſelf ſlewe paſſēt vortigers ſone brytons ſlewe guillomer kyng irlonde men ¶and vter anone batayll toke hys waye warde wyncheſtre doo entyere aurilambros kynge brother tho body borne vnto stonhenge moche honour done make remembraū ce brytons ſlayne thrugh treaſon engiſt ſame day ſholde haue ben accorded ſame place entyered aurelambros ſeconde yere hys regne wyth ye worſhyp ye myght belonge ſuche kynge whoos ſoule god haue mercy amen ¶of vter pendragon therfore called ſo ye ſhall ouertake loue igreyne erle cornewaylles wyf dethe aurilambros vter brother crowned regned well worthely remembraunce dragon lykened lete make two dragon thrugh coūſeyll brytons made one borne hym whā wēte batayll ye abyde att wyncheſtre byſſhop chyrche cauſe called euer vter pendragon ¶and octa engiſtes ſone cōmended vter lytell yt made newe kynge ayenſte hym began meue warre ordeyned grete power frē de hys kynne oſſa hys brother taken londe humbre vnto yorke thoſe yorke helde ſtrongely agaynſt wolde ſuffre come cytee neyther yelde cytee beſyeged towne anone ryght yaue therto ſtronge aſſawte cyte kept well ſtrongely ¶and whan vter herd therof came thyther wyth grete ſtronge power helpe reſcowe ye towne put way ſyege yaue ſtronge batayll octa company defended well myght ye laſte dyſcōfyted moſt partye thē ſlayne octa oſſa taken put pryſon london ¶and vter hymfelf dwelled whyle atte yorke wente london eeſter wold vere crowne holde ſolempne feeſt lette ſomone erle baron ſholde come feeſt thoſe hadde wyues ſholde brynge alſo feeſt ſeygnoury came kynges cō maundemente commaunded ¶the feeſt rychely men ſlewe ſo many saxon hat neuer ſeen ſuche ſlaughter cheldrik hys men left alyue fledde waye kynge arthur purſewed droue wood tha myghte ferder paſſe ¶cheldrik hys mē ſawe well brought moche knyghtes whan hadde nede ¶how arthur enchanced mordred traytour ſlayne alſo kynge arthur wounded deth thys tydynges came kynge arthur bourgoyne full ſore anoyed toke fraunce howell kepe half deale men prayed hym wold kepe tyll came ayen hymſelfe wolde paſſe brytayne auenge hym vpon mordred traytour forth arthur wente waye came wytſande made men go ſhyppe wolde haue arryued sandwyche brought hym grace hoſt frēſhemen alſo owne londe men myght come londe wyth people come hys ſhyppes mordred come wyth power yaue ſtronge batayll ſoo kynge arthur loſt many man myght come londe gawayne hys neuewe ſlayne anguyſſhell helde scotlonde many wherof kynge arthur ful ſory come londe mordred myghte ayenſt endure anone dyſcomfyted flydde then ſame nyght men vpon morne came to· london tho cyte wolde ſuffre hym come then fledde wyncheſtre hym helde people yt came ¶kynge arthur lete take body gawyne cofyn body anguyſſhell lete ye one borne scotlonde douer buryed anone kynge arthur toke waye deſtroye mordred fledde then cornewayle ¶and ye quen gun • yt kyng arthur wyf yt thoſoiourned 〈◊〉 yorke herde ye mordred fledde then might endure ayenſt kyng arthur ſhe fore aferde grete doubte wyſt beſte done ſhe vnderſtode well lorde kynge arthur wolde neuer haue marcy ye grete ſhame ſhe done vnto hym toke waye pryuely four men without moo came karlyon ſhe dwelled lyue neuer ſeen amonges folke lyf duryng ¶kynge arthur wyſt mordred fledde cornewayle lete ſende men scotlonde northomberlonde vnto humbre lete aſſemble folke without nombre came fro then cornewayle ſeke purſewe mordred ¶and mordred aſſembled hym folke cornewayle people without nombre 〈◊〉 wyſt arthur comynge leuer deye take chaūce longer flee abode yaue harde batayll kynge arthur people ſo moche people ſlayne one ſyde noman wyſt better party ſo befell laſt mordred ſlayne al folke good chyualry kynge arthur gadred nouryſſhed dyuer londes alſo noble knyghtes rounde table ſo moche prayſed thorugh oute worlde ſlayne kynge arthur hymſelf wounded vnto dethe lete hym borne auioun heeled woundes yet brytons ſuppoſed lyued lond ſhall come yet conquere alle brytayne ¶but certes ye prophecye merlyn ſayde deth ſhall doubtous ſayde ſothe therof yet men haue doubte ſhall haue euer men ſaye mē wote wyther lyue deed ¶arthur borne auioun xxii yere regne incarnacyon lorde iheſu cryſte vcxlvi yere kynge arthur delyuered reame vnto conſtantyne ſone cador neuewe kynge arthur wyſte myght noo lenger regne lette come hym conſtantyne yt cadors ſone erle cornewayle coſyn hym betoke reame toke ſayd bad hym therof kynge tyll came ayen moche none heeyre hys body begoten grete damage ſoo noble kynge ſoo doughty hadde noo chylde body begoten thynge god woll haue done muſt done whoſe name bleſſyd wythout ende ¶how kynge conſtantyne vexed mordred two ſones conſtantyne noble knyght worthy body tho two ſones mordred begoten grete enuy conſtātyne tho crowned kynge ſo befell yt meued warre ayenſt hym aſſembled grete hoſt mordred ben dryuen waye dyd moche ſarowe anguyſſhe thrughout londe one brother ordeyned purpoſed hym towarde auncyent cyte london take ye cyte went wyncheſtre conſtantyne came lōdon ſlewe ben borne oo body ¶the kynge edell ſuſter called orewenne gaf thrught grete freodſhyp kyng adelbryght wyf begate vpon doughter called argentyll thyrde yere came vpon hym ſtrange ſykeneſſe nedes muſt nouryſſhe hys chambre whan ſhe aege ſhe ſholde maryed ſtrongeſt worthyeſt man myghte fynde thenne ſholde yelde vp londe ayen ¶edell graunted othe confermed hys prayer ¶and whan adelbryght deed enteryd edell tooke damoyſell argentyll nourrſſhed hys chambre ſhe became fayre ony myghte ¶how kynge edell maryed damoyſell knaue kechyne kyng edell vncle argentyll thought myght falſely haue londe fro nyce euer falſely aynſt hys othe thought dyſceyue ye damoyſell marye knaue kechyne called curan became ye worthyeſt ſtrongeſt man body ony man wyſt ony londe tho lyued hym thought ſhamfully haue maryed haue londe afterwarde clene dyſceyued thys curan hauelockis ſone kynge kyrkelane denmarke curan conquered hys wyues londe warde ſlewe kyng edel h • wyues vncle al londe place telleth openly regned iii yere saxon dane hī ſlewe grete harme brytayn srytons bare hym sto • henge entyred hym honourably ¶of kyng conan curans coſyn curan regned coſyn conan wonder proude knyghte regned coude haue noo maner loue euer medlynge wyth hys people tooke vncle warre ſlewe two chyldern ¶the saxon warred ayenſt hym oftentymes ouer came ſoo pea lyf tyme· regned xiiii yere deyed lyeth london ¶of kynge cortyf gurmonde came thorugh paynems brytayne conan regned coſyn cortyf behated peple thynge beloued cortyf loſt brytayne thrugh warre ī tyme fell ye grete myſcheyf brytayn ye cryſtendom deſtroyed ye brytons dryuē londe londe loſt ony recouer warde left londe saxon ye afterwarde ſhall tyme paynem called gormō de kynges ſone daufrices panems folke hadde reame hys fader kynge ſauf bequaue yaue broder ſayd wolde neuer kynge yf myght gete conquere reame ſtraunge countree bolde ſtronge body hym prophecyed merlyn ſayde heſholde wulf ſee lette aſſemble paynems wythout nombre lete appareylle brytons ſo ſent gurmonde irlonde ſhold come brytayne helpe ayenſt ye brytons helpe delyuer londe wolde hym holde gladly theyr lord paynem paynems brytons cryſtened well ought helpe ſo one lawe whā gurmonde herde prayer haſted moche myght arryued scotlonde came northomberlonde saxon dwellynge confermed couenaūtes bytwene made othes hoſtages bere hym true fay holde hym lorde paye hym truage yere ¶tho began saxon ye affricans deſtroye robbe brenne townes deſtroye theng • aſmoche myght ſpared neyther man woman ne chylde lerned ne lewde ſlewe caſte downe townes caſtels chirches ſo put londe grete deſtruccyon ſoone myghte flee fledde then well poore ryche byſſhops abbottes chanons grete ſmal ſome lytell brytayne ſome cornewayle tho ye ſhyppes myghht haue ¶how kynge gurmonde droue kyng cortyf checheſtre ſlewe brytons thrugh crafte engyne gate ſame towne cortyf kyng fledde then checheſtre tho ſtronge helde hym xx dayes gurmonde came beſyeged cytee ſo ſtronge myght gete maner wyſe engyne myght doo tho bethought vpon ſubtylte brenne towne made engynes wyth glewe nettes toke pecys thunder fyre bonde ſparowes foot lete flee anōe flewe lodged thē ye towne ther yt theyr neſtis ſtackes eueſynges houſes ye fyre began kyndle brente ye towne whan brytons ſawe euery ſyde hyed fought anone ſlayne dyſcomfyted whyle batayll dured kynge pryuely hydde hym ſtale awaye walys men wyſt neuer became ſoo towne checheſtre taken deſtroyed gurmonde wente deſtroyed townes cytees neuer made ayen ſeen yet many place thys londe ¶how thys londe called englonde name engyſt many kynges made thys londe whan gurmonde deſtroyed al londe thrugh yaue londe saxon anone toke good wyll saxon longe tyme deſyred aſmoche wereof engiſtꝭ kynred fyrſt londe brytayne lete called englyſſmen cauſe engiſtes name lond lete call englonde theyr langage folke ben called englyſhmen aſmoche thys tyme called engiſtꝭ londe whan cōquered vortiger ſpouſed hys doughter fro tyme yt brute came fyrſt englonde thys londe called brytane folke brytons ſyth tyme yt thys gurmonde conquered eftſones yaue vnto saxon anone ryght chaūged name ſayde whan thys done gurmonde paſſed ouer fraū ce conquered many londes deſtroyed criſten peple came saxon dwelled londe began faſt enhabyte ther owne wyll wolde haue made newe kyngis lordes myght neuer aſſent haue oo kynge attendaunt therfore made many kynges forth came vnto caunterbury ſoyourned kynge adelbryght kent lygnage engiſt goodly receyued ſaynt auſtyn hys felowes wyth moche honour foūde neded ouer yaue theym fayre place called abbay shynt auſtyn hym ſcorned caſte vpon hym reygh taylles ſo mantell hanged full theſe reygh tayles dyſpyte caſte vpon hym guttes reyghes fyſſhe wherfore good man saynt auſtyn ſore anoyed greued prayed god tho departed londe amonge tooke homagꝭ feautees folke countree wente warde walys thot walys herd telle theſ comfyture breic • leycetre wonder adrad tho two kyngeꝭ tooke thoſe amonge good men hooly hemytes monkes preeſtes people grete plentye wente bare foote wulwarde ta haue mercy thes two kynges tho kynges ſo ſterne ſo wyked yt wold neuer ſpeke thē ſlewe euerychone ala ſorowe ne ſpared noomore wulfe ſlayne elfryde flede northumberlonde owne lō de· ¶and people leycetre ſhyre made ſtrenght cadewan yt brycinals ſone kynge leceytre afterregned nobly grete honour ¶how cade wan kynge leycetre elfryde toke homage feautes folke countree aſſembled grete hoſte ſayde wolde goo northumberlonde deſtroy kynge elfryde ſle hym yf myght whan come thether frendes wente ſo bytwene accorde manere elfryde ſholde father dethe fader hadde holde lyf tyme ¶and cadewā another ſone called cadwalyn helde faders londe helde whyle alyue theſe loued bretheren ye loue laſted betwyxt two yere began debat betwyxt throughe ſynple enuyous coſyn cadwalins called bryens ſo yt aſſembled grete hoſte bothe partyes laſte fell ye cadwalin dyſcūforted edwen hym purſued droue hym fro place place ſo laſt fledde irelonde yt helde londes edwyns yefte ¶how kynge oſwallde ſlayne thoughe kynge cadwalin peanda howe oſwy ſaynte oſwaldes broder regned hym ſlewe peanda edwyn ſlayne offris ſone vndertoke warre ayenſte cadwalin came ſo yt offris deyed durynge ye warre ye dethe offris tho regned gentyl cryſten man moche loued god almyghty yt londe northumbrelonde herytage yt called oſwalde kynge londe moche frende edwyn helde oſwalde tyl takē ſlayne cadwalin toruned home ayen ¶whan oſwalde herde theſe tydynges cadwalin tourned home ayen wolde lē ger flee abode peanda yaue hym batayll peanda dyſcomfort • e fledde came batayll oſwalde ſlayne heed ſmyten entered abbay berdenay whiche place god hadde wrought hym many fayre myracle bothe elles ¶and anone oſwy brother ſeaſed londe honde oſwaldis folke northumberlonde loued wonderly well helde hym theyr lorde men kynne worthy ynough wolde haue departed londe warred togyed well aſmoche ſtronge ynoughe came peanda prayed hym helpe ſocour behyght hym ye lōde largely vpō couenāt wold gouerne helpe counſeyl ¶peanda herde theyr prayer ſo ſpake cadwalyn ſholde ordayne grete hoſt faſte ordeyned hym northumberlonde teyght oſwy oſwy meke man moche loued pea charyte god peanda truſted tomoche vpon pryde vpon hoſte gyder ſmote egerly peanda anone dyſcomforted ſlayne incarnacyon oure lorde iheſu cryſte vclv yere oſwy regned xxviii yere kynge called oſwyne peandaes coſyn warred vpon hym togyder fought oſwy hadde victory oſwyne oſwyn dyſcomforted ſlalyne lyeth tynnemouth ¶how kynge cadwaldre cadwalins ſone regned fader laſte kynge brytons deth cadwelin regned hys ſone cudwaldre well nobly moder ye ſyſter peanda whan regned xii yere felle grete ſykeneſſe thenne greate dyſcorde bytwene lordes londe euery warred vpon yet tyme fell ſo grete derth ſcarſyte corn viteylles londe man myghte go iii iiii dayes fro towne towne yt ſholde fynde bye golde ne ſyluer brede wyne ne none vitayle wich man myght lyue onely people lyued rotis herbes lyuynge none ſo moche faylled aboute fyſſhes wylde beſtes thynge ſoo yet myſauenture felle ſoo greate mortalyte peſtelens amonge people corrupcyon ayre ye lyuynge people ſuffyſed burye deed bodyes deyed ſoo ſodenly bothe grete ſmalle lorde ſeruaunt etynge goynge ſpekynge fell downe deyed ſo neuer herde ſodeyne deth amonge people wente burye deed body ſame deed body buryed ſoo myght flee fledde forſoke theyr londes houhes welle grete hungre derth ſcarſyte corne vitayll grete mortalyte peſtylence londe wente londes ſaue theyr lyues lefte londe deſerte waſt ſo yt noman trauayle tylthe londe londe barayne corne fruytes defawte tyllyers myſauenture dured xi yere noman myght ere ne ſowe ¶how cadwaldre wente londe lytell brytayne cadwaldre ſawe grete hungre mortalyte peſtylence londe poore faylynge cornes ād vytaylles folke peryſſhed ſawe alſo mooſte partye londe waſted voyde people apparelled hym folke lefte alyue paſſede ouer lytell brytayne lytell nauy vnto kynge alayne moche loued coſyn fader hadde moche loued tyme ſayled ſee made moche lamentacyon ſo dyde alle tho hym ſayde dediſti no domine tanquan • oues eſcarū et gentibus diſperſiſti no thenne began cadwaldre complayne hym folke pyteouſly ſayd· ala ſayd v wretch caytyues ſorowe grete ſynnys whiche wolde amende v whyle ſpace repentaunce comen vpon v throughe ſauenture whiche chaced v oure reame propre ſoyle whiche ſomtyme romayns becottes saxon neyther danys myght exyle v ¶but auaylleth v tyme oft tymes haue goten many londes ſyth y wyll god abyde dwelle owne londe god iuge yat thynges knoweth ben done made ſeeth wolde ceſſe oure ſynnes enmyes myghte v ne lygnage exyle fro reame wolde amende v oure folyes ſee propre defautes therfore hath ſhewed v wrathe woll chaſtyſe v myſdedes syche doth v batayll ſtrength enmyes grace companyes wretcchedly leue reame propre londe ¶torne ayen ne ye romany torne agayne ye scottes torne agayne ye saxxons torne agayne ye fraū ſoys ſeweth brytayne deſerte whiche power myght neuer make deſerte ne yet oure power hathe put v exyle onely power kynge allmyghty haue often offended folyes whiche wolde leue vntyll chaſtyced v dyuyne power ¶amonge worldes lamentacyon kynge cadwhldre made folke arryued ī lytell brytayne came kynge alayne ſayd ¶and kynge receyued hym grete ioye made hym ſeruede wonder nobly abode longe tyme ¶the engleſſhe people left lyue eſcaped grete hungre mortalyte lyued beſt wyſe myght moche people ſprange came ¶and ſente saxonye borne ther frendes men wyemen chyldren reſtore cytees people townes voyde people laboure traueyll tylthe erthe ¶whan saxon herde theſe tydynges came ye londe wonder thyeke grete companyes herborowed therſelfe countree aboute wolde founde man lete ne withſtonde ſo waxed multeplyed gretely vſed maners cuſtomes countree wherof come vſed alſo lawes langages ſpeche theyr owne londe came fro alſo chaunged name cytyes twones caſtelles brought yaue name called nowe ben called helde counrees baronage lordeſhyps manere brytons tyme compaſſed amonge grete companyes came frome germayne londe came noble quene called se • burga men wymmen without nombre· arrayed coū tree northumberlonde tooke londe frome ilbion vnto cornewaylle folke none myght thē lette alle deſolace voyde people fewe poore brytons lefte mountayns woddes vntyll tyme ¶and fro tyme forthe loſte brytons reame theyr dayes englyſſhe people begane regne departed lōde bytwene made many kynges aboute dyuerſe partyes londe ben dyuyded fyrſt weſteſexe ſecond • merchenriche thyrde eſtangle fourthe kente fyfth southſex thoſe regned londe ye cadwaldre paſſed londe dwelled lytell bryten kynge alayne coſyn true frende whan longe dwellede knowynge mortalyte peſtelence ouerpaſſed londe replenyſſhed ayen wyth people thought torne ayen londe prayed kynge alayne coſyn ſocour helpe yt myghte reſtored ayen owoe propre reame fyrſte dygnyte kynge aleyne graunted hym aſkynge ¶thenne dyde appareylle hym take wayt vyage londe prayed god allmyghty deuoutly wolde make hym demonſtracyon yf prayer londe hyme pleſaunt none ayenſte wyll god allmyghty wolde thynge ¶whā thus deuoutly made prayer avoys fro heuen hym ſayd hadde hym leue ye iurney waye englonde ſholde goo pope rome wyll almyghty god yt brytons ſholde regne brytane ne neuer recouered vnto tyme prophecye marlyn ſayd fu • fylled ſholde neuer vnto ye tyme come relyques body ſhall broughte fro rome tranſlated brytayne whan ralykes ſayntes haue ben hedde ye perſecucyon paynem folke ſhall founde openly ſhewed thenn ſhalle recouer theyr londe agayne whyche haue ſoo longe tyme loſte throughe theyr deſertes ¶whane cadwaldre hadde herde anſwere maruayled gretely tolde kynge aleyne ¶thene kynge aleyne dyde ſende clergye londe made brynge ſtoryes prophecyes merlyn sybyll ſayd theyr prophcyes whan knewe prophycye feſtom prophecyed egle prophecyes accorded dyuyne aunſwere caddewalldre herde counſelled hym ryght faythfully deſyred hym leue people nauy ſubmytte hym dyſpocyſyon god aungell cōmaū ded hym ¶thenye cadwaldre called • ſone ymori coſyn ſyſters ſone ſayd taketh ſayde folke nauy redy paſſe walys ye lordees brytons dyſhonoure come interrupcyon paynem folke defaute lordes ¶and thene hymſelfe lefte reame brytayne folke euer tooke waye vnto pope rome sergius whyche worſhypede hym moche ſo confeſſed toke penaunce hys ſynnes longe dwelled ne deyed xii kalendis maye • yere grace vclxxii ¶how kynge offa ſouerayne aboue kynges englonde euery kynge warred vpon befell ſo kynges tyme yu londe weſtſex marchenryche eſtangle kente southſex coſtes eche warred vpon moſte myght toke londe hym mooſte febleſt ¶but kynge amonge called offa ſaynte oſwaldes brother offa conquered kynges ye londe regned aboue ¶and ſ •• gret yt warre euery bytwene grekes mā myght wyte lond wente abbottos pryours men relygyon wrote yt lyues dedes kynges longe euery theym regned coūtre manere euery kynge deyed byſſhops alſo therof made grete bokys lete calle cronycles good kyng alured booke warde lette brynge vnto wyncheſtre lete faſte tacked pylar men ſholde remeue ne bere then ſo euery man ſholde ſee therupon loke therin ben lyues kynges euer englonde ¶how kynge northumberlonde oſbryght forlaye wyf buerne bocarde thrugh ſtrength buerne conquered kyng power ſtrength thus befell ye ſame tyme kyng northumberlond • e called oſbryght ſoyourned atte yorke ¶and kynge wente hym vppon daye wood hym dyſporte came ayen wente pryuely good mannes houſe called buerne good man place gone tyme ſee ¶for oftentymes wonte ſpye theues robber oftentymes wonte come londe robbe brenne ſlee lady buernes wyfe wonder fayre woman ¶and kynge came vnto whan herhuſbode abſente ſhe truſted none harme vnto kynge welcomed hym moche honour worthely hym ſerued thynge ¶whan kynge hadde eten tooke lady honde • adde chambre ſayde wolde ſpeke counſeyll folke made voyde fro chambre ſaue lady lady wyſt wherfore dyde tyll done alle hys wyll whan hadde done dede torned agayne yorke lady lefte ſore wepynge dede kynge done ¶and whan • lorde came home ſawe wepe ſuche ſorowe mornynge make axed ſhe hadde done ſhe made ſuche ſorowe ¶syre ſhe ſayde ſubtylly falſely kynge oſbryght • hathe doo ſhame vylanye ayeaſt wyll tolde hym truthe kynge • orlayne ſtrengthe wherfore ſhe ſayde ſhe hadde leuer deed tolyue ¶fayre loue ſtylle ſayde ayenſt ſtrengthe febleneſſe yltell worthe therfore ſhalte thou neuertheleſſe beloued namely thou haſt tolde treuthe yf almyghty god graūt lyf ſhall aueng ¶this buerne grete man myghty lorde well beloued grete frendes hadde lete ſende gretteſt lordes londe made he complaynte deſpyte kynge hym hadde done ſayde wolde auenged euer yt hys frendes counſeylled hym ſholde goo vnto yorke kynge hym defye buerne toke mayne came kynge whan kynge hym ſawe called hym curtouſly buerne name buerne hym anſwerred hym ſayde syre defye yelde vp feautes homage londes moche haue holden fro tyme warde wyll neuer nothynge holde ſoo departed fro kynge without ſpeche ony abydynge tooke leue frendes went denmarke playned kynge godern tolde hym deſpyte kynge oſbryght hym hadde donne wyfe prayed hym ſocour helpe hym auenge ¶whan kynge godern denmarke danys hadde herde complaynt thys buerne prayer badde ryght wonder glasde theyr hertes moche myght fynde cauſe goo englonde warree vpon engleſſhe men aenge buerne deſpyte kyng oſbryght hadde done vnto hys wyf moche buerne ſybbe v • kynge denmarke anone lette ordeyne greate hoſte men lete ordeyne theym ſhyppes moche theym nede haue vyage whan hoſt redy kyng made two brethern chyef capytayns noble knyghtes body alſo bolde one called hunga hubba ¶how danys tooke yorke ſlewe kynge oſbrygt ſoone ſlewe kynge eelle sall redy yt two brethern toke leue ofthe kynge godren wente towarde ſee paſſe • ouer inglonde faſt myght ſpede buerne ſo welle comforted faſte hyed hym wyth danys ben arryued north coūtre comen thrugh holdernes deſtroyed countree brenned townes robbed folke ſlewe myght take tyll came vnto yorke whan kyng oſbryght ſawe come tooke alle hys people hym came cytee faught noo foyſon ne hadde ayenſt moche people ſlayne bothe partyas kynge oſbryght hym ſelf ſlayne cyte anene take danys wente ¶and alſo kynge northumberlonde buernes frendes hadde thoſe helde hym kynge man called elle moche wolde kynge oſbryght attendan̄t deſpyte done vnto buerne theyr coſyn ¶it befell thus kyng elle gone wood hym dyoſporte venyſon ſome taken ſate wood meete knyght ſayde ha • wel ſpedde moche venyſon taken ¶and worde came man hym ſayd yf yeſo moche venyſon haue wonne hodred tymes ſo moche ther ayenſt haue ye loſte thys coūtree danys haue goten taken cytee yorke ayenſt ſhall holde neuer ye ſhalcome therin ſoo moche haue ſlayne kynge oſbryght whan kynge elle herde theſe wordes lete aſſemble folke coūtree ordeyned power myght haue wolde haue goten towne yorke ſtrength danys came anone yaue hym ſtrōge batayll ſelwe kyng elle mooſt parte ye peple yt brought hym ¶and ſame place ſlayne ſhalle euer called elle crofte place lytell yorke ¶and reſted danys neuer tyl hadde conquered northumberlonde countree made wardeynes wente londe tooke notyngham abode ye wynter dyed ſorowe myght ¶and whan somer tyme came remeued frome notyngham came nicholl lyndeſey holonde noo man myght wythſtande ſoo moche power ſtrengthe ſaynt edmōde kynge martyred ſoo ferre hadde danys paſſed frome countree edmonde kynge ordeyned moche folke myghte foughte wyth danys folke dyſcomfyted kynge hymſelfe dryuen vnto caſtell f • amelynham danys hym purſhewed came vnto ye ſame caſtell ¶and whan kynge edmonde came redynge toke towne helde tyll kynge edelf weſtſex came thyther power take townes tho came danys yeue batayll edelf batayll ſlayne erle danys called sidrak vpon morowe came kynge eldred hys ¶the lady welcome • kynge ſwetely hym kyſſed toke ye honde nexte hym ſa • te ſo ſouped togyder ¶and cuſtome vſage londe tyme ſo whan drake drynker ſholde ſaye waſſayll ſholde anſwere ſaye drynke hayll
