¶lothariꝰ regned hym two yere deceſſed whan otto regned almayne hadde wyf hyght dalnyham whiche wedded otto ¶beringarius fourth hym man grete tyrannye ſubduedytaly wherfore pope romayns called otto myghte delyuer whiche dyde toke beryngaryus ſtrength twyes outlawed hym toke lotharius wyfe whiche tyraūt pryſoned ¶leo viii pope benedictus one yere foure monethes man choſen comyn voys iohannes depoſyd leo ordeyned pope ſholde made without conſente ye emperour malyce ye romayns whiche oppreſſyd thys man graunted yeftes otto hys ſucceſſours whyche yeuen iuſtinianus karolus ye chyrche myghte defende ytaly frome reberlyons ¶iohanes xii pope hym almooſt viii yere thys iohēs ſuffred grete wronge ye romayns take exyled otto bare heuyly ſlewe noble men rome certayne exyled euer benedyctus vi pope hym vi· yere thys man take caſtell aungell ſtrangled ¶nota ¶the empyre thys tyme tranſlated almayns ſame cauſe • ycyous lyuynge ne theſe vnhappy men cowde informed ſhold eſchewe • woyce thrugh whiche ſa • e ſoo many noble men peryſſhe ¶otto emperour beryngarius xii yere otto fyrſt emperoure almayne vertuous kynge karolus defender chyrche god ſyngular promoter whyche worthy emperoure many men fals byleue conuerted helde hym pope benedictus vſurper popeherd soxony deceſſyd exyle emperoure deceſſyd ryche man vertue goodnes ¶otto ſeconde emperour fader noble man chyrche fader many batayll ayenſt fals men byleue laſte almooſt loſte hoſte kalabur yet ſothe mynde beſought ſaynt peter helpe meruellouſly ſaynte peter delyuered hym wyf doughter ye emperour conſtantynopolytan roman bloode man crowned benedictus pope ¶of ſaynte edwarde martyr eſcrylde hys ſtepmoder lete kylle hym make eldred owne ſone kynge edgar regned edwarde ſone begate vpon hys fyrſte wyfe wyll nobly gouerned londe full maner goodnes ledde full holy lyf aboue thynge loued god holy chyrche quene eſcrylde ſtepmoder lete ſlee hym cauſe make owne ſone eldred kynge daye ſlayne ye ſhalle afterwarde ¶it befell thus vpon day tha • kynge edwarde wente woode playe ſouthe coūtree ſyde towne called warham yt whiche foreſte grete pleyntye harte hyndes whan ben whyle hym playe thought vpon broder eldrede hys moder quene place waſte nygh foreſte thought goo thyder vyſyte ſee hys brother toke hym lytell meyne wente hym towarde hys ſtepmoders hous tyme ſoiourned caſtell corfe rede ye thyckenſſe wood ſpeye hys game befell wente amyſſe loſte hys meyne hym came laſte came wood lo • hym ſawe faſt beſydes • e hys ſtepmoder dwelled thyder warde wente alone anone tolde quene kyng comen alone wyth ony company therfore ſhe made ioy ynough thought ſhe myght ſlayne pryuely ſhe myght called one knyghtes whome ſhe tolde moche counſeyll bytwene bothe came kynge curteyſly hym receyued ¶and kynge tolde come vyſyte alſo ſpeke eldred broder quene many tymes hym thankyd hym prayed alyght borugh al yt nyght ¶the kynge ſayd myght agayne wold goo vnto hys folke yf myghte theym fynde ¶and whan quene ſawe wolde abyde ſhe prayed hym wolde one drynke graunted anone drynke come quene dranke vnto kynge kynge tooke cuppe ſette mouth meane whyle dranke falſe knyght yt ye quene knyfe ſmote kyng vnto herte fell downe deed vnto erthe palfroy quene dede gaue knyght golde ſyluer greate plente ryches ynough knyght anone thys done wente hym ouer ſee ſo eſcaped oute londe ¶whan kyng edwarde thus martred yere incarnacyon lorde iheſu cryſte ixclxxx regned xii yere halfe lyeth glaſtenbury ¶of kynge eldred kynge swyne denmake helde englonde eldred ſaynt edwardes brother beloued hys realme therfore fledde normandye edwarde regned eldred brother ſaynt dunſtane crowned hym· ſaynt dunſtane deyed ſoone hadde foryeuen quene treſpa • cauſe ſhe cauſe kynge edwardes deth ſaynt dunſtane aſſoylled penaunce hadde •• oyned ſhe lyued chaſte lyf clene ¶this kynge eldred wedded englyſſhe woman begate edmonde irenſyde ſone called edwyne deyed quene theyr moder ¶and tyme came swyne englonde kyng denmark chalenge conquere auncetrees tyme ſoo conquered axyng ¶for good erle cuthberte lynd eſeye people northumberlonde almooſt al grece englonde helde wyth swyne kyng denmark ſo moche loued • kynge eldred cauſe hys good brother edwarde ſlayn loue hym therfore man ſette lytell hym wherfore kynge swyne hys wyll toke alle londe eldred kynge fledde th • normandye ſoo ſpake duke rycharde duke yaue hym ſyſter emme wyf vpon whiche gate two ſones one called alured edwarde whan swyne conquered londe regned nobly lyued xv yere thenne deyed lyeth yorke ¶how kynge eldred came ayē normandy knoght dane regned warre betwixt hym edmonde irenſyde thus ye deth swyne dane knoght hys ſone dwelled englonde wolde haue ben kynge tho came agayne eldred normandye moche nombre people ſtronge meyne knoght durſte abyde fledde then denmarke kynge eldred agayne reame helde ſo grete worſhyp began deſtroye tho halpe swyne dane ayenſte hym afterwarde came agayne knoghte denmark wyth grete power ſoo kynge eldred durſte hym fyght fledde then vnto london helde hym ¶tho came knoght hym beſyeged ſoo longe tyll kyng eldred deyed cytee london lyeth ſaynt poules regned ix yere bonu • pope benedictꝰ one yere man abode lytell tyme ¶bonifacius pope hym fyue monethes ¶benedictus pope hym x yere man crowned otto ſeedde made many romayns taken gadred counſeyll agaynſt kynge fraunce gylbert nygramancer depoſed ¶iohannes ·xiiii pope hym viii monethes put caſtell aungell famyned dethe ¶iohannes xv pope hym foure monethes ¶iohannes xvi pope hym almooſt xi yere thys man taught armes made many bokes elles lytell hym wryten ¶gregorius v pope man almooſt thre yere gregorius made pope atte inſtaunce emperour otto thyrde conſyn whan hadde lytell whyle pope emperoure receded cyte rome placentinus put crecenſius counſul moneye thenne ſtryfe fewe dayes emperour came ſoone tooke crecenſius conſull ſtroke heed putte eyen man placencius pope ye whiche put coſyn dignyte pope▪ maymed hym membres knyghtes ne duke halpe hym thynge dyde thynge ſholde haue done ſuffred deſerued ¶nota gregorius emperour otto ordeyned cheſers empyre whiche frome then forth hathe bode vnto daye frenſſhmen ne none myghte breke ordynaunce thoſe • er empyre pope otto made ony blame saxon eſchewe euylles come theyr name ben wryten lerned men latyn theſe verſes maguntinenſis treuerenſis colonienſis quilibe • imperu fit cancellarius horum et palatinus da • ifer dux portitorenſis marchio prepoſitus camere pincerna bohemus huſtatuunt dominum cuntis perſecula ſummum palatinꝰ eſt come ren • marcio eſt brandebur genſis dux ſaxorum et rex bohemorum verū vt quidam dicunt ¶thrugh occaſyon egle hathe loſte many feder ende ſhall made naked ¶otto thyrde emperour xviii yere thys man worthy man alle dayes hys empyre wyſdome fader holy faythfull man chirche many bataylles proſperyd cauſe deuoute vnto almyghty god hys ſayntes yaue myghty worſhyppynge ye relykes ſayntes oftentymes vyſyted hooly place ¶this man crowned gregorius hys coſyn atte laſte deceſſyd rome ¶anno dm̄ miiii silueſter seconde pope gregorius foure yere· made pope helpe • deuyll dyde homage ſholde yeue hym thynge deſyred called hylbecte· enmye gate hym grace kynge fraunce made hym byſſhop remenſis anone depoſyd gate grace emperour made byſſhop rauennie pope hadde ende anone ſoo haue put theyr hope fals deuylles ¶yet men truſte ſaluacyon certayne demonſtracyon ſepulcre grete penaunce dyde hys laſt ende made honde legges curte dyſmembred body caſte doore foules thenne body drawen wyth wylde beeſtꝭ ther buryed ſomeuer reſted honde ſtode ſtyl ſaynt iohan lateranenſis buryed ſygne ſaluacon ¶iohannes xviii pope fyue monethes ¶iohannes xix pope hym fyue yere theſe two dyde lytell thynges ¶henricus fyrſte emperour almayne xx yere henricus duke barry accordynge choſen bleſſyd fame good name whiche hadde ¶and redde many theſe duke barry werre holy men abſteydynge fleſſhely dyſyres alſo vertuous lyuynge man ſyſter holy whome yaue wyf vnto kyng hūgry ſhe brought hungry vnto ryght byleue criſten fayth wyues name ſancta konnogundis lyued vyrgyne lyues dayes alſo dyde many batayle well ytaly almayne ayenſt rebellyous proſperyd ryght wyſly atte laſte wyth bleſſyd ende deceſſyd lyfe ſaytn laurēce hys wyf put enſamples ¶benedictꝰ pope iohānes xi yere man hadde grete ſtryfe hys dayes put nother put benedictus deed ſeen holy mā byſſhop wretchyd fygure grete payne thys fygure ſayd truſted thynge mercy god thyng profyted hym yt done hym goten extorcyon vniuſtely thenne byſſhop left byſſhopryche dred thys ſyght went monaſtery lyued vertuouſly hys dayes ¶iohānes x pope hym ·xi yere lytell profyted ¶of kynge knoght dane dethe eldred knoght dane began regne edmonde irenſyde kyng eldredes ſone fyrſte wyf ordeyned grete power men began warre kyng knoghte ſo dyde many tymes often warre ſo ſtronge harde ye wonder wyte· ¶and quene emme dwelled tho weſtmeſtre grete drede two ſones warre alured edwarde leſt ſholde defoyled myſdone thorugh warre wherfore ſhe ſente theym ouer ye ſee normandy ye duke rycharde theyr vncle dwelled ſaufte pea longe tyme ¶this edmonde irenſyde knoght dane warred ſtrongely gyder laſt accorded manere yt ſholde departe ye reame betwixt ſoo dyde became good frendes ſo well loued gyder ben brethern goten one fader one moder borne ¶how kynge edmonde irenſyde traytourſly ſlayne thorugh traytour ralled eldred strotton tho regned kynge irenſyde knoght dane thus befel afterwarde ſame yere accorded ſo moche loued gyder wherfore fals traytour hadde enuytee loue betwixt theym frendſhyp whoos name edrith stratton yt grete lord edmonde irenſydes man hym helde londe neuertheles thought lord betray make knoght kynge londe entente rychely auaūced hym well beloued wherfore prayed hys lord edmonde irenſyde vppon daye wyth hym ete kynge hym curteyſly graunted hym came prayer mete ye kynge ryally ſerued wyth dyuers meeteꝭ drynkes whan nyght came yt ſholde go vnto bedde kynge toke owne meyne went vnto chambre yt ſholde take nyghtes reſte loked hym ſawe fayre ymyge well made ſemblaūt archer boowe boowe fyne arowe ¶kynge edmonde wente tho nere beholde better myght anon arowe ſmote hym thrughe body ſlewe kynge· engyne made ſlee owne lorde traytourſly ¶and ſoo whan kynge edmōde thus deed ſlayne regned x yere peple hym made moche ſorowe body ba • e vnto glaſtenbury theym hym en • yred ¶and fals traytour edrith anone went unto quene kynge edmondes wyf wyſt lordes dethe anone toke frome tow ſones fayre yonge lorde vpon goten one called edward edwyn lawe theym hym londen toke vnto kynge knoght yt ſholde wyth wyll tolde hym ſubtylly ſlayne kyng edmonde cauſe loue hym ſo kynge knoght englonde power hooly myghte haue ¶o thou fals traytoure haſte thou true brother ſoo true thus ſlayne mā moſt loued ye world heed ſhall thy traueyll well rewarde thou haſt deſerued anone lett hym take bounde honde foot maner traytour lete caſt hym tamyſe thys maner fals traytour ended lyf kynge toke two childern put unto abbot weſtmeſtre warde kepe tyll wyſt beſt ¶how kynge knoght ſente kynge edmondes ſones dēmarke ſlayne ſaued befell ſoone kynge knoghte londe honde ſpowſed quene emme thorughe conſente baronage ſhe fayre woman whiche eldredes wyf duke ſyſter normandye lyued togyder moche loue reaſon wolde kynge axed vpon daye counſeyll quene beſt ſonnes edmonde irenſydes syre ſayd ſhe ben ryght heyres ye londe yf lyue wyll moche ſorowe warre therfore lete ſende ſtrange londe ferre ſome man maye defoyle deſtroy kynge anone lete calle dane called walgar commaunded hym ſholde lede tho two childern denmarke ſoo doo ordeyne ſholde neuer theym syr ſayde walgar gladly commaundement ſhall done anone tho two chyldern toke ladde denmarke moche ſawe chyldern wonder fayr alſo meke grete pyte ruthe wolde ſlee ladde kynge hungry nourſſhe walgar well knowen kynge well beloued anone kynge axed whens childern walgar tolde hym ſayde ryght heyres englonde therfore men wolde deſtroye therfore ſyr vnto come mercy helpe ſeke ſothe yf may lyue men ſhal become ſhall holde theyr londe kynge hungry receyued wyth moche honour lete worthely kepte ¶and thus befell warde edwyne ye yonger brother deyed edwarde ye elder brother lyued fayre man ſtronge large body gentyll curteys condycyons ſo yt men hym loued edwarde cronycles called amonge englyſſhmen edwarde ye outlawe ¶and whan made knyght kynges doughter hūgry hym moche loued hys goodnes hys fayrnes ſhe called derlyng kynge fader perceyued well loue betwixt two heyre doughter kyng vowche ſauf doughter man ſo well dyde hym ſhe loued ſoo well yaue vnto hym good wyll edwarde ſpowſed moche honour kynge hungry ſente hys baronage made ſolempne feeſt ryche weddynge made mē vnderſtande edwarde ſholde kynge londe deceſſe hym tydynges full gladde edward begate vppon lady ſone called edgar helynge afterwarde doughter called margarete afterwarde quene scotlonde kynge scotlonde yt called mancolin ſhe doughter called maude yt quene afterwarde englonde thrugh kynge henry fyrſte ſone conquerour wedded begate doughter called maude afterwarde empreſſe almayn maude came ye kynge englonde vnto thys daye called henry empreſſe ſone yet hadde thys edwarde doughter hys wyfe called cryſten ſhe nonne ¶how kynge knoght proude man conquered normandy became afterwarde meke mylde haue herde edmonde irenſydes ſones kynge knoght wende ben ſlayne commaunded walgar before· kynge knoght hadde honde reame englonde denmarke wente vnto norwaye londe conquere kynge lond called elat came people wende londe haue well kepte defended ſoo faught wyth hym tyll laſte ſlayne batayll tho knoght toke londe hys honde whan conquered norway taken feaute homage came ayen englonde helde hym ſelf ſo grete lord hym thought world hys pere noo man came ſoo proude hauteyne grete wonder ¶and ſo befell vpon daye herde maſſe weſtmeſtre wolde haue gone hys palays wayes tamyſe ſo ſwyftely ayenſt hym came almooſt touched foot tho ſayd kynge proude herte cōmaunde water torne ayen elles ſhall make wawes cōmaundemente wolde ſpare flowed euer heyght ¶the kynge ſo proude herte wolde flee water bete rodde hys honde cōmaunded water ſholde go ferder cōmaundemēt water wolde ceſſe euer wexed hygh ſo kyng wete ſtode depe water whan ſawe abyden longe water wolde thynge cōmaundemēt tho ſoone drewe hym tho ſtode vpon ſtone helde hondes hyghe ſayde theſe wordes herynge alle people ¶this god maketh ſee thus aryſe kynge kyngꝭ myghtes mooſt catyf man deedly maye neuer deye thynge dothe hys commaundement hym obedyent ¶to god praye warraunt knowlege caytyf feble power therfore wyll goo vnto rome without ony longe lettynge wyckedneſſe punyſſhe amende god clayme londe holde none anon made redy heyre hym ſelfe wente rome withoute ony lettynge waye dyde many almeſſe dedes whan came rome alſo whan hadde ſynnes doo penaunce came ayen englonde became good man holy lyued lefte alle manere pryde ſtoutenes lyued hooly lyfe made two abbayes af ſaynt benet one englonde normandye moche loued ſaynte benet ſpecyally thanne ſayntes moche loued ſaynt edmonde kynge ofte yaue greate yeftes ſe wherfore made ryche ¶and whan hadde regned xx yere deyed lyeth wyncheſtre ¶anno dm̄ mxviii benedictus ix pope iohannes grete lechour therfore dampned apperyd certayne man vnder meruaylous fygure horryble heed tayle lyke aſſe parte body lyke bere ſayd man apperyd aferde man ye apeyre lyued vnhappely olde tyme lyke beeſt whan pope mannes tyme grete dyuyſyon ſclaūder ye chirche put two tymes ¶and tholomeus noteth pryde byſſhops hadde euer euyll ende euer occaſyon moche vnreſt batayll ¶conradu • ye fyrſt emperour henricus xx yere man made many lawes commaunded pea kepte mooſt ſtraytly ony man erle ludolf accuſed fledde frome londe deſyred lyue lyke churle lyke gentyll man yet meruayllouſly ſone made emperour cōmaundemente god ayenſt wyll conradus laſte accorded toke corodis doughter wyf ¶of kynge harold leuer goo foot ryde hors knoght haue ſpoken hadde two ſones wyf emme one called hardyknoght harold ſo lyght foot men called hym mooſt comynly harolde hare foot harold thynge condycyons maners kyng • noghte fader ſette lytell pryce chyualrye ne noo curteyſe nother worſhyp hys owne wyll became ſoo wycked exyled hys moder emme ſhe went ye lōde flaū dres dwelled erle wherfore neuer good loue betwixt hym broder broder hated hym deedly • whan regned two yere lytell deyed lyeth weſtmeſtre ¶of kynge kariknoght haroldes brother harold hare foot regned brother hardiknoght noble knyghte worthy man moche loued chyualry maner goodnes whan thys hardiknoght regned lytell whyle lette vncouere hys brother harold ſmote heed brother att weſtmeſtre lete caſt heed gonge body tamyſe came fyſſhers toke body theyr nettes nyght bare hym ſaynt clementes chyrche hym caryed maner auenged hym hardiknoght hys broder none maner myght auengeb· kyng hardiknoght ſo large yeuer meete drynke table ſete euery daye thre tymes full ryall meetes drynkes owne meyne came vnto hys courte rychely ſerued ryall meetes thys kynge hardiknoght ſent emme moder made come ayen ī englonde ſhe dryuen englonde whyle harold hare f • ot regned thrugh counſeyll erle godewin yt tho gretteſt lorde englonde next kyng mooſt myght thrugh oute englonde wolde hys cōmaūdement moche hys ſpouſed doughter ye good kyng knoght dane whiche doughter hys fyrſte wyfe ¶and whan quene dryuen englonde come erle flaundres called balde wyne coſyn founde thynge neded vnto tyme ſhe went ayen englonde kynge hardiknoght ſente ſone made come ayen moche honour kynge hardyknoght whan regned fyue yere deyed lyeth weſtmeſtre ¶of vylany dany • dyde ye englyſſhmen wherfore fro ye tyme dane made kynge londe deth kynge hardyknoght moche hadde noo thynge hys body begoten erles baron aſſembled made coūſell neuer noo man ye dane though neuer ſo grete man amonges ſholde neuer kynge englonde deſpyte dane hadde done englyſſhmen euermoore yf ſo englyſſhmen danys hapened mete vpon brydge englyſſhmen ſholde ſo hardy meue ne ſtyre foot ſtande ſtyll tyll dane paſſed ouer yf ye englyſſhmen bowed downe theyr heedes doo reuerence vnto danys ſholde haue ben beten defoylled ſuche maner deſpytes vylany dyde danys englyſſhmen wherfore dryuen ye londe tyme kynge hardyknoght deed lord ye theym myght mayntene ¶and maner auoyded danys englonde neuer came ayen ¶the erles baron theyr comyn aſſent theyr counſelles ſent unto normandy ſeke thoſe two brethern alured edwarde yt dwellyng duke richharde theyr came entente crowne alured elder brother hym make kynge englonde kynge make ende erles baron made theyr othe erle godewin weſtſex falſely traytourſly thought ſlee ſe two brethern anone ſholde come englonde entent make hys ſone harolde kynge whyche ſone begote vp wyf whiche kynge knoghtes doughter dane ſo godewin pryuely hym wente south hampton mete two brethern whan ſholde come vnto london ¶and thus befell meſſengers went normandy foūde oonly alured elder brother edwarde hys brother gone hūgry ſpeke coſyn edwarde outlawe yt edmonde ſone irenſyde meſſengers tolde ſayde alured erles baron englonde ſente hym boldely ſholde come englonde receyue reame kynge hardiknoght deed dane dryuen londe ¶how godewin fals traytour toke alured vppon gyldeſdowne whan came normandy kynge englonde cauſed hym martyred yle ely alured herde theſe tydynges thā ked god ſhyppe went haſt yt myght paſſed ſee arryued southhampton godewin fals traytour whan traytour ſawe come welcomed hym receyued hym moche ioye ſayd wolde lede hym london ye baron englonde hym abode make hym kynge ſo went theyr waye warde london whan came gyldeſdowne tho traytour godewin wonder wroth ſwore bytwene god thē ſholde deye wors deth dyde edrith strattō yt betrayed lord edmonde irenſyde wolde haue pute hym deth ye theyf traytour fledde then denmark helde hym foure yere loſt londe englonde silueſter thyrde pope benedictus ¶thys silueſter choſe benedictus expulſyd warde expulſyd benedictus put vp ayen put gregorius made pope ¶and ſymple lettred man therfore choſe man conſecrate hym whan many men dyſpleaſed wyth thys godynge two pope thyrde brought whyche ſholde occupye place bothe tow ſo ſtroue amonge themſelf henry emperour came thenne rome befell daye went chyrche weſtmeſtre hadde herde maſſe ſaynt iohan euangelyſt moche loued ſaynt iohn̄ euangelyſt ſpecially god hour lady dyde ony ſaynt ſo came hym pelgryme prayed hym loue god lady ſaynt iohan euangelyſt ſome good hym yeue kynge pryuely toke rynge fynder man perceyued yaue pelgryme receyued wente then ¶this kynge edwarde made good lawas englonde yet ben mooſt vſed holden ſo mercyable ſo ful pyte noo man myght ¶how erle godewyn came ayen englonde ayen londe afterwarde ſaynt edwarde weded doughter erle godewin dwellynge denmarke moche herde godneſſe kyng edwarde yt ſo full mercy pyte thought yt wolde go ayen englonde ſeke haue grace good kynge edwarde ſoo mercy full myght haue ayen hys londe pea arayed hym moche myght put hym warde ſee came englonde london kynge tyme lordes englonde helde parlyament godewin ſente hym yt frendes mooſt gretteſt lordes londe prayed beſeche kynges graet hym wolde hys pea londe graunte hym lordes ledde hym kyng ſeke grade anone kynge hym ſawe apeled hym treaſon deth alured brother theſe wordes vnto hym ſayde traytour godewin ſayd kynge appele yt thou haſt betrayed ſlayn brother alured certes ſyr ſayde godewin ſauynge grace pea lordſhyp hym neuer betrayed ne yet hym ſlewe· therfore put rewarde ye courte fayr lordes ſayd kynge ye yt ben lyeges erles baron londe aſſembled fulle welle ye herde appele anſwere alſo godewin therfore woll ye warde dooth ryght erles barones tho gadred togyder warde themſelf ſo ſpake dyuerſely amū ge ſome ſayd neuer alyaunce homage ſeriment ſeruyce ne lordſhyp bytwene godewin alured whyche thynge myght hym drawe att laſte deuyſyd demed ſholde put hym ye kynges mercy togyder tho ſpake ye erle leuerik couentree good mā god worlde tolde hys reaſon manere ſayd erle godewin beſt fended man englonde kynge well myght agayne ſayd ye wythout counſell godwin alured neuer put dethe wherfore warde towchynge parte hymſelf hys ſone euery v xii erles ben hys frendes goo kynge charged moche golde ſyluer maye bere betwyxt hondes praynge ye kyng forgyue euyll wyll erle godewin receyue hys homage londe yelde ayen accorded vnto warde came thys maner aboueſayd euery holde ſyluer moche myght bere bytwene hondes kynge ſayd fourme maner accorde theyr warde kyng wolde theym agayne ſaye moche ordeyned graunted confermed ſo ye erle godewin accorded kynge ſo ayen londe afterwarde bare hym ſo well ſo wyſely kynge loued hym wonder moche hym fulle preuy within lytell tyme loued ſo moche kynge ſpowſed godewyns doughter made quene neuertheleſſe though kyngge wyf yet lyued euer chaſtyce clē neſſe body without ony fleſſhely dede doynge wyf quene alſo halfe ladde holy lyf two yere deyed afterwarde kyng lyued hys lyf without ony wyf ¶the kynge yaue erledome oxenforde harolde godewyns ſone made hym erle ſo well beloued bothe fader ſo pryue kyng fader ſone myghte doo ryght thynge wolde ayenſt ryght wolde nothynge doo noo maner man ſoo good true conſcyence therfore oure lorde iheſu cryſte greate ſpecyall loue vnto hym ſhewed ¶how kyng edwarde ſawe swyne kynge denmark drowned ſee tyme sacrament ſtode herde maſſe befelle vppon wytſondaye kynge edwarde herde maſſe greate chyrche weſtmeſtre nyghe att leuacyon iheſu cryſtis body alle men gadred chyrche came nyght awter ſee ſacrynge kyng hondes lyfe vp hygher grete laughter toke vp wherfore aboute hym ſtode gretely ganne wonder maſſe axed kynges laughter fayre lorde ſayd kyng edwarde ſawe swyne yonger kynge denmarke come ſee hys power haue come englonde vpon v warre ſawe hym hys folke drowned ſee thys ſawe leuacyon cryſtis body bytwene ye preeſtes hondes therfore ſo grete ioye myght laughter withholde ¶and erle leueryk beſyde hym ſtode leuacyon openly ſawe ye fourme brede torne lykeneſſe yonge chylde tooke vp hys ryght honde bleſſyd kynge erle erle anone torned hym ward ye kȳge make hym ſee ye hooly ſyght ſaide ye kynge ¶syre erle ſayde ſee welle yt ye ſee thā ked god haue honoured god ſauoyour vyſybly iheſu cryſt fourme man whoos name bleſſyd worldes ¶how rynge ſaynt edwarde gyuen poore pelgryme loue god ſaynt iohan euangelyſt came ayen kynge edwarde thys noble man saynt edwarde regned xiii yere thus befelle vpon tyme deyed two men englonde gone holy londe done theyr pelgrymage goynge ayen theyr owne countree came fro went ye waye mette pylgryme curtely theym ſaluwed axed londe countree borne ſayd englonde tho axed kynge englonde anſwered ſayd good kyng edwarde ¶fayre frendes ſayd tho pelgryme whan yt ye come countres ayen praye yt ye wyll go vnto kynge edwarde oftentymes grete hym myn name oftentymes hym thanke hys grete curteyſy hath done namely rynge ye haue whan hadde herde maſſe weſtmeſtre ſaynt iohans loue euangelyſt toke ye pelgremes ſayd pray go bere rynge take vnto king edwarde tel hym ſende hym full ryche yefte wyll hym yeue vpon x daye ſhall come unto euermore dwelle bleſſe without ony ende ¶syr ſayde ye pelgremes mē ye countree dwellynge ¶fayr frendes ſayd iohn̄ euāgelyſte dwellynge almyghty god kynge edwarde frende loue hym ī ſpecyal chauſe hath euermore lyued clenneſſe clene mayde praye meſſage fulfyll haue ſayd whan ye ſaynt iohan euangelyſt thus charged ſodenly voyded theyr ſyghtes bothe pelgrymes tho thanked almyghty god wene forth theyr waye whan hadde gone two thre myle begā waxe wery ſette downe reſt ſo felle one ſlepe whan ſlepte well one woke lyfe vp hys heed loked ſayd felowe aryſe vp walke way ſayd one felowe vnto certes ſayde ſemeth yt ſame coūtree layde v downe reſt ſlepe ieruſalem thre myle toke vp theyr hondes bleſſyd went forth theyr way went theyr waye ſawe ſhep • goynge wyth theyr ſhepe ye ſpake none langage englyſſhe ¶good frendes ſayd one pelgrymes countree lorde therof ¶and one ſheperdes anſwered ſayd ye coūtree kent englonde whiche good kyng ſaynt iohn̄ charged al thynges hadſped waye tooke rynge kynge edwarde tooke • thanked almyghty god ſaynt iohn̄ euangelyſt tho made hym redy euery daye fro daye daye departe thys lyf whan god wolde hym ſende ¶how ſaynt edward dyed ye twelfth day befell thus cryſtmaſſe euen holy man edwarde goodes ſeruyce matyns hereof hyghe ſolempne feeſt became full lyke morowe endured moche payne maſſe maſſe lette hym ladde chambre reſte hym hys halle amonge hys baron knyghtes myght come theym comforte ſolace wonte ye worthy feeſt wherfore theyr myrth comforte amonge halle torned care ſorowe cauſe dradde leſe godewyn thrugh grete lordes reame yt kynne vnto hym ſybbe ſeaſed englōde hys honde anone lette crowne hym kynge enterement saynt edware harolde godewynes ſone ſeconde yere afore ſaynt edwarde deed aſmoche harolde noble wyſe knyght worthy body hys fader accorded good kynge edwarde therfore wolde myſdo hym manere thynges betwext ſpoken ordeyned harolde hys good wyll ſwore vpon boke vpon • oly duke wyllyam lette hym goo yaue hym many ryche yeftes tho wente then came englonde anone dyde manere whan saynte edwarde deed man falſly ſworne lette crowne hym kynge englonde falſely brake coue name yt hadde made wyth duke wyllyam wherfore wonder wroth wyth hym ſwore wolde vppon hym auenged ſome euer hym befell ¶and anone duke wyllyam lette aſſemble grete hoſte came englonde aueng • hym vppon harolde conquere londe yf myght ¶and ſame yere harolde crowned haralde hereſtynge kynge denmarke arryued scotlō de thought haue kynge englonde came englonde robbed deſtroyed myght tyll came yorke ſlewe many men armes thouſande hondred preeſtes whā tydynges came kynge aſſembled grete power wente fyght haralde denmarke wyth hys owne hondes de hym ſlewe dane dyſcomfyted tho lefte lyue wyth moche ſorowe fledde theyr ſhyppes thus kynge harolde englonde ſlewe kynge haralde denmarke ¶anno dm̄ mlxvi ¶how wyllyam baſtarde duke normandy came englonde ſlewe kyng harolde ¶here come norman expulſyd ſoldyurs vpon daye ſate atte meete meſſager came hym ſayde wyllyam baſtarde duke normandy arryued englonde greate hoſte take londe haſtynge alſo myned caſtell whā kynge herde tydynges wente thyther hym truage wolde determyne thys thynge batayll harolde proude man ſtronge truſted wonder moche vpon ſtrength faught duke wyllyam people harolde men batayll dyſcō fyted hymſelfe ſlayne thys batayll yere regne came ayen englonde brought hym maude wyf lette crowne quene englonde oon wytſondaye ¶and tho anone kynge scotlonde thoe called malcolin began ſtryue warre kyng wylyam ordeined hym towarde scotlonde men lō de ſee deſtroye kynge malcolin accorded kynge scotlonde became hys man helde hys londe hym kynge wyllyam receyued hym homage came ayen englonde kynge wyllyam hadde kynge xvii yere maude quene deyed kynge wyllyam hadde begote many fayr chyldern ſaye robert curthos wylllyam rous richarde alſo deyed henry· beauclerke maude alſo erles wyf bleynes foure fayr doughters ¶and wyues ſykeneſſe wolde lyghten thouſande condelles kynge fraūce anone lete aſſemble grete hoſt normandy englyſſhe men begynnynge herueſt came fraunce brente townes came thrugh coūtree robbed dyde ye ſorowe myght thrugh fraunce ye laſt brenned cyte mandos cōmaunded people bere wood moche myght brenne hym ſelf halpe ther ye myghte good wyll greate hete fyre ſo grete ſonne wōdder hote ſtuffed hym ſo yt ſacramē tꝭ holy chyrche deyed ye xx yere regne lyeth cane normandy ¶anno dm̄ mlxvi gregorius vii pope alexander xii yere man ordeyned generall synodus preeſt ſholde haue wyf ne ſholde dwelle wymmen tho holy synodus micena decree ſuffred then̄e preeſtꝭ ſette nought lytell pondred hys ordynaunce pope cōmaunded man ſholde maſſe preeſt concubyne acertayne tyme whan cardynall legate fraunce proceded holy londe forſayd kinges tyme fals cryſten man became ſarraſyne whyle thys kynge regned grete bataylle holy londe bytwene cryſten men ſarraſyns cryſten men ſlayne thrugh greate treaſon ye erle tyrpe wolde haue wyf quene iheruſalem ſomtyme baldewynes wyfe ſhe forſoke hym toke lorde knyght worthy man called ſyr gnyperches wherfore erle tyrpe wroth wente anone ryght soudan soudan babylon became man forſoke hys cryſtendome alle cryſten lawe ceryſten men wyſt dedes wende haue grete helpe hym wonte haue ¶and whan came bataylle thys fals creſten man torned vnto sarraſyns forſoke owne nacyon ſoo brynge before▪ hym man yt hym ſo hurt ſo wounded whan came ye kyng kyng axed hym name ſayd name bertham gurdon wherfore ſayd kynge haſte thou ſlayne ſyth dyd neuer none harme syr ſayd though ye dyde abode· viii daye may kynge made anothe • ſtande pope ordynaunce pandulf ye legate maner thynges whyche accurſyd ſholde make full reſtytucyon mē holy chyrche relygyon goodes taken ayenſt theyr wyll therfore almyghty god hym hathe ſyns ſhewed many fayre myracle dyuers men wymmen ye ſykeneſſe dyſceaſe haue loue hym ¶and merlyon alſo ſayd prophecye afer tyme lame ſholde lyue whyle thenne ſeed ſholde ſtraunge londe wythout ony paſture ſayd ſothe kyng henry lyued whyle symonde mounforde ſlayne kynge henry ne deyed anone hym meane tyme ſyre edwarde hys ſone beſte kyng worlde ef honour tho holy lond gate acre countree begate vpon dame elenore wyf iohan acre hys doughter afterwarde counteſſe glocetre made ſuche vyage holy londe worlde ſpake knyghthode euery man dradde hym hye lowe thorughout cryſtendome ſtorye hym telleth afterwarde ye ſhall openly ¶and tyme yt kynge henry deyed tyll ſyr edward crowned kynge al grete lordes englonde faderles childern wythout ony ſocoure theym myght mayntene gouerne defende ayenſt theyr deedly enmyes gregorius ix pope honorius thys man canonyſed many ſayntes defended myghtely ye chyrche ayenſt frederyk therfore tooke many prelate two cardynalles whiche wente counſeyll ayenſt hym pope ſegyd cyte rome emperour ſawe romayne corrupte moneye emperour thenne toke hys honde heedes appoſtles peter poule went proceſſyon fro chyrche ſaynt iohn̄ latranente ſaynt peter chyrche ¶and ſo gate hertꝭ romayns emperour went fayr waye fro cyte pope made frere ianond compyle fyue bokes decretales many pyſtles decree many trybulacōns chyptyraūt deceſſyd wente heuen ¶celeſtinus fourth pope gregorius almooſt moneth lyf hys conynge laudable olde man feble deceſſyd pope hym almooſt xii month ¶innocenciꝰ fourth pope hym almooſt xi yere vi monethes thys man canonyſed many ſayntes frederyke emperour depoſyd enmye vnto god thyrde yere made pope holpe ianuencꝭ ¶thenne henry ſixt choſen wyllyam pope commaundement ayenſt frederyk one preuayled ouercome hys tyranny ouermyghty ne theſe crowned deceſſyd anone ¶thomas de alquine holy doctour albertus magnus byſſhop ratyſponens euſtacius bonouenture deuoute doctour thys tyme whiche deſtroyed moche hereſye enfected emperour ¶alexander pope innocencius viii yere lytell hym wryten ¶vrbanus hym thre yere thre monethes man droue awaye hoſt sarraſyns men marked croſſe whiche maufred ſent ayenſt chyrche pope toke kyngdome cecyle kynges brother fraunce yt ſholde fyght maufrede thenne deceſſyd maufrede loſte lyf kyngdom bi karolus· ¶alphō ſus kynge caſtell rychardes brother kynge englonde erle corne waylle choſen emperours longe vacacyon empyre cheſers emperour diuyded ſondre grete ſtryfe many yere laſt deceſſyd rycharde alphonſus came agaye afore gregorius ix ſygne pea • vtterly renoūced tytle empyre hadde ony wytty mā noble aſtronemer hys table ben famous whiche made compendyons ¶clemens fourth pope vrbanus iii yere ix· monethes clemēs holy man ſayd thrugh ſpyryte prophecy yt enmyes chyrche ſhold peryſſhe ſmoke byleued god ceſſyd trybulacyons chyrche thorugh merytes thys man afore wyf chyldern whan preeſt byſſhop ſente englonde legate thynge knowyng choſen pope deceſſyd bleſſydly hys vertuous lyuynge ¶gregorias x pope hym foure yere made pope deſyre holy londe whyche entended vyſyte perſonally • e londō fraunce made ſolempne counſeyll wihche counſeyll grekes tartar grekꝭ promyſed refourmed vnyte chirche tartar lytell afore baytyſed promyſed ſame gadred vic byſſhops prelate therfore certayne man ſayde gregorius gadred togyder kynde people decreed perſones vycaryes ſhold called preeſtꝭ prelate yt man ſholde aſſygne tythes chyrche wolde dyed afore ſholde payed moder chirche dampned ye pluralyte benefyces deyed bleſſyd man ¶innocencius v hym v monethes lytell dyd ¶adrianus hym • monethe dyde leſſer ¶iohānis x • hym viii monethes dyuers ſcyences famous man maners fole deceſſyd anone ¶nicholaus thyrd pope iohn̄ oo yere thys mā dayes buldynge noble man well gouerned cyte dayes ſecō de yere deceſſyd ¶radulphus emperour xviii yere man erle hanebrough wyſe mā armes noble vyctoryous choſen baſyle· toke ye croſſe hym holy londe thimperyall bleſſynge pope alowed eleccyon fauour holy londe ¶anno dm̄ mcclxxiiii mar • inus ye iiii pope nycholaus iiii yere thys man grete louer relygyous men great attendynge vertuous werkes thys man curſyd emperour conſtantynople ſo moche promyſed torme fayth generall counſeyl▪ dyde whyche ſuffred many paſſyons holy chyrche alſo curſyd kyng aragon expulſyd kyng cecyle fro kyngdome done many bataylles ayenſt men myſbyleue many trybulacōns ſuffred deceſſyd dyd many miracle ¶nycholaꝰ delira noble douctour dyuyte thys tyme parys man iewe nacyon cōuerted myghtely profyted ordre frere mynours wrote ouer byble grelles yere lord m·cccxxx ſome man ſay braban yt fader moder cryſtne pouerte vyſyted ye ſcole ye iewes ſo lerned iewes langage elles thys nycholaꝰ informed iewes hys yonge aege ¶honorius ye fourth pope martynꝰ two yere lytell hym y wryten temperat man dyſcerte ¶nicholaus fourth pope hym foure yere man frere mynor although good man himſelf yet many vnhappy thynges fell tyme ye chirche many batayll ye cyte thrugh occaſyon drewe moche one parte hym thre pope two yere vi monethes ¶how kynge edwarde kynge henryes ſone kyng henry regned edwarde hys ſone worthyes knyght worlde honour goddes grace hym vyctorye hys enmyes ſoone hys fader deed came london noble company prelate erles baron mē dyd hym moche honour euery place ye ſyr edwarde rode london ſtretes couered ouer hys heed ſylke tapiſcery riche couerynges ioye comynge burgeys cyte caſte theyr wyndowes golde ſyluer hondes full tokenynge loue worſhyp ſeruyce reuerence condyte chepe ranne whyte wyne reed ſtremes water euery man dranke therof ye wolde theyr owne wyll kyng edwarde crowned enoynted ryght heyer englonde moche honour maſſe ye kynge wente place holde ryall feeſt amō ge dyde hym honour whan ſette meete kynge alexander scotlonde came hym honour reuerence q • eynteſye hondred knyghtes hym well horſyd arayde whan alyght theyr ſtedes lete theym go whether wolde myght take tooke theyr owne wyll wythout ony chalenge·r came ſyre edmonde kynge edwardes brother curteys knyght gentyll renowne erle corne wayllle erle gloceſtre thenne came erle penbroke erle garenne eche themſelf ladde theyr honde hondred knyghtes gayly dyſgyſed theyr armes whan alyghted theyr horſes lete go whether welde yt myght catche haue ſtyll without ony chalenge whan done kyng edwarde dyde dylygence myghte amende dreſſe wronges beſte manere myght honour god holy chyrche mayntene honoure amende noyannce comyn people ¶how ydeyne lewelyns doughter walys prynce aymer ye erles brother moūforde taken ſee fyrſte afterwarde ye kynge edwarde crowned lewelyn prynce wale ſent faraunce erle moūforde thorough coūſeyl frendes ye erle ſholde wedde doughter erle tho auyſed hym vpō thynge ſent vnto lewelyn ſayd wolde ſende hys doughter ſo ſent aymer broder damoyſell lewelyn arayed ſhyphes doughter syre aymer faare company ſholde goo lewelyn dyd grete wronge couenaūted ſholde yeue hys doughter manere man without counſell conſente kyng edwarde ſo befell burgeys bryſtow came ſee wyne laden mette toke myght power anone burgeys ſent theym kyng whan lewely herde tydynges wroth alſo ſorowfull· gan warre vpon kynge edwarde dyde moche harme vnto englyſſhmen bete downe ye kynges caſtels began deſtroye kynge edwardes londe whā tydynges cam vnto ye kyng thyng wente walys ſo moche dyde thorough goddes grace grete power drofe lewelyn vnto grete myſchyef fledde maner ſtrength came yelded hym vnto kyng edwarde yaue hym l marke ſyluer haue pea toke damoyſell herytage made oblygacōn kynge edwarde come parlyamente two tymes yere ſeconde yere kynge edwarde crowned helde generall parleamente att weſtmeſtre made ſtatutes defaute lawe comune aſſent baronage eſter nexte ſewenge kynge ſente letter vnto lewelyn prynce wale ſholde come parlemēt londe hys holdynge wale ſtrenthe letter oblygatory wytneſſyd tho lewelyn ſcorne dyſpyte kynges commaundement pure wrache ayen began warre vpon kyng edwarde deſtroyed londe tho whan kynge edwarde herd theſe tydynges wexed wonder wrothe vnto lewelyn haſt aſſembled people went hym warde wale warred ſo vpon lewelyn prynce tyll broughte hym moche ſorowe dyſeaſe lewelyn ſawe defence myghte hym auaylle came ayen yelded hym ye kynges grace cryed hym mercye longe tyme kneled kynges fote kynge hym pyte cōmaunded hym aryſe mekenes foryaue hym hys wrathe hym ſayd yf treſpaſſed hym nother tyme wolde dyſtroye hym euermore ¶dauid lewelyns brother ſame tyme dwelled kynge edwarde felle man ſubtyll enuyous alſo ferre caſtynge moche treaſon thoughte· euermore made good ſemblame ſemyd ſoo true noo man myght perceyue falſnes ¶how lewelyn thrugh eggynge brother dauyd werryd agayn vpō kȳg edward longe tyme ye kynge edwarde yaaf dauyd lewelyns broder lordſhyppe frodeſham made hym knyght ſo moche honour dyde neuer mā walys cauſe hym kynge edwarde helde parlemente london whan hadde walys wolde chaunged moneye full yll kytte wherfore people playned ſore kynge enquered treſpaſſours thre houndred atteynted ſuche maner falſnes wherfore ſome hanged ſomme drawen hangyd ¶and afterwarde kynge ordeyned ſterlynge halfpeny ſholde go thorugh hys londe commaūded man fro daye afterwarde yaue ne feoffed hous religyō londe tenemente without ſpecyall leue kynge yt dyde ſholde punyſſhed att kynges wyll yeft ſhall nought longe ye lewelyn prynce walys thrugh tycemente dauyd hys brother bothe theyr conſente thought dyſheryte kynge edwarde aſmoche myght ſo thorugh ye kynges pea broken whan kynge edwarde herde anon ſent baron northumberlonde surrey alſo yt ſholde go take theyr vyage vpon ye traytours lewelyn dauyd wonder herde warre tho wynter ī walys whan coūtres somer lewelyn lete ordeyne well arayed vytayll hys good caſtell swandon ther huge nombre people plente vytaylles ſo kynge edwarde wyſt wher entre whan kynges men perceyuer alſo ſtrenth walys lete come ſee bargee botes grete plankys many myght ordeyne haue go ſayd caſtell swandon wyth men foot alſo hors walſſhmen ſo moche people ſo ſtronge draue englyſſhmen ayen ſo yt ther ſo moche preſſe people ye tornynge ayen ye charge burden men made ye bargee botes ſynke drowned many good kynght yt ſay ſyr robert clyfford ſyr wyllyam lyndeſeye yt was· ſyre iohn̄s ſone fitz robert ſyr rychard tanny ā huge nombre thrugh owne foly yf good eſpyes harmyd whan kynge edwarde herde tell hys people ſo drowned▪ made ſorowe ynough tho came ſyr iohan veſſy frome kynge▪ aragon brought wyth hym moche people bachelers gaſcoynes ſouldyurs dwelled ſayde iohn veſſy receyued hym wage hym witholde noble men fyght brente many townes ſlewe moche people walſſhmen myght take tho wyth ſtrenth myght made aſſawte vnto caſtell swandon gate caſtell whan dauyd prence brother herde tydynges ordeyned hym flyght lewelyn prynce ſawe broder fledde ſore abaſſhed power warre mayntene ſoo lewelyn gan flee wynde well haue ſcapedde morowe ſyre roger mortymer mette wyth hym oonly wyth x knyghtes ſette hym rounde aboute hym went ſmote hys heed preſented ye ſame heed vnto kynge edwarde thys manere lewelyn prynce walys taken hys heed ſmyten alſo alle hys heyres dyſheryted euermore thrugh ryght full dome lordes reame ¶how dauyd lewelyns broder prynce walys put dethe dauid prynces broder walys thrugh pryde wende haue prynce walys brother dethe vpon ſent walſſhemen hys parleament dynbygh folyſſhely made walys aryſe ayenſt kynge began meue warre ayenſt kynge edwarde dyde ſorowe dyſeaſe myghte hys power whan kynge edwarde herde thys thynge ordeyned men purſewe vppon hym dauyd fyerſly hym defended tyll ye came towned ſaynt morice dauyd take fledde ladde kynge kynge cōmaunded ſholde hangyd drawen ſmyte hys heed quarter hym ſende hede london foure quarter ſende foure chyef townes walys ſholde take enſample therof beware afterwarde kynge edwarde lete crye pea thrugh walles ſeaſed londe honde grete lordes left alyue came feaute homage kynge edwarde theyr kynde lorde tho lete kyng edwarde amende lawes walys defectyue ſent ye lordes walys letter patentes ſholde come parlament whan come yu kyng ſayd full curteyſly lordynges ye welcome behoueth counſeyll helpe go vnto gaſcoyne amende treſpaſſe yt done whan entreate pea bytwene kynge aragon prynce morrey ye kynges lyege men erles baron cōſented graū ted therto tho made hym kynge edwarde redy went gaſcoyne lete amende treſpaſſes yt hym done gaſcoyne debate yt bytwene kynge aragon prynce morrey ſeſſyd made theym accorded whyle good kyng edwarde elynore wyf gaſcoyne good erle cornewayll made wardeyn englonde tyll kynge edwarde came ayen tho enquered hys traytours yt coniected falſeneſſe agaynſt hym eche receyued ther dome deſerue meane tyme good kynge edwarde beyonde ſee doo make amendes ayenſt hym treſpaſſyd ther falſe yf traytoure called ryſap merydok began make werre ayenſt kyng edwarde yt cauſe ſyr payne typtot wrongfully greued dyſceaſed forſayde ryſap meradok whan kyng edwarde herde matere well vnderſtode anone ſente hys letter pryue ſeale forſayd rebellyō ryſap merydok ſholde begynne maner wyſe make reyſe werre yt ſholde pea loue whan came ayen englonde wolde vnder take quarell amende al yt myſdon forſayd ryſap merydok dyſpyſed kynges commaundement ſpared doo ſorowe myght kynges men englond anon take ladde yorke drawen hangyd felonye ¶of dreſſyng kynge edwarde made iuſticꝭ clerkes done ther falſnes draue iewes englonde ther vſury myſbyleue kynge edwarde dwelled thre yere gaſcoyne deſyre came goo englonde ayen whan come ayen foūde ſo many playntes made hym iuſtyces clerkes done ſo many wronges falſneſſe yt wonder whiche falſneſſe ſyre thomas waylond ye kynges iuſtyce ſwore englonde toure london falſneſſe mē put vpon hym wherfore atteynt proued fals· anone whan kyng done wyll iuſtices tho lete enquere eſpye iewes dyſceyued begyled people thorugh ſynne falſneſſe vſury lete ordeyne preuy parlement amonge lordes ordeyned amonge theym iewes ſholde voyde englonde theyr myſbyleue alſo theyr fals vſury dyde vnto cryſten men ſpedde make ende thynge comyn alte englonde yaue vnto kynge xv peny theyr goodes meuable ſoo iewes dryuen oute englonde tho went iewes fraunce dwellyd thorugh leue kynge phylyp tho kynge fraunce ¶how kynge edwarde ſeaſed alle londe scotlonde cōſente graunte lordes scotlonde· longe alexandre kynge scotlonde dede dauyd erle huntyngdon kynges brother scotlonde axed claymed kyngdom scotlond brother deed cauſe yt ryghtfull heyre many grete lordes ſayd nay wherfore greate debate aroſe bytwene theym frēdes aſmoche wolde conſente hys coronacyon meane tyme forſayd dauyd deyed ſo befell ye ſayd dauyd thre doughters yt worthyly maryed fyrſt doughter maryed bayloll ſeconde brus thyrde haſtynges forſayd bayloll brus chalenged ye londe scotlonde greate debate ſtryf aroſe bytwene cauſe eche wolde haue kynge· whan lordes scotlonde ſaw debate bytwene came kynge edwarde englonde ſeaſed hym londe scotlond chyef lord whā kyng ſeaſed ye forſayd lordes ye forſayd baylol brus haſtinges came kynges courte axyd kyng whyche ſhold kynge scotlonde kyng edwarde ye full gentyll true lete enquyre cronycles scotlonde greteſt lordes scotlonde whiche eldeſt blood foūde baylol eldeſt ye kyng scotlond ſholde holde kynge englonde hym frauce homage done baylol went scotlōde crowyed kynge scotlonde ¶and ye ſame tyme vpon ſee grete warre bytwene englyſſhemen norman vpō tyme norman arryued douer ther martred holy mā called thomas douer afterwarde normās ſlayne eſcaped one thē ¶and ſo afterwarde kynge edwarde ſholde lete duchye gaſcoyne thrugh kynge phylyp fraūce thrugh fals caſtynge douſepers londe wherfore ſyr edmond kynge edwardes brother yaue vp domage vnto kynge fraūce ¶and tyme clerkes englond graunted kynge edwarde half • eale holy chirche goodes helpynge recouer londe agayne gaſcoyne kyng ſent thether noble company hys bachelers hymſelf wolde haue gone portelmouth let thrughe one maddok walys yt ſeaſed caſtell swandon honde cauſe kynge torned walys criſtmaſſe cauſe noble lordꝭ englond yt ſent gaſcoyne comforth lorde kynge take ſyr charlys fraūce yt ſay ſyr iohn̄ brytayne ſyr robert tiptot ſyr raufe tanny ſyr hugh bardolfe ſyr adam cretynge yet att aſſenſyon maddok take walys nother called morgan ſent tour london byheded ¶how syre iohan baylol kyng scotlonde ſayde homage whan ſyre iohn̄ baylol kynge scotlonde vnderſtande ye kynge edwarde werred gaſcoyne ye reame scotlond delyuerd falſly tho ayenſt othe ſayd homage thrugh procurynge folke ſent vnto ye court rome thrugh fals ſuggeſtyon aſſoylled othe yt ſwore vnto kyng englonde ſoo letter enbulled ¶tho choſe scotlonde douſepers brnyge edward ryght ¶and ye tyme came two cardynalles ye cource rome fro pope celeſtme trete acorde bytwene ye kyng englōd tho cardinalles ſpake accorde thā turbeluyll takē lyon made homage warde parys put ſones hoſtage thought go englonde aſpye countre tell whan came englond broken kynges pryſon fraunce ryght ſaid wolde yt englyſſhmen walſhemen ſholde aboute kynge brynge ende ſwore vpon thys couenaunt dedes made bytwene ſholde haue yere thouſand poūdes worth londe byrnge thynge ende fals traytour toke leue wente then came englonde vnto kynge ſeyd broke oute pryſon yt put hym ſuche peryll loue wherfore kyng cowde hym moche thanke full gladde comynge ¶and fals traytoure fro daye aſpyed doynge kynge alſo counſelle kyng loued hym full welle hym full preuy clerke englonde kynges hows fraunce herde treaſon falſneſſe wrote another clerke tho dwellynge edwarde kynge englonde thomas turbeluyll hadde done fals c • niectynge counſelle englonde wryte haue ſende vnto kynge fraunce ¶and thoruhhe forſayde letter clerke hadde ſente fro fraunce founde vppon wherfore ledde london hangyd drawe treaſon hys two ſones hadde put fraunce hoſtage thenne beheeded ¶of conqueſt berwyke whan twoo cardynalles gone agayne fraunce trete pea cambroy kynge ſent thether erles baron ſaye ſyr edmonde broder erle lancaſtre lecetre ſyr henry lacy erle nychol wyllyam veſſy baron baronettes aboute xiii beſt wyſeſt englonde ¶and ſame tyme kynge edwarde toke vyage scotlonde werre vpon iohn̄ baylol kynge scotlonde ¶and ſyr robert roos berwyk ſledde fro ye englyſſhmen wente scottes kyng edwarde wente hym towarde berwyk beſegyd towne tho within manly defended ſette fyre brente two kynge edwardes ſhyppes ſayde dyſpyte reprey • hym wenyth kynge edwarde longe ſhankys haue gete berewyk vnthankes gas pykes hym whan doon gas dyke hym whan kyng edwarde thys ſcorne anone thorugh hys myghteneſſe paſſed ouer dyches aſſaylled towne came yates gate conquered towne thrughe hys gracyous power ſlewe xxv thouſande vii hondred ſcottes kynge edwarde loſte man renoune ſaufe ſyr rycharde cornewayle hym kylled flemynge redde halle quarell forſayd rycharde dyde hys helme comaunded theym yelde put kynges grace ye scottes wolde wherfore halle brent caſt downe tho therin brente kynge edwarde loſte noo moo men vyage ſymple eſtate xxvii englyſſhemen wardeyn caſtell yaue vp keyes ye caſtell wythout ony aſſawte taken ſyre wyllyam douglas symonde fryſell erle patryk yelded pea ingham humbreſmylle robert brus kynge edwarde forſoke kynge edwarde helde scottes afterward taken put pryſon tho lete kynhe edwarde cloſe berwyk wyth walles dyches robert rous went tyndale ſette wuyerbrydge fyre exham lamerſtok ſlewe robbyd folke countree wente fro then dunbarre fyrſte weneſdaye marche kynge ſent erle garenne ſyr hugh percy ſyre hugh spenſer wyth fayre company beſege caſtell one called ſyre rycharde sywarde men fared within caſtell ¶and hym worde yf wolde remeue ſege englyſſe men wolde yelde caſtell vnto englyſſhe men ¶the meſſenger tho came ſyr iohan baylol tho kynge scotlōde wyth hooſte meſſenger tolde hym caas ſyr iohan toke hoſte came morowe erly towarde caſtell ſyr rycharde ſywarde ſawe hym come yt mayſter counſeyll keper caſtell ſayd vnto englyſſgmen ſayde ſee fayre company well apparelled wyll goo ayenſte theym wyth mete theym aſſaylle ſyr hughe spenſer ſawe falſneſſe hym· ye treſon· ſayd hym traytour take proue falſneſſe ſhalle auaylle hughe spenſer commaunded anone bynde hym haſt edwarde ſoo take caſtell thre erles vii baron xxxviii knyghtes xi clerkes vii pycardys preſentyd kynge edwarde ſente thē towre london kepte ¶how kynge edwarde greate grace delyuered ayen scottes oute hym grace ledde london whan kyng edwarde come thether brough hym kynge axed howe wolde make amendes treſpaas loſſe doon hym put theym mercy lordynges ſayde kynge wyll londes ne goodes wyll ye make othe vpō goddys body true neuer tyme ayenſt bere armys▪ conſentyd kynges wyl ſwore vpon goddys body ſaye ſyr iohn̄ comyn erle scra • hron erle carryk alſo foure byſſhops vndertoke clergye ſo kynge delyuered thē yaue ſauf conduyce go ther owne londe longe afterwarde ne aryſe ayenſt kynge edwarde cauſe wyſt well kynge edwardes folke take gaſcoyne ſayd ſyr iohn̄ bayloll kynge scotlonde wyſte well londe ſholde haue ſorowe ſhame theyr falſneſſe· haſt wēte hym ouer ſee owne londes helde hym came neuer ayen wherfore scottes choſe vnto theyr kynge wyllyam waleys rybaude harlot comen vp nought moche harme dyde englyſſhmen kyng edwarde thoughte myght haue delyueraunce peple take gaſcoyne ī haſt wente hym ouer ſee flaunders werre vpon kyng fraūce erle flaunders receyued hym wyth moche honour grayntyd hym londys hys owne wyll whan kynge fraunce herde telle kyng englonde aryued flaundres came wyth greate power hym dyſtroye prayed hym trewes two yere ſo englyſſhe marchauntes alſo frenche myght ſaufly go come bothe ſydes kynge edwarde graūted •• ſo muſte haue men pryſon gaſcoyne kynge fraunce anone graunted ſo delyuerd ¶and ye ſame tyme scottes ſente ye byſſhop ſaynt andrewes hym folowed dr • ue hym tyll cam stryuelyn helde hym caſtell walſſhmen euery daye eſcryed menacyed dyde dyſpyte myghte ſoo englyſſhmen vpon tyme mornynge went fro caſtell moūtenaunce x myles paſſed
