experte ſuche mater bycauſe pere put meſure hys prudence toke ſo grete pryde vpon hym ſayd lord worlde many thynges dyde myght power· whyche fayled wretchedly ende yaue enſample prelatis yt ſholde haue ne proude vnder fourme ſhepeherde god ſhod • ſtudy belouyd ſubgectes thā dradde man ſayd yt entred fox lyued lyon deyed dogge ¶this tyme ye yere grace ordeyned hoūdred yere hondred yere fyrſte iubyle yere lord iheſu cryſt thouſande thre hoūdred ¶benedictus enleuenth bonefacius xi monethes man holy man ordre frere prechers lytyll whyle lyued dyſſeſſyd anone adulphus emperour vi yere man erle anoxone adulphus crowned pope ſlayne batayll ¶albertus emperour hym ·x yere man duke aſtryr fyrſte repreued pope confermed ſame pope malyces kyng fraunce ye whiche enmye vnto ye chyrche· ye alberte ſame pope yaue kyngdom fraūce dyde kyngdoms proffyted ye laſt ſlayne neuewe ¶clemens pope benedictus almoſte ix yere greate buylder caſtels thynges dampnyd ordre templaryes ordeyned ſeuen booke decretales whiche callyd queſtyons clementyns ¶and anone counſeyle whyche helde atte vyenna reuokyd ſame boke whiche ſucceſſary iohan called ayen corporyd publyſſhyd clement fyrſte pope teanſlatyd pope ſette fro rome auinion whether done bi mocyon god boldenes man dyuers men meruaylle ¶iohn̄ ·xxii pope bym viii yrre man gloryous thoſe thynges vſed thrugh actyf lyf publyſſhed ye conſtytucyons clementynes ſent thē vnyuerſytees many ſayntes canonyſed theſe fatte byſſhopryches deuydyd ordeyned many thynges ayēſte pluralytae benefyces many herytykes dampned whether ſaued lord wolde ſhewe thoſe louyd well ¶henry vii emperour albert v· yere henry noble mā warre coueyted haue pea londe water gloryous man batayll neuer ouercome enmyes atte laſte poyſened frere whan howſelyd hym receyuynge ſacramente ¶of kynge edwarde kynge edwardes ſone kyng edwarde regned edwarde ſone borne att carnriuan thys edwarde wente hym tho fraunce ſpowſyd iſabell kynges doughter fraunce xxv daye ianuari chyrche lady boloyne yere lorde ihū cryſte ccc vii xx day feuerer nexte yere came crownyd ſolemply att weſtmeſtre archebyſſhop caunterbury ſoo grete preſſe people ſyre iohan bakwell ſlayne murdred anone good kynge edwarde deed ſyr edwarde hys ſone kyng englonde ſent pers ganaſton gaſcoyne ſo moche louyd hym yt callyd hym brother anone yaue vnto hym lordſhyp walyngforde longe yt yaue hym therldom cornewaylle ayenſt lordes wyll englonde ¶and tho brought ſyr walter langton byſſhop cheſtre pryſon duraūce toure london wyth two knaues alonely hym ſerue kynge wrothe wyth hym fore cauſe ſyre water made complaynt hym hys fader wherfore put pryſon tyme troylebaſton ſayde pers ganaſton made ſo grete mayſtreys wente kynges treſory ye abbay weſtmeſtre toke table golde ye treſtls ye ſame many ryche iewels yt ſomtyme noble good kyng arthur toke thē marchaūt called ameri friſcōbande ſholde bere ouer ye ſee gaſcoyne ſo went then came neuer ayen wherfore grete loſſe londe whan pers rychely auaūſyd became ſo proude ſo ſtowte wherfore ye grete lordes reame hym īdyſpyte grete berynge wherfore ſyr henry lacy erle nicholl ſyr guy erle warwyk ye whyche grete lordes good kynge edwarde ſyr edwardes fader kyng englonde chargyd pers ganaſton ſholde come englonde brynge ſone edwarde ryot lordes englonde aſſembled certayn day att frere prechers london ſpake dyſhonour ye kynge edwarde dyde hys reame crowne ſo aſſentyd alle bothe erles baron comyns ſayd peer ganaſton ſholde exyled englonde euer ſo done ſwore englonde went irlonde kyng made hym cheyfteyne gouernour londe hys commyſcyon pers cheyfteyne londe dyd hym lykyd▪ hadde power wolde tyme wer templers exyled thrugh criſtiantee cauſe myn put vppon theym ſholde thynges ayenſt fayth good byleue kyng edwarde louyd peer ganaſton ſo moche myght bere cōpany ſo moche kynge yaue behyght people englonde exylyge forſayd peer ſhold reuokyd atte stamforde thrugh yt hym exyled wherfore pers ganaſton cam ayen englond whan come ayen londe dyſpyſed ye gretteſt lordes londe called ſyr robert clare erle gloucetre horeſone erle nycholl ſyr henry lacy bruſtenbely ſyr guy erle warwyk blacke hound arderne alſo callyd ye noble erle thomas lancaſtre churle many ſcornes ſhamys ſayde many grete lordes inglonde wherfore warde hym full angry wroth ryght ſore anoyed ſame tyme deyed erle nycholl chargyed yt deed thomas lancaſtre erle ſone lawe ſholde mayntene hys quarell ayenſt ſame peer ganaſton vpon bleſſynge ¶and ſo befell thorugh helpe erle thomas lancaſtre ſo erle warwyk forſayd ſyr peer heeded att gauerſich beſyde warwyk xx day iune yere grace mccc xii wherfore kyng ſore anoyed prayed god myght ſe daye auenged vpon deth forſayde peer ¶and ſo befell afterwarde ye ſhall ala ye tyme forſayd erle lancaſtre many grete baron put pyteous dethe martred cauſe forſayde quarell kynge att london helde parleament ordeyned lawes symonde mountforde wherfore erle lancaſtre erles alle clergye englonde made othe thrugh counſeyll robert wynchelſe mayntene ordynauntes euer ¶how robert brus came ayē scotlonde gadryd grete power men werre vpon kynge edwarde whan ſyre robert brus made hym kynge scotlonde fledde norway drede deth good kynge edwarde alſo herde debate tho englond bytwene kynhe lordys ordeyned hoſte came inglonde northumberlonde clene dyſtroyed countree ¶and whan kynge edwarde herde tyynges lete aſſemble hys hoſte mette scottes edſtreyelyn daye natiuite ſaynt iohan baptyſt thyrde yere regne yere oure lorde mccc xiiii ala ſorowe loſſe ther done ſlayne noble erle gylbert clare ſyr robert clefford baron kynge edwarde ſcomfyted edmonde maule ye kynges stewarde drede wente drowned hymſelf freſſhe ryuer called bannokyſborne wherfore ſayd repreyf kynge edwarde aſmoche louyd go water alſo dyſcomfyted bānoſborne therfore ye maydens made ſonge therof ye countree kynge edwarde▪ manere ſōge maydēs englonde ſore may ye morne tyȝt haue loſt lēmans bānokyſborne heuelogh wenyth kyng englonde haue gote scotlond rombylogh kynge edmonde dyſcomfyted wōder ſore faſte fledde folke left aliue wēt vnto berwyk helde hym toke hoſtages ii chyldern rycheſſe towne kynge went london toke coūſeyl thynges nedefull ye reame englōde ¶and ye ſame tyme befel tho englonde rybaude called iohan tāner yede ſayd ye good kynge edwardes ſone lete hem calle edwarde carnariuā therfore take oxforde chalēged frere carmes chyrche kyng edwarde hadde yeue whiche kynges halle afterwarde thys iohan ladde northampton drawen hangyd falſneſſe yt deed confeſſyd ſayd tho deuyll beyhyght hym ſholde kynge englonde ſerued deuyll thre yere ¶how towne berwyk take thrugh treaſon two cardynales robbyd englonde mydlente sondaye yere lorde mcccxvi berwyke loſte thorugh falſe treſon oon pers spaldynge whyche pers kynge put helpe ſame towne many burgeyſes ſame towne wherfore chyldren put hoſtage thrughe burgeyſes berwyk folowed kynges march •• ſe many dayes fettred ſtrōge yrens ye tyme two cardynalles englonde pope theym ſence makepe bytwene englonde scotlonde wente warde durham haue ſacred mayſter lowys beamont byſſhop durham take robbed vpon moore wyngleſdom whiche robbery ſyr gylbert mytton atteynt take hangyd drawen lōdon heed ſmytte put vpon ſpere ſet vpon newe gate foure quarter ſent foure cytees englonde ſame tyme befell many myſcheues englonde poore people deyed englonde hungre ſo moche ſo faſte deyed vnethe mē myght bury quarter whete xl ſhelynges▪ two yeres half quarter worth x marck· tyme poore people ſtole chyldern ete ete alſo ye hoūdes myghte take alſo hors cattes fell grete myrreyne amonge beſtes dyuers countrees englōde durynge kynge edwarde lyues tyme ¶how ye scottes robbyd notūberlonde ſame tyme came scottes ayen englonde dyſtroyed northumberlonde brē • londe robbyd ſlewe mē wymmen chyldren laye cradyls brent alſo holy chyrche deſtroyed cryſtendome toke bare englyſſhe mennys godes ben ſaraſyns paynems wyckydneſſe dyde worlde ſpake ¶how scottes wolde mende theyr treſpaſſe therfore scotlonde enterdyted pope iohan xxii ſaynt petir herde grete ſorowe • che • scottes wrought wonder ſorye cryſtendome ſo dyſtroyed thrughe scottes namely deſtroyed ſo • holy chyrches wherfore pope ſente generall ſentence vnder bulles l • ed vnto archebyſſhop caunterbury tharchebyſſhoppe yorke yf robert ye brus scotlonde wolde iuſtyfyed make amendes vnto kynge englonde edwarde theyr lorde make amendes hys loſſe harmes doon englonde alſo reſtore goodes taked holy chyrche ſentence ſhold pronouncyd thorughe alle englonde whan scottes herde wolde leue theyr malyce pope commaundemente wherfore roberte brus iamys douglas thomas radulf erle moref tho theym comyned helpe worde dede accurſyd euery chirche thrugh englonde euery day maſſe iii tymes maſſe ſhold ſonge holy chyrche thrugh soctlonde yf scottes wolde make reſtitucyon harmes hadde made vnto holy chyrche wherfore many good preſt holy men therfore ſlayne thrugh ye reame scotlonde bycauſe wolde ſynge maſſe ayenſt ye popys cōmaundemet ayenſt wyll fulfyll tyrauntes wyll ¶how ſyre hughe spenſers ſone made kynges chamberlayne bataylle mitone longe warde kynge ordeyned parlemente atte yorke ſyr spenſers ſone made chambrelayne meane tyme whyle werre laſted kynge wente ayen scotlonde wonder wytte beſeged towne berwyk ſcottes wente ouer water sole wath thre myle frome kynges hoſte pryuely ſtole way nyght came englō de robbyd dyſtroyed myght ſparde manere thynge tyll came vnto yorke whan englyſſhmen left home herde thyſe tydīges tho myghte traueyll well monkꝭ preſtes freres chanons ſeculers came mette wyth scotes myton vp ſwale xii day octobre ala ſorowe englyſſhe huſbonde men coude thynge yt werre kyllyd drowned arme ſee cheyftyenes ſyre wyllyam melton arche byſſhop yorke abbot ſelby wyth ſtedes fledde came yorke theyr owne foly myſchaunce paſſed water swale scottes ſette fyre ſta • kes hey ſmote ther ſo huge ye englyſſhmen myght ſe ye scottes whā engliſſhmen gone ouer water tho came ye scottes wyth theyr wynge maner ſhelde came warde englyſſmē araye englyſſhemen fledde • neth hadde ony men army kynge hadde almooſt loſt ſyege berwyk scottes hobylers went bytwene brydge englyſſhmen whan grete hoſt mett englyſſhemen fled bytwene hobylers gret hoſte englyſſhmen almooſt ſlayne myght go ouer water ſaued many drowned ala ſlayne many men relygyon ſeculers preeſtes clerkes moche ſorowe tharchebyſſhop eſcaped therfore scottes callyd batayll whyte batayll ¶how kynge edwarde dyde alle manere thynge ſyr hugh spenſer wolde· kynge edwarde herde tydynges remeued ſege berwyk came agayn englond syr hugh spenſer kynges chamberlayne kept ſo kynges chambre mā myghte ſpeke kynge made hym fret alle nede ouer meſure hugh bare hym ſo ſtowte men hym ſcorne dyſpyte kynge hymſelf wolde gouerned ne rulyd manere man fader hym yf ony knyghte englonde hadde wodes maneyrs londes wolde coueyte anone kyng muſt yeue elles man ought ſholde falſly endyted forfeyt felony thrugh ſuche doynge dyſheryted many bachelere ſo moche londe gate grete wonder whan lordes enlonde ſawe grete couetyſe falſneſſe ſyr hugh spenſer fader ſyr hugh ſone come gentyll erle lancaſtre axyd hym counſeyll dyſeſe reame though ſyr hugh spenſer ſone haſt one aſſente made pryue aſſēble ſhirburne • elmede made othe breke dyſtouble ye doinge bytwene kynge ſyr hugh spenſer ſone vpon theyr power went marche walys dyſtroyed londe forſayd ſyr hughes ¶how ſyr hugh spenſer fader exyled englonde· whan kyng edwarde ſawe ye grete harme dyſtruccyō tho barōs englonde dyde vnto ſyre hugh spenſers londe ſone euery place came vpon kynge tho thrugh hys counſeyl yll exyled ſyr monbraye ſyr roger clyfforde ſyr goſſelyn dauyll many lordes yt theym conſente wherfore baron dyde tho harme dyde whā kynge ſawe ye baron wolde ſeſſe theyr cruelte kyng ſore adradde leſt wolde dyſtroy hym reame mayntenaūce yf aſſented ſo ſente thē hys letter ſholde come london hys parlement certaine daye letter conteyned came thre bataylles well armyd al poyntes euery batayl cotarmours grete clothe therof ryght quarter yelowe wyth whyte bendes wherfore ye parlemente callyd parlement whyte bende ye company ſyr hunfrey de bohoune erle herford ſyre roger clyfforde ſyr iohan monbray ſyr gloſſelyn dauyll ſyr roger mortymer vncle ſyr roger mortymer wygmore ſyr henry tray ſyr iohn̄ gyffarde ſyre barthylmewe badeleſſemore ye kynges ſtewarde yt kynge ſente shyrborne elmede ye erle lācaſtre yt hym trete accorde ye hym alyed baron came company ſur roger dammory ſyr hugh dandale yt ſpouſyd kynges neces ſyſter ſyr gylbert clare erle gloucetre yt ſlayne scotlonde ſayd tho two lordes tho two partyes erldom gloucerte ſur hugh spenſer thyrde party wyues half thyrde ſyſter tho two lordes wente baron wyth theyr power ayenſt ſyr hugh theyr brother lawe ſo came wyth ſyr robert clyfforde ſyr iohan mōbray ſyr goſelyn dauyll ſyr roger mortymer werk ſyr roger mortymer wykmore neuewe ſyr henry tray ſyre iohā gyffarde ſyr barthylmewe bardeſmore theyr cōpany many conſent grete lordes came vnto weſtmeſtre ye kynges parlemente ſo ſpake dyde bothe ſyr hughe spēſer fader alſo ſone lauwed englonde euermore ſoo ſyre hugh fader wente vnto douer made moche ſorowe fell downe vpon grounde ſee banke croſſe wyth armes ſore wepynge ſayd fayr englonde good englonde almyghty god betake thryes kyſſed grounde wenyd neuer haue come ayen· wepynge curſyd ye tyme euer begate ſyr hugh ſone ſayd hym loſt englond tho preſence thē aboute hym yaue hym curſee went ouer ſee londes hugh ſone wolde go englonde helde hym ſee company robbyd ii dromedores beſyde sandwyth toke bare waye alle godoes value lxmli ¶how kynge exyled erle thomas lancaſtre alle helde hym mortymer came yelded hym kynge lordes longe kynge made ſyr hugh spenſer fader ſyr hugh ſone come ayen englond ayenſte lordes wyll reame ſoone kynge ſtrōge power came beſeged caſtel ledys caſtel ye laby bladeleſmore cauſe ſhe wold graunt caſtell quene iſabel kinge edwardes wyfe pryncypall cauſe ſyr berthylmewe ayenſt ye kynge helde lordes englōde neuertheles kynge helpe ſocoure men london alſo helpe southeren men gate caſtel maugre yt toke al myght fynde whan baron englonde herde theſe tidynges ſyr roger mortymer many lordes toke towne brugge wroth wyth ſtrenth wherfore kyng wonder wrothe lete outlawe thomas lancaſtre vmfroy de bohoune erle herforde alle tho aſſentynge ſame quarel kyng aſſēbled huge hoſt came ayenſt lordes englond wherfore mortymers put kynges grace anone ſente toure london kept pryſon whā baron herd thys thyng came poutfert ye erle thomas ſoiourned tolde hym mortymers yelde kynge put hys grace ¶of ſyege tykhyll whan thomas erle lancaſtre herde thys wonder wrothe company greatly dyſcomfyted ordeyned power togyder beſyeged caſtell tykhyll tho wyth manly defended barnos myght gete caſtel whan kyng herde yt caſtell beſeged ſwore god name lege ſholde remeued aſſembled huge power people wente theder ward reſcowe caſtell power encreſyd fro daye daye whan erle lancaſtre erle herforde baron cōpany herde thys thynge aſſembled theyr power wente burton vpon trent kept brydge kyng ſhold paſſe ouer▪ befell ſo tenthe daye marche yere grace mcccxxi kyng spenſers ſyr aymer valaunce erle penbroke iohan erle araundell theyr power wente ouer water dyſcomfyted therle thomas company· fled caſtell tetbury then went pountfret • yage deyed ſyr roger daumore thabbay thebury ſame tyme erle thomas traytour wyth hyme yt callyd robert holonde knyght erle brought vp nought nouryſſhed hym ī hys butrye yeue hym thouſāde marke londe yere ſo moche erle louyd hym myght erles court hym lyked bothe amonge hyghe lowe ſo craftly theyf bare hym ayenſte lorde truſtyd vpon hym ony man lyue erle ordeyned letter goo erledome lancaſtre make men aryſe kepe hym vyage ſaye v hū dred men army fals traytour came manere men warne ne make arayſe helpe lord whan fals traytour herde tell yt hys lord dycomfyted burton vpon trent fals traytour theyf ſtele way robbyd rauēſdele lordes men came fro ſcomfyture toke hors harneys al ſlewe myghte take came yeldyd hym kynge ¶whan good erle thomas wyſte ſo bytrayed ſo abaſſhed ſayde hymſelf almyghty good myght robert holonde fynde hys herteme betray ſythe louyd hym ſo moche god well maye nowe man ſe hym yt man maye dyſceyue nother rathar yt truſtyth mooſt vpon hath full euyll yelded goodnes worſhyp yt haue hym done thrugh kyndneſſe haue hym auaūcyd made hym hyghe yt lowe makyth go hyghe vnto lowe yet ſhall deye euyll dethe ¶of ſcomfyture brurbrygge good erle thomas lancaſte humfroy de bohoune ele herford baron yt theym toke counſell bytwene ye frre prechers poūtfret tho thought thomas vpon traytour roberte holonde ſayde repreyf ala robert holonde hath betrayed red ſome euyll ſhred comyn aſſent ſholde goo caſtell dunſtanbrughe whiche perteyned therldome lancaſtre yt ſholde abyde ther tyll kynge yeue male talente ¶but whan good erle thomas herde anſwered manere ſayd lordes ſayd yf go wade north northen men woll ſaye go warde ye ſcottes ſo ſhall holden traytours cauſe dyſtaūce bytwene kynge edwarde robert ye brus made hym kynge scotlonde therfore ſay touchyng ſelf wyll go ferder northe myn owne caſtell poūtfret ¶and whan ſyre roger clyfford herde aroſe vp anone wrathe drawe ſwerde hye ſwore god almyghty holy name yf yt wolde go ſholde hym ſlee noble gentyll erle thomas lancaſtre ſore ferde ſayd fayr▪ ſyres wyll go whether ſome euer ye bydde tho went togyder north wyth hadde viic men army came burbryg whan ſyr andrew herkela north countre thrugh ordynaūce kynge kepe ye countree scotlonde herde tell yt thomas lancaſtre ſcomfyted hys company burton vpon trent ordened hym ſtronge power ſyr ſymonde warde alſo ſhyref yorke mette baron burburgge anone brake brydge made tree ¶and whan ſyr thomas lancaſtre herde ye ſyr andrewe herkela broughte wyth hym ſuche power ſore adradde ſente ſyr andrewe herkela wyth hym ſpake ſayde hym thys manere ſyr andrewe ſayde ye may wel vnderſtōde lorde ye kyng ladde myſgouerned moche fals counſel thrugh ſyr hugh spenſer fader ſyr hughe ſone ſyr iohan erle arūdel thrugh mayſter robert baldok fals pylled clerke yt kynges courte dwellynge wherfore praye ye wyll come wyth v alle youre power ye haue ordeyned helpe dyſtroie venym englond ye traytours ben therin wyll yeue vnto beſt parte fyue erldoms haue holde wyll make vnto othe wyll neuer doo thynge wythout counſell ſoo ye ſhalbe left well euer robert holande tho anſwered ſyr andrew herkela ſayd ſyr thomas yt wolde ne conſent therto manere thynge wythout wyll cōmaundement lorde kynge ſhold holden traytour euermore whan ye noble erle thomas lācaſtre ſawe wolde conſent hym maner thyng ſyr andrew ſayd wyll ye conſent dyſtroy venym reame conſente one worde ſyr andrewe tel yere begoō ye ſhall▪ take holde traytour ony hold v worſe dethe ye ſhall deye euer dyde ony knyght englonde vnderſtonde wel ye dyd neuer thynge ſorer ye ſhall repente go doo good lykyth wyll put mercy god ſo went fals traytour tyraū ce fals forſworne man thrugh noble erle thomas lancaſtre receyued army chyualrye thrughe hym made knyght tho myghte men ſe archer drawe one ſyde knyghtes alſo foughte tho togyder wonder ſore alſo amonge humfroy de boughon erle herforde worthy knyght renoune thrugh cryſtendom ſtode fought enmyes vppon ye brydge noble lord ſtode foughte vpon brydge theyf rybaude ſculkyd vnder brydge fyerſly ſpere ſmote noble knyght ye fūdement ſo yt bowellys came aboute fete ther ala ſorowe pyte ſlayne floure ſolace comforth alſo curteyſye ¶and syr roger clyfforde noble worthy knyghte ſtode euer fought well worthyly hym defended noble baron laſt ſore woundyd heed ſyr wyllyam sullaynde ſyr roger benfeelde ſlayne batayll whan ſyr andrewe herkela ſawe ſyr thomas mē lā caſtre laſſed ſlakyd anone hys company came vnto gentyll knyght ſyr thomas layd vnto hym hyghe voyce yelde traytour yelde gentyll erle thomas lancaſtre anſwered thenne ſayde nay lordes traitours ben none wyll neuer v yelde whyle oure lyues laſt leuer ſlayne thruth yelde v vnto ſyre andrewe • en gardyd vppon ſyr thomas hys company yellynge cryenge lyke wode wulf yelde traytours taken yelde ſayde wyth hyghe voys beware ſyres yt none ſo hardy vpon lyf lymme myſ thomas body lācaſtre wyth worde good erle thomas yede caſtell ſayd knelynge vpon hys knee torned hys vyſage warde croſſe ſayd almyghty god yelde holy put vnto thy mercy wyth vylaynes rybaudes lept aboute hym euery ſyde tyraūtes wood tormentours dyſpoyled hym armoure clothed hym • obe ray • ſquyres lyuetay • forth ladde hym unto yorke water tho myght men ſee moche ſorowe care gentyl knyghtes ſledde euery ſyde ye rybaudes vyllayns egerly dyſcryed cryed hyghe yelde traytours yelde whan yelden robbyd bounden theuys ala ſhame dyſpyte gentyll orde knyghthode batayll londe tho without lawe holy chyrche tho nomore creuereence burdell hous batyall fader ayenſt ſone • vncle ayenſt neuewe ſo moche vnkyndeneſſe neuer ſeen englonde tyme amonge folkes one nacyon one kynred noo pyte hungry wulf hathe ſhepe wonder grete lordes englonde alle one nacyon medlyd nacōns ſay ſome brytons ſome saxon ſome danys ſome pehypes ſome frenſſemen ſome norman ſome spanyerdes ſome romayns ſome henaude ſome flemynges dyuers nacyons whyche nacyons accordyd kynde blood englonde yf ſoo grete lordes oonly weddyd englyſſhe people thenne ſholde pea haue ben reſte amonge theym without ony enuye batayll roger clyfforde take ſyr iohn̄ mombray ſyr wyllyam tuchy • syr wyllyam fitz wyllyam many worthy knyghtes take batayll syr hugh dandell nette daye taken put pryſon ſholde haue doon dethe yf hadde ſpouſyd kynges nece erle gylbertes ſyſter glouceſtre • anon ſyr berthylmewe badeleſmore taken stow parke maneyr byſſhop lyncoln neuewe many baron baronetters wherfore made moche ſorowe ¶how thomas lancaſtre heedyd pountfret v baron hangyd drawen ſhall tell noble erle thomas lancaſtre wha take brought yorke many cyte full glade vpon hym cryed hyght voys ſyr traytour ye welcome bleſſyd god ye ſhall haue rewarde longe ye haue deſerued caſte vppon hym many ſnowe balles many repreues dyd hym gentyll erle ſuffred ſayd nother worde ¶and ſame tyme ye kyng herde thys ſcōfyture ful glad ioyous grete haſt came poūtfret ſyr hugh spenſer ſyr hugh ſone ſyr iohn̄ erle arundell ſyr edmonde wodeſtoke ye kynges brother erle kent ſyr aymer valaunce erle penbroke mayſter robert baldoke fals pyllyd clerke pryue dwelled kynges court came theder wyth kynge kyng entryd caſtel syr andrewe herkela fals tyraunte thrugh kynges cōmaundement toke wyth hym gentyll erle thomas pountfret pryſoned owne caſtell newe made ſtode ayenſte abbaye kynge edwarde ¶and ſyr hugh spenſer fader ſone caſt thought maner good erle thomas lancaſtre ſholde deed wythoute iugement hys perys wherfore ordeyned thrugh kynges iuſticus kyng ſholde put vpon hym poyntes treaſon ſo befell ledde barre kynges iuſtices bare heed theyf fayre halle owne caſtell yt made ther many fayre feſte ryche poore ¶and theſe iuſtices ſyr hugh spē ſer fader aymer balaunce erle pē broke ſyr edmonde wodſtok erle kent ſyr iohan brytayne erle rychemonde ſyr robert malemethrop iuſtyce ſyre roberte hym couplyd manere ¶thomas court excludeth maner anſwer thomas lorde kynge puttyth vppon you▪ ye haue hys londe ryden wyth baner dyſplayed ayenſt pea traytour ¶and ye worde gentyll erle thomas hygh voyce ſayd nay lordes forſoth ſaynt thomas neuer traytoure ¶the iuſtyce ſayd ayen tho thomas oure lorde kyng putteth vpon ye haue robbyd folke murdred people theyf thomas alſo kynge puttythe vpon dyſcōfyted people wyth folke owne reame wherfore ye wē te fledde woode outlaw▪ thomas traytoure ye ſhall hangyd reaſō ye kynge hathe foryeuen iugement loue quene iſabell thomas reſon wolde yt ye ſholde hangyd ye kynge hath foryue iugemēt cauſe loue lygnage aſmoche thomas ye taken fleenge outlawe kynge woll heed ſhalle ſmyten anone haue hym oute prees brynge hym iugement ¶whan gē tyll knyght thomas herde theſe wordes wyth hygh voyce cryed ſore wepynge ſayd ala ſaynt thomas fayr fader ala ſhall deed thus graunt bleſſydful▪ god anſwere auayled hym thynge curſyd gaſcoyns put hym hyther thyder hym cryed wyth hyghe voys kynge arthur mooſt terryble dredefull well knowen ſhewed thyn open traytour euyll deth ſhalt thou ryght anone deye haſte thou ryght well deſerued ¶and thenne thyſe cruell folke ſette vpon gode knyhht thomas ſcorne olde chaplet alle rente yt worth halfe peny ſette hym vpon whyte palfroy full vnſemely alſo bare wyth olde brydell wyth horryble noyſe draue hym caſtell warde hys deth caſt vpon hym many balles ſnowe dyſpyte traytours lad hym caſtell tho ſayde theſe pyteous wordes hondes helde vp hygh warde heuen kyng heuen yeue u mercy erthly kyng hathe v forſaken frere precher wente hym caſtell tyll came place endeth lyfe vnto whome ſhroue hym hys lyfe gentyll erle helde frere wonder faſt clothes ſayd hym fayr fader abyde v tyll yt deed fleſſhe quakyth drede dethe ¶and ſothe ſay gentyll erle ſette hym vpon hys knee torned hym warde eeſt rybaude called hygone moſ •• ſette honde vpon gentyll erle ſayd dyſpyte hym syr traytour torne towarde scottes thy fowle deth receyue torned warde noſth noble erle thomas anſwered tho wyth mylde voys ſayd fayr lordes ſhall wyll worde ye frere went hym ſore wepynge anone rybaude wente hym ſmote hys heed xi kalendas auerell yere grace mccc xxi ¶alas euer ſuche gentyll blood ſholde deth withouten cauſe reaſon traytourſly kynge counſeylled whan thrugh fals counſeyll spenſer ſuffred ſyr thomas vncles ſone put ſuche deth ſo beheeded ayenſt maner reaſō grete pyte alſo ſuche noble kynge ſholde dyſceyued myſgouerned thrugh counſell fals spenſers whyche tho mayntened thrughe loſelry ayenſt honour alſo proffyte warde fell grete vengaunce englonde cauſe forſayd· thomas dethe whan gentyll erle lyf paſſyd ye pryour monkys pounfret gate body ſyr thomas kynge buryed hyghe awter ryght ſyde ¶that ſame daye thys gentyll knyght dede hangyd drawen ſame quarel poūtfret ſyr wyllyam tuchet syr wyllyam fitz wyllyam ſyr werreyn iſell syr henry bradborn ſyr wyllyam cheyne baron al iohn̄ page eſquyrer ſoone yorke drawen hangyd ſyr roger clyfforde ſyre iohan mambray baron ſyr goſelyne deuyll knyght ¶and bryſtowe drawē hangyd syr henry wemyngton ſyr henry moun • torde barōs ¶and gloucerre drawē hangyd ſyr iohn̄ gaffarde ſyr wyllyam elmebrughe baron londō hangyd drawen syr henry tyes baron ¶and atte wynchelſe ſyr thomas clepepyr knyght ferthermore telle thys cruell occyon atte wyndſore drawe hangyd ſyr fraunc • waldēham baron caunterbury drawē handyg ſyr berthylmew badeleſmore ſyr berthylmew aſſhe bourucham baron cardyf walys ſyr wylyam flemmynge baron ¶how kynge edwarde wente scotlonde wyth hundrde thouſande mē army myght ſpede whan kynge edwarde englonde brought floure cheua • ▪ vnto theyr deth thrugh counſell con • ente ſyr hugh spenſer fader ſyr hughe ſone became woode ony lyon▪ ſo euer spenſers wolde haue done well kynge louyd theym yt myght hym thynge lyked wherfore kynge gaaf vnto ſyr hughe spenſer fader ye erldom wyncheſtre vnto ſyr andrewe herkela erldome cardoyll • preiudyce harmynge hys crowne kyng edwarde tho thrugh counſel spenſers dyſheryted alle ayenſt hym ony quarel thomas l • caſtre many dyſheryted alſo cauſe spenſers coueyted haue theyr londes ſo wold deſyre wyth wronge ayenſt reaſon tho made kynge robert baldok fal • e pylled clerke chaunceler englond thrugh counſell forſayde spenſers ¶and falſe rybaude coueytouſe ſo counſeylled kynge moche kyng lete take hys owne warde gooddes lordes put wrongfully deth hys owne honde aſwell toke goodes yt within hooly chyrche e goodes yt wythout lete theym put hys treſoury london lette calle hys feytes coūſell ye kynge wrought euer dyſheryted godes ought thrugh ther coūſell lete arer talegge goodes englonde wherfore rycheſt kyng yt euer englonde wyllyam baſtarde yt comquered englonde yet thrughe coūſell hym ſemyd yt hadde ynough made yet euery towne englonde fynde man army vpon theyr owne coſtes go werre vpon scottes yt enmyes wherfore kynge went scotlonde houndred thouſande men army wytſontyde yere lord iheſu criſt mcccxxii scottes wente hyd moūteyns wodes caryed englyſſhmen fro day day kynge myght manere thynge fynde thē playne felde wherfor many englyſſhmen lytyl vytaylles deyed ther hungre wonder faſt ſodenly goynge comynge namely tho bene ayenſt thomas lancaſtre robbyd men vpon hys londes whan kynge edwarde ſawe vytaylles fayled hym wonder ſore dyſcomfyted bycauſe alſo yt hys men deyed myght ſpede enmyes att laſt came ayen englonde anone came iames douglas alſo thomas radulph huge hooſte englonde northumberlonde wyth englyſſhmen dryuen englonde came robbed countree ſlewe ye people alſo brente twone yt callyd northallerton many twones yorke whan kynge herde thys tydynges lete ſo mane maner men myght trauyllee ſo englyſſhmen mette scottes ye abbay beyghelande xv day mygelmas en ſame yere aboue ſayd englyſſhmen dyſconfyted dyſcomfyture take ſyr iohan brytayne erle rychmonde helde countree erldome lancaſtre payed huge raunſonne lete goo wente fraunce came neuer agayne ¶how ſyr andrewe herkelay take put deth erle cardoil tyme ſyr andrew herkela ye new made erle cardoil cauſe taken good erle thomas lancaſtre ¶he hadde ordeyned thrugh kynges cōmaundement englonde bringe hym power yt myght helpe ayenſte scottes aſ abbaye beglonde whan ye fals traytour gadred people myght ſhold haue come kynge vnto abbaye beyghelande ye fals traytour ladde nother coūtre thrughe copelonde thrughe therldome lancaſtre went thrugh ye coū tree robbed ſlewe folke yt myght ferthermore fals traytour take grete ſomme golde ſyluer ſyr iames douglas ayenſt kyng englonde helpynge holdynge scottes thrugh whoſe treaſon kynge englonde ſcomfyted beyghelande yt came thyder wherfore kyng ward hym wonder wrothe lete pryuely enquere coūtre aboute yt ſome men enquered aſpeyed ſo laſte trough foūde ſought atteynte take fals traytour ye gode erle thomas lancaſtre hym tolde yt pute vnto deth hys ta • ynge att burbrugge hym ſayd ye doon ſholde take holde traytour ſo holy mā ſayd ¶wherfore kyng ſent pryuely ſyr anthony lucy knyght countre cardoil ſholde take ſyr andrew herkela put hym vnto dethe brynge thynge vnto ende kynge ſente hys commyſſion ſo thys ſame andrewe take cardoill ladde vnto barre maner erle worthyly arayed wyth aſwerde gyrde aboute hym hoſyd ſporyd ¶tho ſpake ſyr anthoyn maner ſyr andrewe ſayd kynge puttyth vpon aſmoche thou haſt orpyd ī thy dedys dyde moche honour made erle cardoil traytour thy lorde laddeſt people hys countere ſhold haue holpe hym batayll beyghel thou laddeſt awaye countree copelande thrugh erldom lancaſtre wherfore lorde kynge dyſcomfyted scottes thrugh thy treaſon falſneſſe yf thou haddeſt come tymes bataylle treaſon thou dydeſt ye grete ſomme golde ſyluer thou receyued iames douglas scot kynges enmye lorde kynge wyl yt ordre knyghthode whiche thou receyued al thyne honour worſhyppe vppon thy body brought nought thyn eſtate vndoyne knyghtes lower degree mowe beware whyche lorde hathe auaunted hugely dyuerſe countrees englonde al may take enſample lorde warde truly ſerue ¶tho commaunded anone knaue hew hys ſpores helys lete breke ſerde ouer hys heed whiche kynge yaue hym kepe defende hys londe ther wyth whan made hym erle cardoyll lette hym vnclothed hys furred taberde hys hode furryd cote gyrdell ¶and whanne done syr anthony ſayde thenne vnto hym andrewe ſayde nowe arte thou noo knyghte knaue thy treaſon kynge wylle thou ſhalte hangyd drawen thy heed ſmyten thy bowel take oute thy body brente thy body quartryd thy heed ſente ſonne torned blood peple ſaw dured morne tyll xi cloke ¶of myracles yt god wrought ſaȳt thomas lancaſtre wherfore kynge lete cloſe ye chyrche dores ye pryory poūtfert mā ſholde come therin offre ſone good erle thomas lancaſtre martryd preeſt lōge tyme blynde dremed ſlepe ſholde go ye hylle good erle thomas lancaſtre doon vnto deth ſholde haue ſyghte ayen ſo dremed thre nyghtes ſewynge preeſt lede hym ſame hyll whā came ye place yt martryd deuowtly made prayer prayed god ſaynt thomas myghte haue hys ſyght ayen hys prayer layed hys ryght hōde vpon ſame gode man martryd drope drye blood ſmale ſonde cleuyd hys honde ſtryketh eyen anone thrugh myght god ſaynt thomas lancaſtre ſyght ayen thankyd tho almyghty god ſaynt thomas whan myracle knowen amonge men people came thither euery ſyde knelyd made theyr prayer tombe pryory pountfret prayed holy martyr ſocour helpe god herde prayer ¶alſo yonge chylde drowned welle towne pountfret deed thre daye thre nyghtes men came layed ye deed chylde ſayd thomas tombe holy martyr chylde aroſe dethe lyfe many man ſawe ¶and alſo moche peple ther mynde god ſent theyr mynde ayen thorough vertue holy man god hathe yeue alſo cryppyls theyr goynge crokyd theyr hōdes foot two blynd alſo theyr ſyght many ſyke folke • elthe dyuers maladyes loue gode martyr ¶alſo ryche man coūdom gaſcoyne ſuche malady al ryght ſyde rotyd fel way frō hym men myght ſee lyuer hys herte ſo ſtanke vnneth myght come nyghe hym wherfore hys frendes hym wonder ſory laſt god wolde prayed ſaynt thomas lancaſtre wolde pray almyghty god pryſoner behyght go pountfret doo theyr pylgrymage thought martyr ſaynt thomas came hym anoynted alle ſike body therwith good man woke hole fleſſhe reſtored ayē ro • yd fallē way whiche myracle good man frē de louyd god ſaynt thomas euermore good man came englonde toke foure felowes came poūtfret ye holy martyr dyd theyr pylgrymage good man ſyke came thyther nakyd ſaufe preuye clothes whan done torned home ayen theyr owne coūtre tolde myracle wher ſoo euer came ¶and alſo two men haue ben heelyd mormale thrugh helpe ye holy martyr thoughe euyll holde curable whan ye spenſers herde yt god dyde ſuche myracles thys holy man nolde byleue yt noo manere wyſe • ſayde openly grete hereſye ſuche vertue hym byleue whan ſyr hugh spenſer ſone ſawe doynge anone ſente maſſager pountfret dwelled kyng edwarde yt tho grauen ſcypton cauſe yt kynge ſholde vndo ye pylgrymage rybaude ye meſſager went warde kynge meſſage came hylle • e good martyr doon dethe ſame place made ordure whan hadde done rode warde kynge ſtronge flyre came vpon hym came yorke tho ſhed alle hys bowelles fūdment whā ſyr hugh spenſer herde tygynges ſomdele adradde thoughte vndo thys pylgrymage yf myghte ony manere waye anone wente kynge ſayde martyr enteryd thus dyd ayenſt fraūchyſes holy chirche ſo ye foure yere myght pylgryme come holy bodye bycauſe monkes ſuffred men come honour holy body ſaynt thomas ye martyr thrugh coūſell ſyr hym fraunce wherfore kynge ſore anoyed put ſame stephen conſtabellary ¶how quene iſabell went fraunce treate pea bytwene lorde ye kynge englonde kynge fraū ce broder kyng went tho vnto london thrugh coūſell ſyr hugh spenſer fader ſone mayſter robert baldok fals pylled clerke chaūcheler let ſeaſe quenes londes hys hondes alſo ye londes ſyre edwardes ſone ſo put theyr wagys ayēſt maner reaſon thrugh falsneſſe spenſers ¶and whan kyng fraunce yt quene iſabelles brother herde falſneſſe ſore anoyed ayenſt kynge englonde fals counſellers wherfore ſent letter kyng edward vnder ſeale· yt ſhold come certayne day hys homage therto ſomoned hym el ſholde leſe gaſcoyne ſo ordeyned englonde thrugh kyng hys coūſel quene iſabel ſholde go fraunce treate pea bytwene lorde broder olyuer yngham ſhold go gaſcoyne haue hym viim men army moo seneſchall wardeyne gaſcoyne ſo ordeyned quene iſabell came fraunce wente ſyr aymer valaunce erle penbroke murdred ſodenly apreuyſege thrugh goddes vengaūce one iuſtycys cōſented ſaynt thomas deth lancaſtre wolde neuer repent hym wyckyd dede tyme ſyr olyuer yngham wente ouer gaſcoyne dyde moche harme ye kynge fraunce tho gate ayen kynge edwarde loſte moche therto ¶how kynge edwarde ſente ſyr edwarde hys ſone eldeſt fraunce quene iſabell quater yere dwelled fraunce whan ſyr edwarde eldeſt ſone axed leue tho go fraūce ſpeke moder iſabel quene fader kynge grauntyd good wyll ſayd hym go fayr ſone goddys blyſſynge myn thynke come ayen haſtely thou may wēte ouer ſee fraunce kynge fraunce hys vncle receyued hym moche honour ſayd vnto hym fayr ſon ye welcome cauſe father come homage ye duchye guyon auncetours wont yeue lordſhyp holde herytage manerauncetours dyd wherfore callyd duke guyon ¶how kynge exyled quene yſabell edwarde eldeſt ſone kynge vnderſtonde aſmoche edwarde kynge englonde ſome tyme ordeyned aſſent playne parlement vnder warde gouernaunce henry erle lancaſtre coſyn ſaluacyon hys dody take caſtell kenilworth warde thrugh colour quene iſabell mortymer without conſent ony parlement tooke ladde hym neuer none kynred myght wyth hym ſpeke ne ſee tratorurſly toke morored hym whoſe deth aroſe ſklaūdre thrugh cryſtendom whan done alſo treſore ye ſyre edwarde kernaruian left many place englonde walys waſtyd borne awaye wythout wyll kynge edwarde ſone dyſtruccyō hym al folke ¶alſo thrughe whoſe counſeyll ye kynge yaue vp kyngdom scotlond whiche reame kynges aūcetours full ſore traueiled ſo dyd many noble mā theyr ryght delyuered vnto dauyd robert brus ſone ye ryght yt ryght reame world wyſt alſo chartres remēbraunces yt ryght scotlond take treſory taken scottes kynges enmyes dyſheritynge hym ſucceſſours grete harme hys lyeges grete repreef englyſſhemen euer ¶alſo wherfore dame iohan toure kynges ſyſter edward dyſperagyd maryed vnto dauyd robertbrus ſone traytour enmye vnto englonde thrugh whoos counſeyl ſhe take enmyes hondes englonde ¶and meane whyle ye good erle henry lā caſtre hys companie toke counſeyl thoſe poyntes aboue ſayd myght amended worſhyp kynge hys profyte profyte leygꝭ quene iſabel thrughe coniectynge alſo mortymers lete ordeyne parlement salyſburye ye ſame parlement mortymer made erle marche ayenſt baron wyll englonde preiudyce ye kyng hys crowne ſyr iohan eltham kynges brother gyrde ſwerde corne waylle tho callyd erle corne waylle euer quene iſabell procuryd ſo moche ayenſt ſone ye kyng ſhe warde ye forſayde ſyr edward lōdes parlemente erle lancaſtre wolde come ordeyned power ayenſt quene iſabel mortymer men london ordeyned fyue hūdred men army ¶whan quene iſabel wiſt doynge 〈◊〉 ſwore god hys name full angerly euell tyme thought vppon tho poyntes tho ſente quene iſabell mortymer theyr retenwe kyngys retenewe ſoo ordeyned amonge huge hoſte counſeylled kynge ſo vppon nyght • rode xxiii myles bedford erle lancaſtre company thought haue hym dyſtroyed nyght ſhe rode beſyde kynge ſone knyght drede dethe done kyng vnderſtond erle henry lancaſtre hys company wolde haue dyſtroyed kyng hys counſeylle euer wherfore kynge ſomdele wardes hym heuy anoye • ¶whan erle marſhall therle kente kynges brother herde thys tydynges rode ſoo meſſage bytwene theym kynge grauntyd hym hys pea therle henry lancaſtre certayne raunſomme leuen thouſande pounde neuer payed afterwarde thyſe lordes helde syr henry lancaſtre syr beaumont ſyr fouk fytz waren ſyr thomas rocelyn syr wyllyam truſdr •• • ynghtes moo hym conſented alle thoſe exyled thrughe counſeylle quene iſabell mortymer ye mortymer wayted haue theyr lōdes yf myght thrugh ony maner coniectynge coueytous hadde moche wyll grete pyte ¶how kynge edwarde went ouer ſee doo homage vnto kynge fraū ce duchye guyhenne longe kyng fraunce thrugh counſeyll hys donzepers ſente kynge edwarde englode ſholde come parys homage reaſon wolde duchye guyon ſo thrughe coūſell lordes englonde kynge edwarde went ouer ſee aſcyon tyde came vnto parys thyrde yere regne homage vnto kyng fraūce kyng receyued hys homage made hym moche ioy worſhyp whan kynge edwarde done hys homage haſtyly ſent englonde thrugh quen iſabell moder anone haſtyly came ayen englonde vpon wytſonday without ony takynge leue ye kynge fraū ce wherfore wonder wrothe ¶how ſyr roger mortymer bare hym proudely ſoo hyghe ſhall ye ſyr roger mortymer wygmore deſyred coueted hygh aſtate ſo kyng grauntyd hym callyd erle marche thorughe hys lordſhyp became ſoo proude hauteyn yt wolde leſe forſake name yt elder euer fore ye cauſe let hym calle erle marche none comnyns englonde durſte calle hym name callyd ſo ye kyngys crye men ſhold calle hym erle marche mortymer bare hym ſo hauteyn ſo proude wonder wyte alſo dyſguyſed hym wōnder ryche clothes al manere reaſon ſhapynge werynge wher englyſſhmen grete wonder manere myght contryue fynde ſuche manere pryde ſ • yd amonge comynly yt pryde ſholde longe endure ¶and ſame tyme ſyr gyffray mortymer yonge mortymers ſone lete calle hym kynge foly ſo befell warde dede ſoo full pryde wretchydneſſe helde rounde table walys men der came coūterfeted doynge manere kyng arthur table openly fayled noble kynge arthur ye mooſt noble lord renomme worlde hys tyme yet came neuer none ſuche ye noble knyghtes ī cryſtē dom dedys army aſſayed dwellyd wyth kynge arthur helde hym lorde ſouerayne well ſeen conquered bataylle romayne yt callyd froll gate hym reame fraunce ſlewe hym wyth hys owne hondes alſo faught gyaunt callyd dynabus ſlewe hym rauyſſhed fayre elayne kyng howels ne • e kynge lytyll brytayn ſlewe bataylle emperour rome yt callyd lucye hadde aſſembled ayenſt arthur fyghte wyth hym ſo moche people romayns pebytes ſaraſyns man cowde nombre dyſcomfyted alle ſtory tellyth ¶and ſame thyme comyn voyce ſpronge englond thrugh coniectynge ordynaunce frere prechers ſyr edwarde carnariuan kyng edwardes fader whome geſte tellyth ſayde alyue caſtell corf wherof comyns englonde almooſt ī ſorowe drede whether ſoo wiſt traytourſly mortymer hym done murthred ¶how edmonde wodſtok erle kente kynges brother edwarde carnaryuan heedyd wyncheſtre vppon tyme befell ſoo ſyr edmonde wodſtok erle kent ſpake vnto pope iohan xxii auinion ſayde almyghty god ofte tymes done thomas loue lancaſtre many grete myracles many men wymmen yt thrughe dyuers maladyes vndoone ¶as vnto worlde thrughe prayer broughte vnto helthe ſoo ſyr edmonde prayed pope hertely wolde graunt hym grace forſayde thomas myghte traunſlatyd pope ſayde naye ſholde traunſlatyd vnto tyme better certyfyed clergye englond ſeen theyr obedyence thynge god done loue ſaynt thomas lācaſtre ſuggeſtiō forſayd erle kent hadde vnto hym made whan edmonde ſaw myght ſpede purpos touchynge traunſlacion prayed hȳ coūſell touchynge ſyr edwarde carnariuan hys brother ſayd longe agon kynge englonde thynge myghte beſte done touchynge delyueraūce ſythe yt comune fame thrugh englonde yt alyue hole ſauf whā ye pope herde hȳ tell yt ſyr edwarde alyue cōmaūded ye erle vpō blyſſynge ſholde helpe power myght deliuered pryſon ſaue body manere myght brynge thynge ende aſſoyled hym cōpany pena et culpa delyueraūce tho toke edmond wodſtok leue ye pope came ayen englōde whā ſyr edmonde come ſome ye frere prechers came ſayd ſyr edwarde brother yet alyue ye caſtell corf vnder ye kepynge ſyr thomas gurnay tho ſped hȳ forſayd edmonde faſt myght tyll came ye caſtel corf acquaynted hym ſpake ſo fayre iohn̄ dauerel coneſtable ſame caſtell yaue hym ryche yeftes haue acquayntaunce hym knowe coūſell thus befel forſayd edmonde prayed ſpecyally tel hym pryuely lorde brother ſyr edward yf lyued deed yf alyue prayed hym one haue ſyght hym ſyr iohn̄ daueryl hygh herted mā ful courage anſwerde ſhortly ſyr edmond ſayd ſyr edwarde hys brother helth vnder hys kepynge durſt ſhewe hym vnto man ſyth defended kyngys halfe edwarde yt edwardes ſone carnuariuan alſo cōmaundement quene iſabel ye kynges moder ſyr roger mortymer ſholde ſhewe hys body noo mā world ſauf thē vpō lyf lym̄e diſherytynge heyres euer fals traytour falſly lyed warde take thēs lad caſtell berkeley ſyr thomas gurney cōmaūdemente mortymer tyll dede ſayd ſyr edmonde wodſtok wyſt thynge ſyr edwarde brother deed wherupon toke letter vnto kyng edward brother worthy lorde receyued ye letter hym behyght hym ryght faythful meſſage without fayll ſyr edmonde toke leue forſayd iohn̄ yede owne coūtre lordſhyp kent anone ſame iohan wiſt ſyr edmonde gone kent owne lordſhyp anone went ye haſt myght fro caſtell corf came vnto ſyr roger mortymer toke hym letter ſyr edmond wodſtok erle kent taken hym cloſyd enſealed owne ſeale whan ſyr roger mortymer receyued letter vncloſed ſawe conteyned therin began rede wherof begynnynge ¶worſhyppes reuerence wyth brother alyegaunce ſubieccyon ſyr knyȝt worſhypfull dere brother • yf pleaſe praye hertely ye gode cō forthe ſhall ſoo ordeyn yt ye ſhall come pryſō delyuered dyſeſe ye ben vnderſtondyth grete lordſhyp haue myn aſſentynge mooſt grete lordes englonde wyth theyr apperyll ſay wyth armour treſour wythout nombre mayntene quarell ſo ferforth ye ſhall kynge agayn ye haue ſworne vpon boke aſwell prelate erles baron ¶whan ſyr roger mortymer ſaw vnderſtode myght ſtrenth letter anone hert wrathe began boll euyll herte bare ward ſyr edmōde wodſtok erle kent wyth haſt myght wente vnto dame iſabell quene ye kynges moder ſhewed ſyr edmonds letter wyll purpoſe coniected ordeyned put downe kynge edwarde wyndſore ſone ryalte kyngdome nowe certes ſyr roger ſayd ſhe hathe ſyr edmonde done ſo faders ſoule ſayde ſhe wyll therof auenged yf god graunte lyf ſhorte tyme quene iſabell wente vnto kynge edwarde ſone att parlemente wyncheſtre haue amende wrongys treſpaſſes done amonge people hys reame tho ſhe toke ſhewed hym letter ſyr edmond wodſtok made enſealed hys owne ſeale badde hym vpon bleſſynge ſholde auengyd vpon ſyr edmond vpon dedely enmye tho quene ſore wrothe warde ſyr edmonde erle kente ſeſſyd neuer praye vntyll ſone tyll ſente haſt hym vpon kynge ſent hys letter ſyr edmoode wodſtok ſholde come ſpeke wyth hym att wyncheſtre manere thinge left whan ſyr edmond ſawe kynge ſente hym wyth hys letter enſealed ye haſtyd hym alle yt myghte tylle came wyncheſtre ¶but whan quene wyſt ſyr edmonde come wyncheſtre tho anone ſhe prayed ſo faſte wende vnto kynge edwarde ſone good erle areſted anone ladde vnto barre robert hamonde coroner kynges houſholde aſſocyed vnto hym ſyr roger mortymer tho ſpake ſayd roger ſayde ſyr edmonde erle kent ye ſhall vnderſtō de done v wyte pryncypally vnto lyege lorde kynge edwarde englonde almyghty god hym ſaue kepe ye deedly enmye traytoure alſo comune enmye reame ye haue ben aboute many day make pryue delyueraunce ſyr edwarde ſomtyme kynge englonde broder whiche ſomtyme put downe hys ryaltee ye comyn aſſent lordes englond peaſynge lorde kynges eſtate alſo reame ¶tho anſwerd good man ſayd ſoth ſyr vnderſtonde well neuer traytoure kynge ne reame doo god worlde therfore kynges leue ſhalle preue defende man ought ¶tho ſayde mortymer ſyr edmonde ſo ferfor knowe may well gaynſayd preſence ſhalle well prouyd fals mortymer ſame letter ſyr edmonde hadde take syr iohan daueryll caſtell corf take kynge edwarde hys brother ſyr edmonde wyſt ne ſuppoſed thynge ſyr iohn̄ daueryll ſo fals delyuer letter ſuche wyſe vnto mortymer thought manere thynge letter thenne mortymer ſayd ſyr edmonde ſhewed letter ſealed axed hym yf knewe ye letter ye ſeale ſyr edmonde lokyd theron auyſed hym longe tyme prynte ſeale myght ſee letter wyſt well ſeale thought ſomme letter bore grete charge thought thinge letter ſayd openly herynge ye ſoth thys ſeale wyll ſake ¶lo ſayde mortymer ſyres ye al hath ſayd knowlegyth hym letter hys ſeale ye ſhall conteyned therin thenne mortymer openyd letter folde tofore togyder redde openly worde worde herynge theym whan letter redde ſayd loo ſyres ye haue herde alle ye herin wrytē hath knowlegyth letter ſeale may go therfro thenne cryed yaue dome ſholde hangyd drawen hys heed ſmyten manere traytour hys heyres dyſheryted euer ſo ladde forth put pryſon whan done quene wiſt dampned way lawe lyf lym̄e hys heyres dyſheryted euermore thrugh open knowlegynge playncourt thought good forſayd ſyr edmond haſtyly ſlayne wythout wyttynge kyng elles kynge wolde lyghtly foryeue hym hys dethe thenne ſhode torne theym ſo moche ſorowe ſo empechyd anone quene thrugh counſeyll mortymer wyth ony counſell ſent haſt baylyfe wyncheſtre ſholde ſmyte syr edmondes heed erle kente wythout ony manere abydynge reſpyte vpon payne lyf lymme ſholde haue none execuſyon cauſe caryenge withſtandynge iugement tho toke baylyes ſyr edmonde pryſon ladde hym beſyde caſtell wyncheſtre made gonfermer ſmyte hys heed none durſte doo ſoo deyed ala whyle ſay tenth daye octobre thyrde yere kynge edwarde regne ¶and whan kyng wiſt therof wonder ſory lete entyere hym frere mynors wyncheſtre ¶of deth ſyr roger mortymer erle marche ſo befell tyme ſyr roger mortymer erle ye marche ſo proude ſo hauteyne helde lorde reame pere tho became ſo coueytous folowed dame iſabell quenes courte kynge edward moder beſet hys peny worth offycers quenes houſe holde ſame manere kynges offycers dyde ſo made takynge touchynge vytayle alſo caryages dyde bycauſe expencys gadre treſoure ſo dyde without nombre myght ¶tho made hym wonder preuy wyth quene iſabell ſo moche lordſhyppe rete grete lordes englonde hym adrad wherfore kyng counſeylle warde hym agreued ordeyned amonge vndo hym thoroughe pure reaſon lawe cauſe kynge edwarde ye kȳges fader traytourſly thrugh hym murdred caſtel corf ſayde playnly ſome parte boke deth ¶and ſome kynges counſeyll louyd mortymer tolde hym preuyte ye kynge counſel aboute daye daye hym dyſtroye vndo wherfore mortymer ſore anoyed angry deuyll ayenſt kynges counſeyll ſay wolde auenged ſo euer toke ¶it longe afterwarde kynge edward dame phylyp wyf dame iſabell kynges moder ſyr roger mortymer ne wente vnto notyngham ſoiurne ſo befell quene iſabel thrugh coūſeyll mortymer toke keyes yates caſtell notyngham man myght come nother ne thrugh commaundement mortymer ne kynge ne none coūſeylle ¶and tyme fel mortymer deuyll wrath bolled alſo wrathe ayenſt kynges men edward pryncypally ayenſt theym hym accuſyd kynge deth ſyr edwarde fader ¶and pryuely coū ſeyll take bytwene quene iſabell mortymer byſſhop lyncoln ſyre symōde bedford ſyr hugh trompyngton preuy theyr counſeyll vndo theym mortymer accuſyd vnto kynge faders deth treaſon felonye ¶wherfore tho kynges coūſeyll whan wiſt mortymers caſtynge pryuely came kynge edwarde ſayd mortymer wold theym dyſtroye bycauſe hym accuſyd kynge edwardes dethe fader prayed hym wolde mayntene theyr ryght ¶and thyſe lordes purſued quarell syr wyllyam mountagu ſyr wyllyam de bohum syr wyllyam broder ſyr rauf stafforde ſyr robert herforde ſyr wyllyam clynton ſyr iohan neuell hornby many theyr cō ſent thyſe ſwore vpon boke mayntene quarell moche myghte befell ſo after· ſyr wyllyam mountagu ne none kynges frendes muſte herberowed caſtell mortyme • went toke theyr herberowe dyuerſe place twone nothyngham tho ſore ferde leeſt mortymer ſholde theym dyſtroye haſte came vnto kyng edward ſyr wyllyam mauntagu caſtell pryuely hym tolde ne none hys cōpany ſholde take mortymer without counſeyll helpe wyllyam elande conſtable ſame caſtell ¶now truelye ſayd kynge loue well· therfore counſeyl ye go forſayd coneſtable commaūde hym name frende youre helpe take mortymer al thynge yleft vpon peryll lyf lym̄e ¶tho ſayd mountagu syr lorde graunt mercy ¶tho wente forthe forſayd mountagu came coneſtable caſtell tolde hym kynges wyll ¶and anſwerde ſayde· kynges wyll ſholde doone moche myghte wolde ſpare manere dethe ſwore made othe ¶tho ſayde ſyr wyllyam moū tagu conſtable herynge alle helpynge ſame quarell certes dere frende v behouyth werke aduys take mortymer ſyth ye keper caſtell hath keyes warde ¶syr ſayd conſtable wyll ye vnderſtonde caſtell yates ben lockyd keyes dame iſabell ſent hyther nyght ſhe hath keyes ther layeth vnder lurſell bedde vnto morowe ſo ye maye come caſtell yates manere wyſe knowe aleye ſtretchythoute warde vnder erthe ſayde caſtell gothe weſte whiche aleye dame iſabel quene ne none men ne mortymer ne none company knowith ſo ſhall lede thrugh ye aley ſo ye ſhall come caſtell withoute aſpyenge ony man yt enmyes ſame nyghe ſyr wyllyam mountagu lordes quarell ſame conſtable alſo went theym hors made ſemblaūt go mortymers ſyght anone mortymer harde thys tydynges wende yt wolde haue gone ouer ſee fere hym ¶and anone ryght cōpanye toke coūſeyll amonge theym lete theyr paſſage ſnetelletters anone porter ſo none grete lordes ſholde go home theyr owned coūtrees yf areſted take amonge thynges wyllyam elande coneſtable ſayd caſtell pryuely ladde ſyre wyllyam mountagu hys company ſayd waye vnder erth tyll came caſtell went vp toure mortymer ſyr hughe trompynton theym aſcryed hydouſly ſayd traytours nought ye ben comyn caſtell ye ſhall deye yet euell dethe euerychone anone one theim mountages company vp wyth mace ſmote ſame hugh vpon heed brayne braſte fell grounde ſoo deed euyll deth ¶tho toke mortymer armyd hym toures dore whan herde noyſe theym drede ¶and whan quene iſablell ſawe mortymer taken ſhe made moche ſorowe herte thyſe wordes vnto theym ſhe ſayd fayre ſyres praye ye doo noo harme body thy knyght welbeloued frende dere coſyn ¶tho wente then came brought mortymer preſentyd hym vnto kynge edwarde commaunded brynge hym ſaue warde ¶but anone conſentynge vnto mortymers doynge herde tell taken wente hydde pryuely nyght wente towne eche one waye heuy herte mornynge chere lyued vpon theyr londes well myghte ¶and ſame yere mortymer take hadde ix ſcore knyghtes without quyres ſergaū te army fote men then̄e mortymer ladde london ſyr edmonde bedforde ladde wyth hym taken ye conſtable toure kepe ¶but warde mortymers lyfe examyned weſtmeſtre kynge geate lordes englonde peryll myght falle reame enquer • alſo whiche conſentynge ſyr edwardes dethe kynges fader alſo thrugh whome scottes eſcaped fro stanhope ſcotlonde without leue kynge edwarde alſo ye chartre ragman delyuered vnto scottes homage feautees lordes scotlōde conteyned scottes ſholde doo euer englyſſhe kynge reame scotlond wherfore iugyd drawen hangyd treaſon myſcheyf came vnto hym ſaynt andrewes euen yere incarnacyon lorde iheſu cryſte mcccxxx ¶howe kynge edwarde gate ayen vnto hym gracyouſly homage feautees scotlonde wherof put oute thrughe ye falſe counſeyll quene iſabell moder ſyre roger mortymer newely made erle matche haue ye herde iohan bayllol tyme pea choſen kynge scotlonde cauſe came eldeſt doughter erle dauyd huntyngton kynge alyſanders broder scotlond deyed without heyre hys body begoten iohan made feaute homage kynge edwarde henryes ſone thyrde londes scotlonde afterwarde ſayd hys homage thrugh counſeyll scottes yere lorde ·mcclxxiiii ſente vnto pope thrugh fals ſuggeſtyō made hys othe vnto forſayd kynge edwarde ouer hys eſtate wil whyche othe pope hym aſſoyled thrughe hys bully hym yſent ¶and anone kynge edwarde wyſt therof ordeyne anone hys baron came vnto berwyk cōquered towne whyche conqueſt ſlayne xxv thouſande vii hundred bayllol kyng scotlond came yeldyd hym gode kynge edwarde ye kyng delyuered hym toure london grete lordes hym yt tho taken berwyk yaue theym ſaufconduyte goo scotlonde scottes ſythe thrugh theyr falſneſſe warred vpon good kynge edwarde whan ſyr iohan bayloll kynge scotlonde ſawe wente ouer ſee vnto dunpier lyued vpon hys londes well myght tyll ye scottes wolde amende theym theyr myſdedys treſpaas ladde hym ſyr edwarde ſone wherfore scottes dyſpyte hym callyd hym ſyr iohan turnlabard bycauſe wolde ne offend ne treſpaas ayenſt good kynge edwarde englonde ſoo ſoke hys reame scotlonde ſette therof lytyll pryce ſyr iohan dwellyd longe tyme fraunce tyll deyed ſyr edward ſone receyued hys herytage dyde homage kynge fraunce londes dunpier ſo befell afterwarde edward iohan bayllols ſone hym ſquyre englond yt yorke ſhyre callyd iohan barnaby edwarde bayllol louyd hym moche nyghe hym full preuy ſo iohn̄ barnaby debate frenche man towne dunpier ſo ſlewe hym wente hys way haſte myghte caſtell haue ſocoure helpe hys lorde anone came offycers towne take iohn̄ barnaby felon ſyr edward lorde holpe hym reſcowed hym nyght made hym go caſtell ſo went hys waye came englonde withoute ony harme ¶and whan kyng fraunce ſaw ſyr edwarde reſcowed felon became wonder wrothe ayenſt ſyr edward anone lete hym areſtyd toke hys hondes londes tho dwellyd ſyr • edward pryſon vnto tyme ſyr henry beaumount came fraunce whiche henry ſomtyme erle anguyſſhe scotlonde put therof whan chacordement bytwene englonde scotlond thrugh quene iſabell ſyr roger mortymer theyr company ye moryage ſhe made bytwene dauyd roberte brus ſone dame iohanne tour kynge edward ſyſter englond well vnderſtonde thys att ende ſholde come ryght yf ſyre edwarde baylloll ryght heyre reame scotlonde ¶and kyng fraunce lowys louyd moche ſyr henry wyth hym full preuy thought make delyueraunce ſyr edward baylloll yf myghte ony maner wyſe ¶tho prayed kynge wolde grace gaūt hym ſyre edwarde bayllols body vnto nexte parlement myght lyue hys owne rente meane tyme myghte ſtonde iugyd perys att parlement kynge grauntyd hym prayer made forſayde edwarde delyuered pryſon manere aboue ſayd anone pryſon ſyr henry toke hym forth hym ladde hym englonde made hym dwelle pryuely att manere sandhall vpon ouſe yorke ſhyre lady veſcy ſoo ordeyned hym huge retenewe englyſſhmen alſo alyuntes conquere ayen herytage ſo yaue moche ſyluer vnto ye ſouldyours alyauntes helpe hym • behyght helpe hym myght faylled hym att hys mooſt nede ¶and tyme dauyd erle moryf herde tell ſyr edward bayloll pryuely come englond came hym made wyth hym gerte ioye comynge ſayd vnto hym behyght hym greate lordes englonde ſholde hym entendaunte ſholde hym holde kynge ryght heyre scotlōde dyd hym feaute· ¶tho came ſyr henry beaumonte kynge edwarde englonde prayed hym waye charyte wolde graunt greate vnto ſyr edwarde baylloll myghte ſau • ly goo londe frome sandhall vnto scotlonde conquere hys ryght herytaunce scotlond ¶the kynge anſwerde ſayde yf ſuffre bayllol go thrugh londe scotlonde thenne people wolde ſaye yt ſhold aſſentynge vnto company ¶now ſyr praye yt ye wolde yeue hym leue take hym ſouldyours englyſſhmen myght ſaufly lede hym thrugh londe scotlonde ſyr vpno thys couenaunte yf ſo befall god bydde dyſcomfyted bytayll thrugh scottes alſo al lordes holde bayllol ben euer rente haue englonde kynge vppon couenaunte grauntyd theyr bone towchynge hym tho ſame quarell whiche claymed haue londes rente reame englonde thyſe name tho lordes purſued ſayd matere quarell ¶that ſaye ſyr edwarde bayllol whiche chalengyd reame scotlonde ſyr henry beaumonte erle anguſſhe ſyr dauyd stroboly erle theles ſyr geffray mombraye walter comyn many put theyr herytage sctlonde whan pea made bytwene englonde scotlonde ſayde ye ſhall vnderſtonde thyſe lordes tooke theym fyue houndred men armes two thouſande archer fote men tho wente ſhyppe rauen pore ſayled ſee tylle came vnto scotlond came londe kynkehorne xii myle fro ſaynt iohannes towne anone ſent ſhyppes agayne ſhold hurte ne empeyred neyther taht man ſholde go ſhyppes agayne thoughe nede abybe perylles flee ſtonde rather ſuffre deth flee mayntene true quarell whan erle fyffe fyers man ſterne harde bayllol come taſte londe scotlond came haſt kynke horne ·iii thouſand scottes dyſtroye hym ſhold come londe ſyr edwarde bayllol company hym dyſcomfyted whiche dyſcomfyture ſyr alyſāder seton ſlayne many erle fyffe th • ſore full euyll aſhamyd ſo lytyll cō pany hym dyſcomfyted ſhamefully put hym company alyue flee ¶tho came ſyr edwarde bayllol toke coō tree aboute hym tyll came vnto abbay dūfermlin ther founde vytaylles hym folke amonge thynge founde chambre aboute fyue houndred grete ſtaues • fyne oke longe prykes yren ſtele toke delyuerd moſte ſtrōgeſt men companye anone yede fro then lodged hym felde ii myles ſaynt iohānes towne whan burgeys towne herde erle fyffe dyſcomfyted thrughe baylloll brake ye brydges made ouer water erne ſo bayllol myght go ouer wherfore lodged hym nyght lytyll hede toke reſte ſayde vnto people dere lordes ye know full well ben lodged bytwene enmyes maye v hampre noo bote dethe wherfore yf abyde ſtylle nyght· wene ſhall torne v moche harme power scotlonde may euery wexe encrece maye ſo doo ben lytylle people ayenſte theym wherfore praye loue almyghty god make v bolde hardy may myghtely take scottes nyght boldly werre vpon theym lete v purſue theym thys nyghte yf trauaylled thorugh v ſee hardyneſſe scottes ſee ſo traueylled wery· ſorer woll adradde v fyght fyerſly thenne ſhall fyght purſue soo thrughe grace god worlde ſhall ſpeke doughtynes chyualry ¶and ſyres vnderſtondeth wel companye came ſyr robert baylloll graunted well vnto counſeyll therof ryght gladde anone purſued vppon scottes became wonder wery baylloll company ſore folowed dyde moche harme ſorowe thrugh ther aſſente ſo thy myght feblyneſſe theym helpe lytyl people ¶but tho ſayd scottes amonge nowe befall ſo lytyll people baylloll hath wynge doth v ſo moche traueyll ſorowe certes ſemyth v werketh grace wonder gracyous hys quarell certes ſhall dede maye come hym v yelde sith fader ſete v pryce ¶and amonge alle hys thynges baylloll people paſſed water erne ſo robert swynerton ſone fyers angrye wente forthe ſawe people army full well arayed forth wente vnto wyth faught ſlewe toke many wolde abyde neuertheles aſſewte wende grete hoſte scotlond whan came morowe gadred theym togyder reſtyd theym whyle· ¶and whyle englyſſhemen reſted noble baron thomas veſcy noble barō stafforde pryckyd theyr hors vp downe hylles kepe eſtrees countree pryckyd vp downe ſaw grete hoſt gode araye ordeyned theyr wynge helmes ſheldes ſhynynge comynge vpon then̄e came tho two barōs ayen vnto bayllols folke ſayd loue god almyghty good cōforth ye ſhall haue batayll one ryght ¶and tho ſpake ſyr fouk ſone garenne· baran greate renowne dedys army syres vnderſtonde wyll ſaye haue ſeen many dyuers wynges well amonge ſaraſyns iewes amonge scottes yet ſawe neuer fourthe parte wynge fyght therfore yf ye wyl abyde enmyes ben ynough yf gode herte good courage loſte therfore loue god take v gode herte lette v bolde ad thynke neuer wyues ne oure chyldren cō quere enmyes batayll ¶and thrugh helpe lorde ſhall ouercome wyth came hoſte scottes warde theym full ſerely ayenſt ſyr edwarde baylloll thre bataylles well arayed armoure ¶and wonder fyerſly came warde bayllols company whan ſyr donald erle marcell scottes ſawe ſayd vnto roberte brus ſone robert brus thyſe wordes syr robert ſayd full fore thynkyth att herte thyſe people baylloll hathe brought wyth hym ſholde deye wyth dy • te scottes ſwerdes ſythe ben cryſten men ben therfore thynkyth grete charyte ſende vnto theym yelde theym vnto mercy raunſomme theym vnto greuous raunſomme moche haue taken oure londes done yll certes ſayd ſyr roberte brus haue well rerceyued thou arte enmye traytour vnto scotlonde ſythe thou wylte conſente ſaue dedely enmyes haue done v moche ſorowe ſhame ſemyth wel ye theyr aſſente certes robert ſayde ſyr donald falſly ye lye theyr company ne theyr conſent yt haſtyly ye ſhall ſe wyll fyz • e wyth rather ony thys company certes ſyr robert ſayd ſhall mauger thy hede aſſayll thou wyth yt pryckyd theyr ſtedys fye • ſly vpon gaſkemore theyr wynge theym folowed reng tho came mette wyth baylloll hys cōpany hangynge bough ī ſtrayte paſſage ſo faſt haſtyd thē vnto ye englyſſhmen ye thouſand felle vnto grounde echone ouer vpon hepe hors man bayllol men myghtyly ſtode ayenſt theym faſt ſlewe scottes grounde many wounded ſoo longe tyll ſtode vpon theym foyned theym wyth theyr ſwerdes ſperes thrughe theyr bodyes fulle ſore trauaylled vppon theym tylle became wonder wery wyſte doo scottes lete alyue fledde awaye ſaue ſelfe beſte manere myght tho purſued theym ſyre edwarde baylloll hys men ſlewe theym tyll nyght fro thēs wente saynt iohannes towne toke helde vytaylled ſelf owne wyll foūde ynough wherwith make mery tho made baylloll men yt wonded goo ſhyp ſayll englonde hele ther woundes ye tyme flēmynge ſee ſtonge theyf robber callyd crab flēmī ge dryuen flaundres hys wyckydneſſe therfore came scotlond holde ſcottes dyde moche harme englyſſhmen myght thys crabbe mette bayllols men ye ſee woūded batayll yt ſent ayen englonde hele theyr woundes crabbe yaaf theym gete aſſawte wold haue ſlayne theym euery chone englyſſhmen defended well manly dyſcomfyte crabbe company tho gan fle scotlond ¶and cam towarde ſaynt iohānes towne foūde grete conpany ſcottes yt come ayen togyder dyſcomfyture gaſkemore whyche byſeyged bayllol hys men ī ſame towne ſaynt iohan· anone tolde tolde scottes dyſcomfyted englyſſhmen yt woundyd gaſkemore went towarde englonde fort hele theyr woundes ſayd scottes yt ſholde haue nother power ne myghte ne grace ayenſt edwarde bayllol cauſe ſcomfyted empeyred alle chyualry scotlond handfall men • ōpte ayenſt scottes ſlayne wherfore coūſeylled remeue ſege ſaynt iohannes towne kepe theym beſt manere myght ¶the scottes vnderſtode crabbe ſayd ſothe ſoke ſege wente then nyghte ¶whan thys thynge knowe thrughe scotlonde lordes knyghtes dyſcomfyted gaſkemore scotlonde thrughe ſyre edwarde bayllol ye ſhall vnderſtonde yt lordes ladyes gentyls scotlond came wonder faſte ſaynt iohannes towne yeldyd theym vnto bayllol hym dyd homage feaute theyr ſondes yelde theym pea theym receyued frely fro then wē te abbay scone crowned kyng scotlond lete crye hys pea thrughe londe ¶and ſame tyme befell kynge edwarde helde parlement amonge hys leyges newe caſtell vpon tyne amende treſpaces wronges ben done londe ſyr edwarde bayllol kynge scotlonde came hym thyther dyde hym homage feautee reame scotlond thys maner kynge edwarde englonde gadred ayen hys homage feautees scotlonde wher put thrughe counſeyll aſſent dame iſabell hys moder ſyr roger mortymer erle marche tho toke bayllol kyng scotlond hys leue kynge edwarde englonde went then owne londe scotlonde ſet lytyll ſuche counſeylled hym holpen hym hys quarel wherfore wente hym went lyued theyr owne londes renttes scotlond ¶and ſo befel warde longe kynge scotlonde ne remeued came toure anande tooke hys dwellynge thyder came hym company knyghtes ſtronge men worthy yelded vnto kynge bare theym ſo fayr dede coū tenaūce ſo truſtyd moche vpon theym anone traytours ſawe truſtyd moche vpon theym ordened amonge theym fyfty company wolde haue ſlayne theyr lorde kynge thrugh grace almyghty god brake thrugh walle hole chambre god wolde ſcapyd theyr trechery hys men ſlayne eſcaped moche dred vnto towne cardoyll helde hym ſore anoyed befell vpon ladyes euen ye cōcepcyon ¶tho ſent kynge edward baylloll kynge edwarde englonde falſly tratourſly lytyll tyme put ſhame ſorowe thrughe lyege men vppon truſtyd wonder moche prayed hym ye loue god wolde mayntene hym helpe hym ayenſt hys enmyes kynge englond hym grete pyte behight helpe hym ſocour hym ſēt hym worde ſhold hold hym pea ſtyll ye forſayde cyte cardoyll tyll yt gadred power ¶tho ordeyned kyng edwarde englonde counſeyll london lete gadre men diuers ſhyres englond whan alle redy wente towarde towne berwyk vpon twede theder came hym kyng edward baylloll ſcotlond powere beſeged towne made without towne fayr towne pauylyons dyched theym abowte ſo drede the▪ scottes made manye aſſawte • onnes wyth engynnes ye towne wherwyth dyſtroyed many fayre houſes chyrches alſo beten downe ye erthe grete ſtones ſpitouſly came gonne engynes neuertheles ye scottes kept ryght well towne yt tho two kynges myghte come therin longe tyme n • theles kynges abode ſo longe tyll tho within ye towne fayled vytaylles alſo ſo wery wakynge wyſt ¶and ye ſhall vnderſtende tho ſcottes yt wythin ye towne berwyk thrugh comyn counſeyl theyr aſſent lete crye vpon ye wally twone myght haue pea englyſſhmē therof prayed kyng grace mercy prayed gym trwes viii dayes vpon couenaunte yt yf reſcowed ſyde towne towarde scotlond ye scottes within viii dayes yt wolde yelde theym vnto ye kyng towne alſo holde couenaunt prouffred kinge xii hoſtages towne berwyk ¶whan hoſtages delyuerde vnto ye kynge anone tho towne ſent vnto ye ſcottes tolde theym theyr ſorowe myſcheyf scottes tho came pryuely ouer water twede ye bought abbaye ſyr wyllyā dyket tho stewarde ſcotlonde many came wyth hym put theym theyr grete peryll themſelf att tyme ther lyf came ouer brydge yt broke ye ſtones away many theyr company drowned forſayd wyllyam went ouer company came ſhyppes englond ſlew barge hull xvi· mē went towne berwyk water ſyde wherfore scottes helde tho towne reſcowed aſkyd theyr hoſtages ayen kynge englonde kynge ſente theym worde ayē axyd theyr hoſtages wrō ge ſyth thath came towne enlonde ſyde couenaunt bytwene theim towne ſholde reſcowed halfe scotlonde anone tho commaūded kynge edwarde yelde towne wolde haue hoſtages scottes ſayd towne reſcowed welle ynoughe therto wolde theym holde whan kyng edwarde ſawe scottes breke theyr couenauntes made wonder wrothe anone lete ſyr thomas fytz wyllyam ſyr alyſā der feton warden berewyk whyche thomas perſon dunbarre lete thē take fyrſte afore hoſtages cauſe syr alyſanders fader keper towne ¶and tho commaunded euerye daye two hoſtages towne tyll deth yf yelded towne ſo ſholde teche breke theyr couenauntes whan towne herde thyſe tydyngꝭ became wonder ſory ſente kyng wolde graunt viii dayes reſpyte bytwene two hundre men army xx men armes myght ſtrenthe go bytwene ye towne berwyk theym vytaylle towne muſt holde reſcowed yf ſoo xxi xxii ſlayne tho two hundred ſayde towſholde holde reſcowed thys couenaunte holde ſente hym xii forſayd towne hoſtage kynge englonde grauntyd theym theyr prayer toke hoſtages ſaynt margaretꝭ eue yere grace m·cccxxxiii corden alein stewarde wyllyam abbrehin wyllyā morys iamys fytz wyllyam adam lemoſt walter fytz gylbert iohn̄ cerleton robert wallam viic men army xviim comyns ¶in thyrd parte batayll scotlonde thyſe ¶the ſūme comnyns amounteth liiim iiic ¶the ſōme totalle people aboueſayd amounteth lxvmviicxlv thyſe lx vi gretate lordes ladde greeſte lordes aboueſayde infonre bataylles tolde beforen allon fote kynge edwarde englonde edwarde bayllol kyng scotlonde hadde well apparelled theyr folke foure bataylles fyghte fote ayenſt scottes theyr enmyes ¶and englys mynſtrels blewe theyr trumpetes yr claryons hydouſly aſcryed scottes tho euery englyſſhe batayll two wynges pryce archer whiche batayll ſhot arowes ſo faſte ſoo ſore scottes myghte helpe themſefle ſmote scottes thouſandes vnto grounde began flee fro englyſſhmen ſaue theyr lyues whan scottes knaues ſaw ſcomfyture scottes fall faſt grounde preckyd faſte theyr mayſters horſe ſporis kept theym peryl ſete theyr mayſters force whan thenglyſſmen ſaw lept theyr horſes faſte purſued scottes abode ſlewe downe ryght ¶there men myght ſee doughtineſſe noble kynge edward hys men manly purſewed scottes flowe drede men myght ſee many scottyſſhman caſte downe vnto ye groū de baners dyſplayde hackyd peces many gode haberyoyne ſtele blode bathe many tyme scottes gadred cōpanyes euer diſcomfyted ¶and ſo befell god almyghty wolde scottes day nomore fayſon ne myghte ayenſt englyſſhemen xx ſhepe among v wulues ſo scottes dyſcomfyted yet ſcottees well v men ayenſt one englyſſhmen ye batayll done halydoune hyll beſyde towne berwyk whiche batayll ſlayne scottes xxxv· thouſande vii houndred xii englyſſhemen xiii victory befel englyſſhmen ſaynt margyretes euen holy virgyn martyr yere lorde iheſu cryſte mcccxxxii ¶and whyle thys doynge laſtyd englyſſhe page toke pylfre scottes ſlayne euery man myght take wythout ony chalengynge ony man ſo thys gracyous victory kynge torned hym agayne vnto ſame ſyege berewyk ¶and whan ſyeged ſawe herde kynge edwarde ſpede yelded hym towne wyth caſtell morowe ſaynt margaretes daye ¶and thenne kynge dyde ordeyne ſyr edwarde baylloll noble worſhypfull men kepers gouernours scotlonde hys abſence hymſelfe torned ayē came enlōde vyctorye moche ioye alſo worſhyp nexte yere folowynge ſay yere incarnacyon oure lorde iheſu eryſte mcccxxxiii kynge edwarde vii· wente ayen scotlonde wynter tyme atte whiche vyage caſtell kylbrygge scotlonde hym men hym recouered ayenſt scottes owne luſte ¶and ſame yere ſyr edwarde bayloll kyng scotlonde helde parlement scotlonde many noble lordes let make agayne morowe aſſumpcōn lady kynge edwarde paſſed ouer ye water seyn goyege warde creſcy dyſtroyed way townes peple dwellynge ther feeſt ſaynt bartholomewe paſſed ouer water ſōme vnhurt englond whan caſtels townes yolden hym longe holden fraunce grete company aſſembled togyder ſyr bartram claykyn noble knyght good warryour wente purpoſed hym put pers kynge spayne kyngdome helpe mooſte partye forſayd grete company truſtynge alſo vpon helpe fauour pope moche come eeres ye ſame pers ſholde lede vſe ſynfull lyf whiche pers ſmyten wyth drede tydynge fledde gaſcoyne prynce edwarde haue ſocoure hym whan fledde spayne henry broder baſtarde aſſent mooſt party spayne thrughe helpe ye ferefull company ſpake fyrſt crowned kyng spayne ye nombre ſame cōpany rekened ſette nombre xlm fytynge men ¶this ſame yere moneth iune come grete cōpany nauye ye dane gadred togyder northe ſee purpoſynge come englonde reue robbe alſo ſle countred mette ſee maryners gode fytynge men • countre dyſperpled theym aſhamyd went home ayen theyr owne coū tre amonge ye boyſtous veſſell ſtronge theyr nauye ouer ſaylled englyſſhmen peryſſhed drenched whiche stewarde worthy greate men denmarke taken pryſoners kynge englonde coūſeyll pryſoned whiche lordes dane afterwarde ſought haue hadde ayen wyth theyr goodes yt loſt well apayed ne pleaſed ye anſwer torned homwardes ayen leuynge behynde thē innes preuely writen ſcrowes walles yet ſhall dane waſt wane thenne happed englyſſhe wryter wrote ayenſt duke manere ſhall dane fette theyr banys ¶and time pers kynge spayne kynges ſaye kynge nauerne kynge malogre beynge meanes wenten bytwene prayed counſeyll helpe ſyr edwarde prynce who counſeyll whan vnderſtandynge theyr artycles deſyre requyred tho kynges lothe aſhamed ſaye nay contrary netheles gaſt leſt ſhold ony preiudyce ayenſt pope longe tyme taryed wolde graunte conſente therto tyll better counſeyl rauyſemente good delyberacyon kyng edward fader whan hym euery day contynually beſechynge many noble men requyred ſpoken many prayer ſente made bytwene thā prynce edward ſente fader cōplaynyng letter alſo confortable conteynyng al theyr ſuggeſtyons cauſes wyth ye kynges epyſtles letter haue cōforte helpe wronges done kyng spayne alſo ſuche thynges myght falle kynges alſo yf ye ſoner holpē amended thrugh done helpe knyghthode thē aſked deſyred ¶the whiche letter whan kynge hys counſeyll ſeen ſuche kynge ſpoylynge robbynge moche merueyll ſente ayen comfortable letter prynce edwarde hys ſone kynges warned arme ordeyne theym ayenſt miſdoer withſtande helpe god ryght byleue faythe holy chyrche alſo wyth theyr mynyſters ryghtes libertees defende theyr enmyes euylles al ayenſt bytterly punyſſhe deſtroble al ye ryghtꝭ lybertes preuyleges holy chirche encreaſe mayntene amende alle thynges yt wronfully taken withdrawen borē waye hym ony cauſe hym haſtely reſtore ayen dryue put oute ſaraſyns myſbyleued people kyngdom wyth ſtrenth power ſuffre ne admitte none ſuche manere thynge ne cauſe dwelle therin whan taken cryſten woman ſholde neuer come none woman bedde ne none mannes wyfe defoyle ¶all thyſe ſayd thynges trewly kepe contynue fulfyll alle hys lyfe tyme douuden othe afore notaryes preſence wytneſſe tho kynges wyth prynces ¶and gracyous prynce edwarde vndertoke cauſe quarell kyng depoſed behyghte hym grace almyghty god reſtore hym ayen kyngdom lette ordeyne gadre togyder forth alle haſte nauye men armes warre fyght ſayde cauſe ¶and ſame yere vpon ſande scottes ſee yt many man ſawe thre dayes togyder ſeen two egles whiche ye one come ſouthe north cruelly ſtrongly fought togyder wraſtled togyder ſouth elge fyrſt ouercome ye north egle rente hym bylle clawes yt ſhold reſte ne take byrthe ſouth egle fleyth home owne coſtes· ¶and anone folowed ſeen morne ye ſonne ryſynge laſt daye octobre ſauynge one many ſterres gaddred togyder hepe felle downe erthe leuynge byhynde fyre bemes maner lyghtnynge flammes brent cōſumed men clothes men
