nede wolde gladly euery man hys power ſtate hym helpe lene publyſſhed ſhewed parlemente many playntes defautes dyuers offycers ye reame namely lorde latymer kynges chamberlayne bothe kynge eke reame ¶and alſo att laſte ſpoken treated dame alyce pers grete wronges euyll gouernaunce yt done hyr counſeyl reame whiche dame alyce pers ye kyng holden longe tyme hys lemman wherfore laſte wonder though thrugh frealter woman excytynge hyr ſteringe conſented hyr lewdneſſe euyll coūſeyl whiche dame alyce alſo lorde latymer ſuche ye meued kynge euyll gouernaunce ayenſt profyte reame alſo comynalte aſked deſyred ſholde remeued put awaye theyr ſtedes wyſe mē worthy trewe wel aſſaied proued good gouernaunce ſholde put theyr ſtedes amonge al one amonge comunes wyſe knyght trewe eloquent man whoos name pers delamare ſame pers choſen ſpeker comunes parleament ſame pers tolde publyſſhed trouthe reherſed ye wronges ayenſte forſayd dame alyce certayne perſones kynges counſeyll bydde comyns ¶and alſo truſtynge moche ſupported mayntened thys mater helpe fauour prynce anone prynce dede att inſtaunce requeſte forſayd dame alyce thys pers de amare iugyd perpetual pryſon caſtell notyngham ¶and vi kal iule laſtynge ye ſame parlemente deyed prynce edwarde kynge edwardes fyrſt ſone ſaye trynyte ſonday worſhyp whyche feſte wōte euery yere euer ī ye worlde holde made mooſt ſolēpnyte myght who name fortune knyghthode yf ector alle men bothe cryſten hethen whyle liued good poynt wōdred moche dradde hym wonder ſoore whoos body worſhypfully buryed crychyrche caunterbury ſame yere mē erles tenauntes warwyk aroſe malycyouſly ayenſt ye abbot couent eueſham theyr tenauntes deſtroyed thabbaye towne woūded bete theyr men ſlewe many theym wente theyr maners place dyde moche harme brake downe ther parkes cloſes ſlewe theyr wylde beſtes chaced brekynge theyr fyſſhe poundes hedes lete water theyr pondes ſtewes ryuers renne toke fyſſhe bare dyde theym ſorowe myght ſo ferforthe forſoth deſtroyed perpetuall abbay theyr membres apportenaunces yf kynge ſoner holpen taken hede therto therfore kyng ſent letter ye erle warwyk chargyng hym cōmaūdynge hym ſholde ſtynt redreſſe amende tho euyll doer brekers pea ſo meanes lordes frendes pea made bitwene hurtynge ſayd ye kynge wolde gouerned tyme bi lordes ye parlement toke made ſone duke lancaſtre gouerneur reame whiche ſtode ſoo ſtyll gouernour tyl ye tyme dyed ¶the ſame yere cā delmaſſe parlement done kynge aſked ſubſidye clargy lay fee graūtyd hȳ ſay ſholde haue euery perſone ye lay fee man woman paſſed fourtene yere aege foure pēs takē pore beggers knowen openly nede pore beggers ¶and ſhold haue euery man holy chyrche benefyced promoted twelue pen promoted iiii pen taken iiii ordres frere beggers ſame yere myghelmaſſe rycharde prynce edwardes ſone made prynce wale kyng gaf ye duchy cornewayle ye erldom cheſtre tyme ye cardynale englond ye iiii day mary mawdalenes day dyner ſodaynly ſmyte paſlye loſte ſpeche mary mawdalen • daye deyed ¶of ye dethe kynge edwarde ſyr iohan monſter warch knyght drawē hanged falſneſſe ryght anone lii yere kynge edward begynnynge octobre pope gregorye ix broughte remeued courte wyth hym auy • yon come ¶and xii daye apryl iohan monſterwarthe knyght att london drawen hangyd quartred ſent four cheyf townes englond heed ſmyten ſete vpon londen brydge ſame iohn̄ full vntrewe kynge ye reame coueytous vnſtable tooke oftymes grete ſōmes money kynge coūſeyll men armes wage ſholde haue paed tooke owne vſe dradde att laſte ſholde ſhent accuſed ſame cauſe fled pryuely kyng fraunce ſworne hym become hys man behyghte hym greate nauye spayne confucyon deſtroynge englonde ryghtfull god preuyte vnknowen ſuffred hym fyrſt beſhente ſpylt ſo traytourſly falſly betrayed hys lyege lorde kynge englonde peple hys reame whiche groū de ſame iohn̄ borne wyckydly thrughe batayll deſtroyed brought hys curſed purpoſe feeſt saynt george tho next kynge edwarde gaaf rychard burdeux heyr yt prynce edwardes ſone wyndſore thordre knughthode made hym knyght whyche kyng edward whan regned li yere xi kal iune deyde shene buryed worſhypfully weſtmyſter who ſoule god haue mercy thys kynge edwarde ſoth paſſynge godenes full gracyous amonge worthy men worlde paſſed ſhone vertue grace gauen hym god aboue predeceſſours yt noble men worthy well harted man hardy drade neuer myſhappes ne harmes ne euyll fortune yt myght fall noble warryoure fortunate londe ſee batayls aſſembles paſſinge glory ioy vyctory meke benygne homely ſobre ſoft mē well ſtraūgers owne ſubgettes yt vnder gouenaūce deuoute holy bothe god hooly chyrche worſhypped holpe mayntened holy chirche theyr mynyſtres wyth maner reuerence treatable well auyſed temporall worldly nedes wyſe counſeylle dyſcrete meke ſpeke dedes maners gentyll well taught hauynge pyte dyſeace plecteuous geuynge bene faytes almoſes beſy curyous bayldynge lyghtly bare ſuffred wronges harmes whan gyuen ony occupacyon lefte thynge tyme tended ther ſemely body meyne ſtature hauynge al waye hyghe lowe good chere ſpronge ſhone ſo moche grace hym man beholde hys face dremed hym roged daye thynge ſholde hap hym ioyfull lyſynge gouerned hys kyngdome gloryouſly vnto aege large geuynge wyſ ſpentes fulfylled wyth honeſte good maners vertues vnder lyue regne wherfore hys fader loo ſpronge ſo ferre came hethenes barbary ſhewynge tellynge worthynes manhode alle londes londe vnder heuen brought forthe ſo noble kynge ſoo gentyll ſoo bleſſyd myght reyſe ſuche whan dede neuertheles lechery meuynge fleſſhe hauntyd hym aege wherfore rather ſuppoſe vnmeſurable fulfyllynge luſte lyfe ſhorted ſoner ¶and hereof take good hedelyke dedys bereth wymeſſe hys begynnynge alle thynges ioyfull lykynge hym people hys myddel aege paſſed people hyghe ioye worſhyp blyſſydnes ryght ſoo whan drewe aege drawynge donwarde thrughe lechery ſynnes lytell lytell alle tho ioyfull bleſſyd thynges proſperite decreaſyd deceſſyd bleſſyd man ¶karolus iiii emperour lodewyk xxxi yere chi man kynge beme wyſe man myghty man choſen emperour cōmaundement clemens lodewyk beynge lyue contemacy bycauſe aſked mekely poopes ſame ſutes hertes ſayde frome toure horſbacke thrughe cytye london ſmytfelde iuſtes ſholde holden ¶and feeſte iuſtes holden generalle al tho wolde come theder londe nacyon euer holden durynge xxiiii dayes kynges coſtes theſe xxiiii lordes anſwere manere people wolde come thyd theder came erle ſaynt poule fraūce many worthy knyghtes wyth hym dyuerſe partyes full worthely arayed holande henaude came lorde oſtruaūt ye duke ſone holande many worthy knyghtes hym holand full well arayed whan feeſt iuſtynge ended kynge thanked ſtraungers gaf thē many ryche gyftes ſo token theyr leue kynge lordes ladyes went home ayen theyr owne coūtres grete loue moche thanke ¶and ye xiii yere kyng rychardes regne batayll done kynges palays att weſtmynſter bytwene ſquyer nauerne yt wyth kynge rycharde ſquyre yt called iohn̄ walſſh poȳtes treaſō thys nauerne put vppon walſſhman nauerne ouercomē yelde hym recreaūt aduerſary anone dyſpoyled armure drawē oute palays tyburne hāged falſnes xiiii yere kynge rychardes regne ſyr iohan gaunt duke lancaſtre wente ouer ſee spayne chaleng hys ryght wyfes tytle vnto crowne spayne grete hoſt people mē armes archer hym • ducheſſe hys wyf hys thre doughters ouer ſee spayne ther grete whyle att laſt kynge spayne began treate duke lācaſtre accorded togyder thrugh theyr bothe counſeyll maner ye kynge spayne ſholde wedde duke doughter lancaſtre ryght heyre spayne ſhold gyue vnto ye duke lancaſtre golde ſyluer caſte grete wegges many iewels moche viii charyetes myght carye euery yere duringe duke lyf lācaſtre duches wyf x thouſande marke golde whyche golde auenture charge ſholde theym spayne yerely bryng vnto bayon duke aſſygnes ſuerte made alſo duke maryed hys doughters vnto kyng portyngale ſame tyme▪ whā done ſo come home ayen englonde hys good lady hys wyf alſo many worthy men deyed vpon flyx ¶in xv yere kynge rychardꝭ regne helde cryſtmaſſe manere wodſtok erle penbroke yonge lord tendre aege wolde lerne iuſte knyghte xvi yere kynge rychardes regne iohan hē de beyng tyme mayer london iohn̄ wal worth henry vanner beynge ſhreues london ſame tyme baker man bare baſket hors brede fletſtrete warde hoſtre came yonge man byſſhop salyſbury called romayn toke bors lofe baſket ye baker aſked hym dyde ſoo romayn torned ayen brake baker heed neyghbours came wold haue areſted thes romayn brake fledde lordes place ye conſtable wolde haue hym byſſhops men ſhette faſt yates kept place yt man myght entre moche people gadred thyder ſayd wolde haue hym el wolde brenue vp ye place alle wyth came mayer ſhreues wyth moche people ceſſyd malyce comyns made euery man go home hoſes kepe pea thys romayns lord byſſhop salyſbury mayſter iohan waltham ye tyme treſorer englonde ſyr thomas arundell archebyſſhop yorke chaunceler englonde byſſhop made hys complaynte vnto chaunceler peple cyte lōdon theſe two byſſhops grete malyce vengeaunce come vnto kynge wyndeſore made greate cōplaynt vpon mayer ſhreues anone cyte warde came kynge counſeyll caſte vnto cytye greuous herte wonder grete malyce anone ſodeynly ye kyng ſent ye mayer lōdon two ſhreues came hym vnto caſtell wyndſore kynge rebuked mayer ſhreues full foule offence done ayenſt hym offycers hys chambre london wherfor depoſed put mayer bothe ſhreues done xiiii dayes afore ye feeſt ſaynt iohn̄ baptyſt ye kynge called hym knyght called ſyre edwarde dalyngrygge made hym wardeyne gouernour cyte chambre lō ouer hys people ther ſo kepte offyce foure wekes bycauſe ſo gentyl tendre cytezens london wherfore kynge depoſed hym made ſyr bunde wyne radyngton knyght conrtrouller kynges houſhold wardeyne gouernour chambre people ther choſe hym worthy men cyte ſhreues wyth hym gouerne kepe ye kynges lawes cyte one called gelbert mawefelde thomas ne wenton ſhreues ye mayer two ſhreues alderman wyth worthy craftes london wente foot vnto toure london came coneſtable towre gaaf mayer ye ſhreues theyr othe charge ſholde haue taken eſcheker weſtmynſter ye kynges court iuſtyces baron eſcheker went home ayen kynge hys counſeyll grete malyce deſpyte yt cyte london remeued courtes weſtmynſter vnto cyte yorke yt ſaye chaūceler eſcheker lōdon ſoo weſtmynſter grete eaſe offycers vauntage kyng comunes reame ¶and whanne people london ſaw knewe theſe courtes comē ayen kynge hys people alſo mayer alderman chyef comunes cyte gaue grete ſomme golde comunes cyte ordeyned made grete ryaltees ayen hys comynge london haue hys grace good lordſhyp alſo theyr lybertees fraunchyſes geaūted vnto ayē wonte haue afore tyme thrugh grete inſtaunce prayer quene lordes ladyes kynge graū ted theym grace done shene sutherey kynge within two dayes came london mayer ye cyte ſhreues aldermē worthy men afterwarde rode ayenſt hym good araye vnto hethe hys ſyde shene mayer ſubmyttynge theym homely mekely maner obeyſſaunce vnto hym oughten thus brought ye kynge quene london whan ye kynge came yate london brydge preſenttd hym wyth mylke whyte ſtede ſadled brydled trapped wyth cloth golde reed partyed gyder quene palfrey alle whyte ſame ararye trappyd white andreed al conduytes london ranne wyth wyne whyte reed maner people drynke wolde bytwene ſaynt poules croſſe chepe made ſtage ryall ſtandynge vpon hygh theyn many angelles dyuers melodyes ſonges angelle came downe frome ſtage hyghe vyce ſete crowne golde pyght wyth ryche perles precyous ſtones vpon kynges heed vpon quenes heed ſoo cytezeyns brought kyng quene weſtmynſter theyr palays morne mayer ye ſhreues alderman london camen vnto kynge hys palays att weſtmynſter preſente hym two baſyns ſyluer ouergylted full coyned golde ſomme xx hoūdred pounde prayenge hym hygh mercy grace lordſhyp ſpecyally grace myght haue good loue lybertees fraunchyſes lyke wyſe wōte haue tymes letter patentes chartre confermed quene worthy lorde ladyes fell ther knee beſoughte kynge grace conferme kynge toke vp quene graunted hyr hyr aſkenge thanked kynge quene wente home ayen ¶and xvi· yere kyng rychardes regne certayn lordes ſcotlonde came englond gete worſhyp foot armes perſones erles marre chalēged erle marſhall englond iuſte hym certayne poyntes horſbak wyth ſharpe ſperes rode togyder two worthy knyghtes lordes certayne courſes full chalenge scottes erle made calle bothe hors man two hys rybbes brokē falle ſo borne thēs ſmythfelde home inne within lytyll tyme caryed home hors lytter att yorke deyed ¶and ſyr wayllyam darell knyght kynges banerer scotlonde made chalenge wyth ſyr peres courtayne knyght kynges banerer englonde certayne courſes yet horſbacke ſame felde whan ryden certayne cours aſſayed myghte haue better gaaf ouer wold nomore chalenge ſyr pers courtayne knyght kyngꝭ banerer englonde torned hors rode home vnto hys owne inne one cockeborne ſquyre scotlonde chalenged ſyr nycholl haberke knyght certayn courſes yet wyth ſharpe ſperes roden fyue courſes togyder euery courſe scot caſte downe hors man thus ouer englyſſhe lordes thanked god hadde felde ¶and xvii yere kyng rychardes regne deyde good gracyous quene anne wyt kyng rycharde manere shene ſhyre surrey vpon wytſondaye ſhe broughte london ſoo weſtmynſter ſhe buryed worthely entered beſyde saynt edwardes ſhryne whoos ſowle almyghty god haue pyte hys mercy amen ¶how kynge rycharde ſpowſed dame iſabell kynges doughter fraunce towne calays broughte hyr englond lette hyr appoyntemente ſholde comen vppon hym whan bedde ſlepe fetheren bedde anone bounde honde foot charged hym lye ſtyll whan hadde done thus token twoo ſmale towelles made theym two rydynge knottes caſte towelles hys necke tooke fetheren bedde laye vnder hym caſt aboute hym drewe theyr welles eche wayes ſome laye vpon ye fetheren bed vpon hym vnto tyme dede bycauſe ſhold make noys thus ſtrangled thys worthy duke vnto deth vppon who ſoule god hygh pyte haue mercy amen ¶and whan kynge hadde reſted thus worthy duke vncle ſente hym calays came ayen london haſte wyth wonder greate people ſoone comen large vnto parlement tyme founde ſoffycyent ſuerte abyde ye lawe anſwere manere poyntes kynge counſeyll wolde put vpon hym ¶and xxi • yere kynge rychardes regne ordeyned hym parlement att weſtmynſter whiche called greate parlemente parlement made iuge thys thre worthy lordes moo lyſt tyme iugement kynhe lete make haſt lōge hous large tȳbre whiche called halle couered tyles ouer open aboute ſydes maner men myght ſe thrugh dome holden vpon theſe forſayd lordes iugement gyuē forſayde parlemente come vnto parlement kynge ſent hys wryttes euery lorde baron knyght euery ſquyre euery ſhyre thrugh cheſtreſhyre cheyftayns countre gadred brought grete huge company people bothe knyghtes ſquyres prencypally yomē cheſtreſhyre whyche yemen archer kynge tooke hys owne courte gaate bowge court good ſtuffe ryght good ordynaunce longed vnto warre paſſed ouer ſee ordeyned made ſyr edmōde langley vncle duke yorke hys lyueteaunte englonde hys abſence gouernaūce counſeyll theſe foure knyghtes taken englond ferme kynge paſſed ſee came irlonde wel worthely receyued theſe rebelles ben called wylde iryſſhmen came downe kynge yolde hym body goodes owne wyll ſwore vnto hym lyege men dyde hym homage feaute good ſeruyſe thus conquered mooſt parte irlonde alytyll tyme ¶and whyle kynge rycharde thus irlonde ſyr henry bolyngbroke erle derby kyng made duke herforde whyche duke kynge exyled londe comen ayen enlonde chalenge dukedome lancaſter ryght trew herytage came downe fraunce londe vnto calays thē met hym ſyr thomas arūdell archebyſſhop caunterbury exyled englōde hym came erle arūdell ſone heyre whiche kepyng ſyr iohn̄ ſhelly knyght ſomtyme erle hūtindon duke exceſtre whyche tho caſtell reygate soutſex ſtale hym waye came calays keped well worthely tyll theſe two lordes comen calays ¶and worthy duke ſyr thomas arundell archebyſſhop caunterbury ſhypped hauen calais drewe theyr cours norwarde aryued yorke ſhyre rauenſporne faſte wydlyngton came en • red fyrſte londe two lordes hym theyr nauye ſo moche people reame whan herde comynge knewen anone drewen vnto hym welcomed theſe lordes ſoo gaaf theym courage manere thynge ſo paſſed forthe londe gadred moche people ¶and whan kyng rycharde hede wyſte theſe twoo lordes comen ayen englond alſo lō ded kynge lefte ordynaunce irlonde come englond warde haſte myght come caſtell flynte abode take counſeyl myghte done hym come none thanne ſyr thomas percy erle worcheſtre kynges ſtewarde wiſt knewe anone came halle amonges people brake yerde ryall kynges houſholde anone euery man dyſparple wente hys waye forſoke theyr mayſter ſouerayne lord lefte hym allone thus kynge rycharde broughte downe deſtroyed ſtode hymſelf allone wythout comforth ſocoure yf ony good counſeyll ony mā ala pyte ryall kynge anone came worde ſyre henry bolyngbroke vp ſtronge powre people ſquyres englonde reyſon vp ſhyres ſtrenthynge hym ayenſt kyng rycharde ¶and thus ſone come north countre bryſtowe met ſyr wyllyam • rope erle wyltſhyre treſourer englonde ſyr iohn̄ buſſhe ſyr henry grene iohn̄ bagot eſcaped frome theym wente ouer ſee irlonde ſethre knyghtes taken theyr hedes ſmytē thus dyed theyr fals couetoyſe ¶and kynge rycharde taken brought vnto ye duke anone duke put hym faſt warde ſtronge holde vnto hys cominge london rumore london ſtronge noyſe kynge rycharde came weſtmynſter peple london ranne thyder wolde haue done moche harme hurte woodneſſe myyer alder men worthy mē ceſſed wt fayr wordes torned theym home agayne vnto lōdon syr iohan slacke dene ye kynges chapell weſtmynſter taken broughte london put pryſon ludgate iohan bagot taken irlonde ſo brought london put pryſon newgate kepte abyde hys anſwere ¶and ſoone duke brought kynge rycharde pryuely vnto london put hym toure vnder ſure kepynge pryſoner came lordes reame theyr counſeyll vnto toure kynge rycharde ſayd hym myſgouernaun • e extorcyon hadde done made ordeyned opreſſe comyne peple alſo reame wherfore comyne people reame wolde hym haue depoſed kyngdom· ſo depoſed tyme toure london lordes counſeyll comune aſſent alle reame put frome toure vnto caſtell lede kente ther kepte whyle thanne frome then vnto caſtell pounfret north countree kepte myghtely togoder laſte knyght ouer come clerke made hym yelde hym recreaunt fals enpechement ſayd hym dyſpoyled armure drawen oute ye felde tybu • ne hangyed knyght taken grace good man ¶and ſame yere wente ſee wyth many ryall ſhyppes full well arayed enparelled enarmed wyth many good man armes arch good defence warre kynges name englonde ſoo londed laſte coſte brytayne yle bryak alle folke dured xv wekes longe ¶and x yere kynge henryes regne fourthe came soneſchall henaude menye englonde ſeke auentures gete hym worſhyp dedes armes bothe horſback foot att maner poyntes war • e ¶and ſeneſchal chalenged erle somerſet erle delyuered hym full manfully chalenges put aduerſary vnto worſt poyntes wāne hym grete worſhyp degre felde next day came felde man armes seneſchals partye ayenſt hym came ſyr rycharde arundell knyght henaude better hym foot poynte brought hym knee thyrde daye come man armer felde ayenſt hym trere came ſyr iohn̄ corne waylle knyghte manly knyghtly quyte hym mane poyntes ayenſte aduerſary better felde fourth daye came nother man armes henaude felde ayenſte hym came ſyr iohn̄ chaynes ſone manly quyte hym ayenſte aduerſary caſte hors man felde kyng manhode tyme dubbed hym knyght fyfte day came man armes henaudes partye felde hym came syr iohan ſtewarde knyght manfully quyt hym maner poyntes better ſyxte daye came henaunde hym came wyllyam porter ſquyre manfully quyte hym better ye felde kynge dubbed hym knyght ſame tyme ſeuenthe day came man armes henaude felde hym came iohan ſtandiſſhe ſquyre manfully quyte hym aduerſarye better hym felde kynge dubbyd hym knyghte ſame daye ſame daye came man armes henaude hym came ſquyre gaſcoyne proudely manly quyte hym hys aduerſary better hym felde anone kynge dubbed hym knyght ¶and viii daye came felde two men armes henaude wyth mette two ſouldyours calays whiche two bretheren called burghes well manly quyte ſelfe vpon theyr aduerſaryes haddē better theym felde thus ended theſe chalenges wyth many grete lordſhyppes thenne kynge att reuerēce theſe worthy ſtraungers made greate feeſt gaafe vnto theym many grete ryche gyftes thenne toke theyr leue went home ayē theyr owne countree ¶and xi yere kynge henryes regne fourthe grete batayl doo ſmythfelde bytwene two ſquyres one called glouceſtre parlement arthur defendaunte well manly foughten togyder longe tyme kyng theyr manfulneſſe grace toke kynge henryes ſone wedded counteſſe somerſette ¶and ſame yere cam ye embaſſatours fraunce englonde frome duke burgoyne vnto prynce englonde kynge henryes ſone heyre haue helpe ſocour men armes archer brydge sem • clowe ſlewe moch • people frenſſhmen arbalaſters remenaunte fledde wolde lenger abyde englyſſhmē came ayen parys toke theyr leue duke came ayen englonde ſaufte duke gaafe grete gyftes ſone iohn̄ duke bedforde hys ſone humfrey duke glouceſtre syr thomas beauferd erle dorſet duke awe marle made duke yorke thā kynge ordeyned ſone ſyr thomas duke clarence thomas beauforde erle dorſet normandye londed hogges mette theym lorde hambe theyr londynge wyth vii thouſande men armes frenſſhmen thre serge auntes armes put flyght taken theym ·vii hondred men armes iiii hondred horſes tho xiiii yere kyng henryes regne fourth lete make galays warre hoped haue paſſed grete ſee ſo forth iheruſalem haue ended hys lyf god vyſyted hym ſo ſoone infyrmytees grete ſekeneſſe yt myght well endure whyle ſo feruently taken brought bedde weſtmynſter fayre thambre laye hed aſked hys chāberlayll called chambre laye anſwered ſayd iheruſalem ſayde prophecye ſayd yt ſhold make ende deye iheruſalē caunterburyes ſhryne thus ended worthy kynge henry mydlente ſondaye yere oure lorde mcccc xxi vppon whoos ſoule god haue mercy amen martyn v pope iohn̄ xiii yere man choſen counſeyll conſtantynoble peaſyble ye deth martyn man doubted pope ſoon expulſed frome rome ſo fledde naked alſo cyted counſeyll baſylyens depoſed dyſcharged hym begā ſtryffe ayen whiche ſtode deth thoſe yt fauoured hym ſayde god haue mercy amen ¶and ſame yere certayne lollers taken fals herytykes purpoſed thrugh fals treaſon haue ſlayne oure kyng haue deſtroyed clargye reame myghte haue theyr fals purpoſe lorde god wolde ſuffre haſte kynge hadde warnynge therof alle theyr fals ordynaunce werkinge came ſodenly power saynt iohans withoute ſmythfelde anone toke certanye lollers fals herytykes broughte kynges preſence tolde fals purpoſe ordynaunce howe wolde haue doo wrought yf myghte haue regned hadde theyr wyll tolde whyche theyr capytayens gouernours ye kynge commaunded theym towre london thanne toke moo theym bothe within cytye wythoute ſente newgate bothe counteers thanne broughte examycyon clergye kynges iuſtyces conuycted theyr fals hereſie dampned iuſtyce theyr fals treaſon ¶and theyr iugement ſholde drawen frome towr london saynt gelys felde hanged brente galowes ¶and taken ſyr roger acton knyghte hereſye eke treaſon ayenſte kynge reame came afore clergye conuy • te hereſye dampned iuſtyce drawen frome towre london thrughe cyte saynt gelys hanged brente ¶and ſeconde yere kynge henryes regne fyfthe helde counſeylle alle lordes reame atte weſtmynſter putte hym demaunde prayed beſought theyr goodneſſe theyr gode counſeyll wylle ſhewe hym touchynge tytle ryghte hadde normande gaſcoyne guyhen whiche kynge fraunce wythelde wrongfully vntyghte fully whyche hys aunceſtrees hym hadde trewe tytle conqueſt ryghte heretage whiche normandye gaſcoyn guyhen good kynge edwarde wyndeſore hys aunceſtres hym hadde holden theyr lyues tyme lordes gaaf hym counſeyl ſendde enbaſſatours vnto kynge fraunce hys counſeyll ſholde gyue vp vnto hym hys ryght herytage ſaye normandye gaſcoyne guyhen whiche predeceſſours hadde holden afore hym el wold wyn̄e wyth ſtrength ſwerde ſhorte tyme helpe almyghty god ¶and thanne dolphyn fraunce anſwered oure enbaſſatours ſayde thys manere kynge ouer yonge terder aege comak ony warre ayenſte hym lyke yet good warroure doo make ſuche aconqueſte vppon hym ſomwhat ſcorne dyſpyte ſente hym tonne fulle tenes balles bycauſe wolde haue ſom playe wyth alle hym lordes wolde come hym better thenne • mayntene ony warre ¶and thenne anone oure lordes werre enbaſſatours tooke theyr leue came englonde ayen tolde kynge hys counſeyll vngoodly anſwere dolphyn preſent ye whyche ſent kynge ¶and whan kynge herde theyr wordes anſwere dolphyn wōder ſore agreued ryght euyll apayed towarde frenſſhemen towarde kyng dolphyn thought auenge hym ſoone god wold ſende grace myght anōe lette make tenes balles dolphyn haſt myght grete gonſtones ye dolphin playe anone ye kynge ſente hys lordes helde grete counſeyll weſtmynſter tolde vnto anſwere yt dolphyn worthy preſē te ſent hym lordes playe kyng lordes accorded yt ſholde redy armes wyth ther pow • r beſt araye ſtuffe vytayll ye longed ſuche warryoure maner ordynaūce hauē southampton nombere ccc xx ſaylles felle greate dyſeaſe foule myſchef iii lordes whyche kynge truſted moche thrugh fals couetyſe purpoſed ymagyned kynges deth thought haue ſlayne hym bretherne taken ye ſee whiche thre lordes named thus ſyre rycharde erle chambrydge broder duke yorke ſeconde ſhe lorde scrop treſourer englonde thyrde ſyr thomas gray knyght north countre theſe thre lordes afore ſayd lucre money hadde made promeſſe vnto frenſſhmen haue ſlayne kynge henry fyfte alle brethern fals trayne ſodaynly ware god almyghty helde hys holy honde ouer ſaued theſe peryllous menye haue done thys receyued frenſſhemen myllyon golde openly knowen theyr fals treaſon al thre iuged vnto deth iugemēt ſholde laadde thrughe hampton withoute northgate heded thus ended theyr lyues thyr falſe couetyſe treaſon anone done kynge men ye made redy wente ſhyppes ſaylled forthe wyth fyften hondred ſhyppes aryued seyn kydecauſe vpon ladyes euen aſſumpcyon normādy wyth hys ordynaū ce ſo went forth harflet beſyeged towne alle aboute londe eke water ſent capytayne towne charged hym delyuer towne capytayne ſayd yt wolde delyuer hym none wolde hym yelde bad hym beſt kynge layd hys ordynaunce vnto twone ſaye gonne engynnes trypgettes ſhotten caſte att walles eke vnto towne caſte downe towres towne layd theym vnto erthe played att tenes wyth hys harde gon ſtones ¶and within towne whan ſhold playe theyr ſonges well awaye ala euer ſuche tenes balles made curſyd tho warre began tyme euer borne ¶and morne kyng dyd crye att euery gate towne euery man ſholde redy morne erly make aſſaute vnto ye towe wyllyam boucher iohan graunte wyth xii burgeys worthy men came kynge beſought hym hys ryall pryncehode power wythdrawe malyce deſtruccyon dyd beſought hym viii dayes reſpyce trewes yf ony reſcowe myghte come theym el yelde vp towne vnto hym wyth theyr goodes kyng ſent forthe capytayne kept remenaunt ſtyll hym ye lorde gaucort capytayn towne went forth royn al haſt vnto dolphyn helpe ſocour none ne man reſcowe dolphyn wold abyde thus capytayne come ayen vnto kynge yelded vp towne delyuered hym key bad hym go put frenſſhmen men woman chyldren ſtuff hys towne har • et wyth englyſſhe people kynge ſente englonde dyde crye euery good towne englonde crafty man wolde come thydes enhabyte hym towne ſholde haue houſe houſholde hym heyres euer ¶and ſoo tho wēte many dyuerſe marchauntes crafty men enhabyte theym ſtrength towne welcome ¶and whan kynge ſawe thys towne well ſtuffed vytayls mē worthy prince toke leue went calays warde londe frenſſhmē herd comyng thought haue ſtopped hym way ſhold paſſe waye haſt myght braken alle brydges ony paſſage hors man ſo moche myght man paſſe ouer ryuer nother horſe ne foot yf ſhold haue drowned therfore kynge people wente ſought thys waye ferre vp parys warde ther ryall power fraunce aſſembled redy gyue hym batayll dyſtroye alle people almyghte god hys guyde ſaued hym al menye defended hym hys enmyes power purpoſe thanked god ſaued ſo hys owne knyght kynge ryghtfull tytle ¶and kynge holdynge ſeyenge grete multytude nombre enmyes wythſtande way gyue hym batayll kynge wyth meke herte good ſpyryte lyft vp hondes almyghty god ſouhht hym hys helpe ſocoure daye ſaue trewe ſeruauntes oure kynge gadred lordes peple bad gode ſholde haue fayre daye gracyous vyctorye better theyr enemyes prayed thē alle make redy vnto batayll wolde rather deed daye felde taken enmyes wold neuer put reame englonde raumſome perſone ¶an duke yorke fell hys knee beſought ye kynge aboue wolde graū te hym daye auauntwarde hys batayll kynge grauntyd hym hys aſkynge ſayd gramercy coſyn yorke praied hym make hym redy hadde euery man ordeyne hym ſtake tree ſharpe endes ye ſtake myght pyght erthe ſlope theyr enemyes ſholde ouercome horſback fals purpoſe arayed thē ouer ride enmye ſodaynly att fyrſte comynge fyrſte brunte nyght batayll frenſſhmen made many grete fyers moche reuyll howtynge • ſhowtynge playd kynge hys lordes dyſe archer alwaye blanke theyr money wēde yt bē theyrs morne aroſe daye ganne ſpynge kynge good auyſe lete araye hys batayll wynges charged euery mē kepe thē hoole togyder prayed alle good whan redy aſked tyme day ſayd pryme ſayd kynge good tyme englond prayed v therfore good chere lete v goo oure iourney ſayde wyth hyghe voys name almyghty god ſaynt george auaunce baner ſaynt george thys day thyn helpe ¶and frenſſhemen came pryckynge downe wold haue ouer ryden meny god oure archer made thē ryght ſone ſtomble archer ſhote neuer arowe amyſſe peryſſhed brought vnto ye groū de hors man ſhote day wager ſtakes made theym toppe ouer terue eche one ouer laye onhepes two hepes lenth hyghe kynge menye men armes archer ſthacked ſoo thycke arowes layd ſtaues kȳ ge wyth hōdes fought māly daye thus god almyghty ſaynt george brought oure enmyes groūde gaf v daye vyctory werre ſlayne frenſſhmen ye daye felde agyngcourt moo xi thouſand wyth pryſoners taken nombred daye frenſſhmē felde moo ſyr ſcore thouſande god daye faughte v came tydynges kynge new batayll frenſſhmen ordeyned redy ſtele hym came towardes hym anone oure kynge lette crye euery man ſholde doo ſlee hys pryſoners hadde taken anone make theym ayen redy fyghte wyth frenſſhe men whan ſaw men kylled downe theyr pryſoners dyde wythdrawe brake theyr batayll araye thus kynge worthy conquerour daye vyctory felde agyngcourte pycardye oure kynge retorne ayen batayll ſee people ſlayne englyſſhmen yf ony hurt myght holpen deed felde duke barrye ye duke alaūſome ye commodytes thā proceſſe tyme tooke hys leue kynge yode made knyght garter reteyned wered ye lyueray thanked kynge hys lordes kynge wente ouer ſee vnto calays aboden longe tyme haue anſwere frenſſhe puryfycacyō lady nexte graunted vnto hym mayntene warres ſpyrytualtee tēporalte hoole • dyeme anone kynge prayed hys lordes make redy ſtrengthe hym ryght anone lete make newe retenue charged al mē redy hampton wytſon weke next wyth ony delaye kynge made duke bedford protectour defender reame englōde hys abſence charged hym kepe hys lawes mayntene bothe ſpyrytuall temporall whan kynge thus ryall caſtell therin anone ſent heraudes capytayne charged hym delyuer towne caſtell el wolde gete theym ſtrenght honde anſwered ſayde toke none kepe ne none wolde delyuere vnto hym ſo anone layde ſyege vnto towne layde gonne euery ſyde caſte done bothe walles towres ſlewe moche people theyr houſes alſo ſtretes good duke clarence layde downe walles ſyde vnto ye bare groande ſo wyth whyle kynge counſeylle aſſauted towne anone duke clarence entred towe ſlewe downe ryght tyll came kynge ſpared nother man chylde euer cryed clarence clarence ſaint george deede walles kynges ſyde worthy mā called sprynges yt whiche ye kynge cōmaunded buryed abbaye canefaſt wyllyam conquerour who ſoule god huue mercy amen kynge came towe wyth hys broder duke clarence many worthy lordes wyth moche ſolemnyte myrthe ye kynge cōmaunded capytayne delyuer hym caſtell beſought ye kynge gyue hym xiiii dayes reſpyte yf ony reſcowe wolde come yf none wolde come delyuer hym keyes caſtell cōmaundement vnder comepoſycion ye towne caſtell bayou townes fortreſſes vyl • age nobre xiiii· vpon hylle fore caſtel cane kynge pyght tentes ſemed towne moche cane tyme came tydynges none reſowe wolde come ſo xiiii dayes ende capytayne caſtell came deliuered keyes caſtell kynge bayou xiiii townes delyuered vnto hym alſo anone kynge delyuered keyes duke clarence made hym capytayne bothe towne alſo caſtel made hym capytayne bayorus towny alſo ſo entred towne caſtell helde ſaint george feeſte made xv knyghtes bathe ſyr lowes robert ſalyn chaynye mougomerye many worthy men kynge cōmaunded put frenſſhemen woman man ſo hardy defoule woman ne take noo manere good awaye frome theym let paſſe pea payne dethe paſſed oute towne one daye moo xv hondred woman kynge lete ſtuffe towne caſtell englyſſhemen ordeyned twoo capytayns one ye towne caſtell ¶and charged theym vppon theyr lyues kepe well towne caſtell oure kyng wente then gate valeys newelyn layde aſyege chyrburgh ſeyge layde duke glouceſtre wyth ſtronge power myghty proceſſe tyme made ther capytayne ſame towne ¶and ſame tyme good eerle warwyk layed ſeyge vnto donnfronte gate put therin capteyne ſpeke eerle marche kynge ordeyned tho ſcomme ſee kepe coſtes englonde manere enmyes wynde roſe vppon theym wende haue bē loſte thorough grace almaghty god good gouernaunce rodden afore yle wyght ſtorme ther loſte two carackes twoo balyngers wyth marchaundyſe grete goodes al people within theym caracke broke vp hampton threwe maſte ouer walles towne ſaynt barthelomeus daye whan ſtorme ceſſed thys worthy erle marche toke ſhyppes wyth hys menye wente ſee londed normandye hogges ſo roden forth wardes ye kynge ¶and euer came frenſſhemen fledde came theym anthony pygge folowed hooſte alle waye tyll came grete water dradde haue drowned drenched water cloſed theym ſoo myghte noo gete oute ¶but laſte god almyghty thys anthony pygge broughte theym alle ſaufte oute caughte theym gyde knewe countree aboute brought theym thorough quycke sande ſo forthe ile alſo toke many pryſoners waye warde kynge theyr iourneye ſo men vnto caſtel cane kynge welcomed hym toke hys iourney atte argentun anone tho • yolden kynge theyr lyues wente theyr waye oure kynge remeued vnto ſtronge towne tho called ceſe fayer mynſter yelde vp anone vnto kynge thanne kynge wente then • laūſome wanne towne brydge kynge ſent erle warwyk towne called beleſme wyth grete ſtronge power anone yelde put al kynges grace hys mercy ſo dyde many ſtronge townes caſtels tho partyes then wente vernyll perche anone yolden vnto kynge bothe towne caſtell bodyes godes kynges good grace ſo kynge gate conquered townes caſtelles pyle ſtrengthes abbays vnto cyte rone ¶and fyfth yere kynge henryes regne fyfth ſyr iohan oldcaſtell ye lorde cobham areſted hereſie broughte vnto towre london anone afte brake towre wente wale kepte hym longe tyme att laſt lord powys toke hym ſtode att grete defence longe tyme ſoore wounded wolde taken ſoo lorde powys men brought hym wale vnto london agayne whyrlcole ſoo brought weſtmynſter examined certayne pointes put vppon hym ſayd naye ſo conuyte ye clargye hys hereſye dampned iuſtyces vnto dethe treaſon ladde toure ayen layde hurdell drawen thrugh cytye ſaynt gelys felde made newe payre galowes ſtronge coler yren hym hanged brēte galowes al leudeneſſe fals opynyons vi yere kynge henrye fyfth ſente hys vncle ſyr thomas beauforde duke exceſtre fayre menye mē armes archer cyte rone dyſpleyed baner ſente herodes vnto towne badde theym yelde cyte vnto kynge theyr lyege lorde ſayde tooke none kepe ne none ſholde haue yf dere bought meued theyr hondes anſwere wolde none gyue gonne ¶and duke toke gode ſemēt ye grounde anone yſſued cytee grette menye men armes bothe horſbacke foote anone menye mette wyth ouer trewe greate hepe takē ſlayne xxx perſones full ryght good mennys bodyes remenaunt fledde aien towne duke wente vnto pountlarge vnto kynge tolde hym al ſpedde howe lyked grounde ¶and anone duke gone caſte downe ſubarbes aboute cyte vnto harde grounde bycauſe kyng ſholde noo refuſynge vpon frydaye lammaſdaye thanne nexte folowynge onre kynge hoſte came rone anone ſete hys ſyege rounde cytye anone lete laye hys ordynaunce vnto towne kynge wyth hys lordes logded wythin chartre houſe grete ſtrengthe aboute theym eeſt partye cytee duke clarence lodged hym ſtrengthe power att weſte ende waſte abbaye proce chanx duke excheſtre menye northe ſyde porte beauueſyn bytwene duke clarence duke exceſtre erle marchall lodged wyth moche people ſtronge power caſtell gate ¶and thanne erle ormonde lorde haryngton alſo lorde talbott wyth theyr retenue companye next hym ¶and thanne syr iohan cornewayle manye othere noble knyghtes squyres name wyth theyr retenue laye wyth noble duke clarence ¶and thanne frome duke exceſtre towardes kynge lodged lorde roos lorde wylleby wyth lorde phehewe syre wyllyam porter knight theyr retenue porte saynt hyllary than̄e erle mortaye retenne lodged abbaye saynte katherynes ¶and erle saleſbury wyth hys retenue laye ſyde saynt katherynes syr iohan graye knyght lodged att abbaye called mounte du ſaynt mychel ſyr phylyp leche knyght kynges treſourer lodged bytwene water seyn abbaye kept warde vnder hylle baron carowe lodged vnder water ſyde kepe paſſage ienyco ſquyre laye nexte hym water ſyde theſe two ſquyres kept manly water ſeyn fought theyr enmyes oft tymes ſyde seyn laye ye erle hontyngdon maſter neuyll erles ſone weſtmer london ſyr gylbert vm • reuyll erle keme ſyr rycharde erle arundell lorde feryers wyth theyr retenue porte du poūte eche theſe lordes ſtronge ordynaūce kynge dyde make poūtlarge ouer water seyn ſtronge amyghty chayne iron put yt thrught grete pylis faſt pyght grounde wente ouer ryuer seyn veſſell myght paſſe yt kynde aboue chayn kynge lete make brydge ouer water seyn man hors caryage myght go fro tymes whā nede came ye erle warwyke goten doūfronte vnto kynge henry englonde anone kynge ſent erle warwyk cawdebeke ſeyge yt whan came towne ſente heraudes vnto capytayne badde hym yelde vp towne vpon payne dethe anone layde ſege capytayne beſought erle myght come vnto hys preſence pleaſed hym ſpeke wyth hym ſoo good erle graūted hym come came oute foure burgeys came wyth hym entreated ſoo wyth erle ſame towne vnder compoſycyon done cyte rome dyde erle graunted conſented tho • vpoon thys condycyon kynges nauye englonde wyth hys ordynaunce myghte paſſe theym ſaufte ony manere lette dyſturbaunce compoſycyon ſete theyr ſeales ſhyppes paſſed vp ſaufte came cytee rone hondred ſhyppes caſte theyr ankers thanne thys cyte beſyeged bothe londe water whan done ſhyppes comen vp came erle warwyke ayen kyng lodged hym bytwene abbaye ſaynt katherynes kyng tyll abbaye enteraced ſo yolden vnto kynge thanne remeued hym then lodged hym porte martenuylye tho erle salyſbury commaunded kynge make hym redy ryde came haſty tydynges made hym abyde ſoo retorned ayen lodged hym beſyde good erle huntyngdon tylle ſyege ended ¶and thenne came good duke glouceſtre kynges brother ſyege chyrbourghe whiche hadde goten ſtuffid agayne vnto kynges behoue profyte vnto crowne englond whan comen kynge rone lodged greate ordynaunce porte saynt hyllary nerer towne hys enmyes thenne ony laye xl roddes lenthe within ſhote quarell wyth hym laye erle southfolke lorde bergeyeney wyth hys retenue ſtronge ordynaunce manly proudly faughte euery day wyth theyr enmyes euer whan yſſued cyte ¶and thanne came pryoure kylmayne irlonde ouer ſee kynge wyth fayr meny armes theyr owne countree gyſe ſomme xvi hondred good mennys bodyes kyng welcomed theym made theym goode ¶and thanne came thydynges vnto kynge kynge fraūce dolphyn duke burgoyne wolde come downe reſcowe cyte rone ſtronge power manere nacyons breke ſyege caſteth hym entre northe ſyde hooſte cauſe beſte entrynge mooſt playne kynge aſſyned pryoure kylmayne wyth power lodged hym northe ſyde hoſte ſtoppe theyr paſſage foreſte lyon ordynaunce full gladde ſo went forthe haſte kepte grounde place kyng counſeyll aſſygned quyte good warryours vnto thyer kynge ¶now wyll tell whyche chyef capytayns gouernoure cytee rome monſyr • uy boteler cheyf capytayne bothe cyte caſtell mon ſyre teymygan capytayne porte canx mon ſyr de al roche capytayne dyſners mon ſyr anthony lyuetenaūt mon ſyr guy botyler henry chantfyen capytayne porte dela pounte· iohan materuas capytayne porte de la caſtell mon ſyr de preant capytayne porte saynt hyllary baſtarde tyne capytayn ye porte martenuylle graunt iakes worthy warryoure capytayne al mē warre wy gouernour outwarde horſbacke foot men armes whan yſſued cytee porte arayed al ſholde encountre menye eche capytayns ladde fyue thouſande men armes ſome moo fyrſte comynge kynge theyr nombred heroudes thre hundred thouſande mē womē chyldren yonge olde amonge theſe many man full man hondes ſo preued whan yſſued cytee horſbacke foot came neuer att one gate allone thre foure gate attē euery gate two thre thouſande good mennys bodyes armed manfully encoūtred englyſſmē moche people ſlayne dyuerſe tymes wyth gonne quarelles ordynaunce ſyege dured ·xx wekes euery towne truſted haue reſcowed cam none ſo att laſte kepte towne ſoo lange deyed many thouſādes within towne defaute mete men chyldren eten theyr horſes dogges cattes towne often tymes men armes drofe pore people att gate towne ſpendynge vytaylles anone englyſſhmen drofe theym towne ayen soo laſte capytayne towne ſawe myſchyef reſcowed alſo ſcarſyte vytaylle people deyed ſoo defaute meete euery daye many thouſandes alſo ſawe yonge chyldren lye ſouke theyr moders pappes deed ¶than anone ſente kynge beſechynge hym hys grace mercye broughte keyes towne vnto kynge delyuered towne hym al ſoudyours voyed towne theyr horſes harnes comunes towne abyde dwelle ſtyll towne yerely paye hym hys ſucceſſours alle manere cuſtomes ſee fermes katerenes kyng entred towne reſted hym caſtell tyll ye wne ſette rule gouernaunce ¶how kynge englond made enheyrytoure regente fraūce wedded quene katheryne anone rone goten depe manye townes baſſe normandye gaf ouer without ſtroke ſyege whan vnderſtode kynge goten rone alſo yere pea made ſworne bytwene duke bugoyne dolphyn whiche ſworne goddes body ſholde loue aſſyſſe eche ayenſt theyr enemyes contrary othe duke iohn̄ burgoyne ſlayne pyteouſly murdred preſence dolphyn wherfore frenſſhmen gretly deuydeb neceſſyte laboured haue treatye wyth kynge englonde kynge englonde wanne dayely townes caſtels▪ fortreſſes ¶alſo thys ſame yere quene iane areſted brought vnto caſtell lede kent one • rere radulfe doctour dyuynyte confeſſour whyche afterwarde ſlayne perſoone toure fallynge wordes debate warde quene iane delyuered ¶and vii yere kynge fraū ce englonde accorded kynge henry made heyre regent fraunce wedded dame katheryne doughter fraunce troyes champayne▪ trynyte ſondaye made menne phylyp newe made duke burgoyne whiche ſworne kynge henry auenge hys faders deth become englyſſh ¶and thanne kynge wyth hys newe wyfe wente parys ryall • receyued then wente wyth lordes duke bourgoyn many lordes fraunce layd ſyege dyuerſe townes caſtels helde dolphyns partye wanne towne milon helde longe tyme therin good defender viii yere kyng quene came ouer ſee londed landelmaſſe daye morne att douer xiiii daye feuerer kynge came london ye xxi daye ſame monthe quene came xxiiii ſame ſhe crowned weſtmynſter ¶alſo ſame yere anone eſter kyng helde palement weſtmynſter whiche parlemente ordeyned golde englyſſhe coyn ſholde weyed none receyued weyght • nd anone wytſontyde kynge ſaylled calays paſſed forth ſo fraūce xxii daye marche kyng came ouer duke clarence ſlayne fraunce dyuerſe lordes taken pryſoners erle huntyngdon erle somerſet dyuerſe bycauſe wold taken none archer thoughte haue ouercome frenſſhemen themſelf without archer yet whan ſlayne archer came reſcowed ye body duke whiche wolde haue caryed god haue mercye ſoule valyaunte man ſame yere bytwene cryſtmaſſe cādelmaſſe towne mylon yolden vnto kynge ¶in ii yere ſaynt nycholas daye decembre borne henry kynges fyrſte begoten ſone wyndeſore who god faders font ſtone ſyr henry byſſhop wyncheſtre iohn̄ duke bedford ducheſſe holonde godmoder henry chychelay archebyſſhop caūterbury god fader confermynge ¶and x yere ye cyte mew bry goten whiche ben longe beſyeged ſame yere quene ſhypped hampon ſayled ouer kynge fraunce ſhe worſhypfully receyued kynge alſo kyng fraynce hyr fader hyr moder thus kynge henry wanne faſte fraunce helde grete aſtate ſate greate feeſt parys crowned ye quene alſo whiche hadde ſeen alle people reſorted vnto courte kynge fraunce helde none aſtate ne rule lefte almooſt allone ¶alſo yere weder toke ſete vpon poules ſteple london yere monethe auguſt kynge waxed ſeke boy devyncynt whan ſawe ſholde deye made hys teſtamēt ordeyned many noble thynges hys ſoule deuoutly receyued ryghtes holy chyrche ſoo ferre whanne anoynted ſayde ſeruyſe preeſt ye verſe ſpalme miſerere mei deus benigne fac dn̄e bona voluntate tuaſyon vt edificentur mury iheruſalem badde tarye ſayd thus good lorde thou knoweſt myn entente hathe ben yet yf myght lyue redyfye walles iheruſalem thanne preeſt proceded forth made anende anone thys mooſte noble prynce dyctoryous kynge floure hys tyme cryſten chyualrye whome worlde doubted gaaf hys ſoule handes god deyed made en de naturall lyfe att ſayde boy de vyncent beſyde parys ye xxxvi yere hys aege vppon whoos ſowle god haue mercy amen ¶than body enbamed cyred layd ryall chare ymage lyke hym layde vpvon corp open wyth dyuerſe baners horſes couered rychely armes englonde fraunce alſo olde armes ſaynt edwarde ſaynt edmonde grete multytude torch whome wente kynge scotlonde many lordes whyche accompanyed body tyll came vnto weſtmynſter london englonde euery towne waye ſolempnely dyryge euē maſſe morne moche almes gyuen poore peple ye waye vii daye nouembre ye corp brought thrugh london wyth grete reuerēce ſolempnyte weſtmynſter nowe lyeth worſhypfully buryed layd tombe ryal ymage lyke hȳſelf ſyluer gylde made att coſt quene katheryne thus ended entered buryed noble kyng hē ry ye fyfth vpon whoos ſoule al cryſtē ſoules god haue mercy amē ¶of ye lawe kynge hēry ye fyfth ordeyned kyng rycharde hymſelf dethe noted kynge henry fyfth noble prynce kynge crowned hys yo • gth wylde recheles ſpared noo thynge hys luſt ne deſyres accōpleſſhed lykyng ſoone crowned enoynted ſacred anone ſodaynly chaunged newe man ſet entent lyue vertuouſly mayntenynge holy chyrche deſtroyenge heretykes kepynge iuſtyce defendynge reame ſubgettes ¶and moche hys fader depoſed hys labour good kyng rycharde pyteouſly made hym deye offence done hym ayenſt legaunce ſent rome aſſoyled therof whiche offēce holy fader ye pope enyoyned hym make hym prayed perpetually lyke done takē hym naturall lyf therfore ſhold fyſide four taper brēne perpetually body extynccōn bodely lyf ſoule may euer remembred lyf heuē ſpyrytual lyfe alſo ſholde euery weke ye daye come aaboute hys deth haue ſolempne maſſe requiē ye euē afore dyryge wyth ix leſſons doole poore peple alwaye daye xi ſhellynges vii pen deled peny mele one yere annyuerſary termēte holden ye moſt honeſt wyſe • bedeled ye daye xx poūde pen poore people euery monke xx ſhellynge whyche alle theſe thynhes performed thys noble kynge fader kyng henry fourth fader performed durynge hys lyf whome ſayd god dyd touche hym lepreor deyed ¶and alſo thys noble prynce lette calle ye abbottes pryours ſaynte benet order englond chapytre hous weſtmynſter reformacyon theyr order wherin comunycacyon alſo wyth byſſhops mē ſpyrytualte ſo ferre forth doubted ſore wold haue temporaltes theyr hondes wherfore aduyſe labour procurynge ſpyrytuallyte encouraged kyng chalenge normandye ryght fraunce entente ſet hym warke ſhold ſeke none occaſyons entre ſuche mater lyf tyme afterwarde laboured beſy warre conquerynge grete parte reame fraunce ſo afterwarde yt grement kynge charles gouernaunce rule reame fraunce proclamed regnet heyre fraunce ¶and ſo notwithſtandynge alle grete warre neuertheles yet remēbred ſoule alſo thought mortall nedes muſt deye whyche cauſe ordeyned hys lyfe tyme place ſepulture buryed hath euery daye thre maſſes perpetually ſongen chapell ſepultur whiche ye myddyll maſſe fyrſte laſte maſſe ſhall aſſygned hym apperyeth theſe verſes folowynge henrici miſſe quinti ſunt hic tabulate que ſucceſſiue ſunt per monachos celebrate ¶de dm̄ca prima ſit aſſumpre de feſto virginis alme poſcit poſtremā criſtus de morte reſurgens ¶feria ſecunda prima ſalute de feſto virginis extat nunciat angelicis laudē poſtrema choreis ¶feria tercia eſſe deum natum de virgine prima fatetur cōmemorat natam ſic vicima miſſe mariam ¶feria quarta prima celebretur ad honorē neupmatꝭ almi vltima conceptam denunciat • ē mariam ¶feria quinta semper prima colideber de corpere criſti vltima ſit facta de virgine purificata ¶feria ſexta concedet vt prima celebretur de truce ſanctā que ſalutate f • et poſtrema maria ¶sabbato omnes ad ſanctos eſt prima coleda ſuper no vltima de requie pro defunctis petit eſſe semper erit medium de proprietate • ci ¶and yet noble kynge henry fyfte founded twoo houſes relygyon called syon beſyde braynforde ye ordre saynt brygf • te mē woman ſyde ryuer tamyſe hows monkes chartrehous whyche twoo place contynually prayed nyght daye euer whan syon reſten chaptre hous theyr ſeruyce lyke wyſe whan chartre hous reſten gooth ryngynge belle eyther place eche knoweth whan haue ended theyr ſeruyte whyche nobly endowed dayly grete almes dedes charter hous certayne chyldren founde ſcole syon certayn almes geuen dayly yet beſyde thys founde recluſe whyche ſhall alway preeſt praye hym ſayd chartre hous whyche preeſt ſuffycyently endowed hym ſeruaunt lo may prynces take enſample thys noble prynce regned ſo lytyll tyme fully x yere dyde ſo many noble actes well ſoule perpetually remembred prayed conqueſtes beynge moſte luſty aege dyſpoſyd eſchewe ſynne grete iuſticer • ſo moche yt prynces cryſtendome dradde hym alſo hethenes determyned hymſelf yf god wolde haue ſpared hym haue warred saraſyns knowe ayde prynces alle paſſages ye iourneye ſente knyght henaude named hugh de lanoye vnto iheruſalem retorned deyed boy de vencence xxxvi yere hys aege who ſoule god iohan norman choſē mayer london daye ſholde take hys othe att weſtmynſter wente thyder water wyth alle craftes afore tyme tho mayer alderme craftes rode horſbacke whiche neuer vſyd ſyn tyme haue euer pea departe concluſyon • e treated one ſyde erle warwyk marche men entred twone ſyde fought ayenſt kynge party ſo began batayll fyghtinge whiche endured greate whyle concluſyon duke yorke obteyned anone grete parlemēt london whiche parlement duke yerke made protectour englōde erle warwyk capytayne calays erle salyſbury chaunceler englonde ſuche perſones rule aboute kynge ſet parte myght rule dyd ¶and ſame yere deyed pope nycholas ye fyfte hym calixt thyrde calixt catalane actes hym ſhal ſhewed folowynge· ¶in ſame yere fell grete affraye lōdon ayēſt lūbardes cauſe begā bycauſe yonge man toke dager frome lūbarde brake wherfore yōge mā morne ſēte fore come mayer aldermē offēce cōmytted warde thēne ye mayer departed fro yelde halle goo home dyner chepe yonge mē mercerye mooſt partye prentyſes helde mayre shyrefs ſtyl chepe wolde ſuffre theym departe vnto tyme theyr felowe whyche commytted warde delyuered ſo force reſcowed theyr felowe pryſon done mayre departed shrefes alſo pryſoner deliuered whiche yf put pryſon ieoperdye lyfe thene began rumoure cyte ayenſt lōbardes ſame euenynge ye hond crafty men towne aroſe rāne lumbardes houſes dyſpoyled robbed dyuers wherfore mayre alderman came honeſt people cyte droue then ſente ſome theym ſtolen newgate ¶and yonge man reſcowed felowes ſawe greate rumoure affraye robbed enſewed hys fyrſte meuynge lumbarde departyd wente weſtmynſter ſaynt wary elles hadde coſte hym hys lyfe anone came downe oyer determyne iuſtyce theym ſo rebelled cytee ayenſte lumbardes whyche ſatte wyth mayre tyme wyllyam marowe duke bokyngham many lordes ſe execucyon done comynes cytee ſecretely made redy dyde arme theyr howſes purpoos haue rongen comyne belle whiche called bowe belle lete ſyde men whiche came ye knowlege duke bokyngham lordes ¶and contynente aroſe durſte noo lenger abyde dowted hole cyte ſholde haue ryſen ayenſt theym yet neuerthels two thre cyte iuged dethe robbery hangyd tyborne ¶and anone kynge quene lordes rode couētre withdrewe theym fro london cauſe lytyll duke yorke ſent grenewych dyſchargyd protectourſhyppe erle salyſbury chaūchelerſhyppe thys ſente fore preuy ſeale come couētre almooſt diſceyued erle warwyke alſo ſhold haue ben dyſtroyed yf ſeen well ¶how lorde egremōde take ye erle salyſbury ſōes ye robbynge sandwytche yere taken four grete fyſſhes bytwene ereth london one called mors maryne ſeconde ſwerde fyſſhe two whalys ſame yere certayne affrayes done ī northe coūtre bytwene lord egremōde erle salyſbury ſones ye ſayd lord egremond whō cōdempned grete ſom̄e money ye ſayd erle salyſbury therfore cōmytted pryſon newegate london whan certayne ſpace brake pryſon thre pryſoners hym eſcaped wēt waye alſo yere erle warwyk wyf wēt calays fayre feliſſhyp toke poſſeſſyon offyce tyme grete reformacōn many moneſteryes relygyō dyuerſe partyes worlde wiche refourmed fyrſt inſtytutycyon cōtynued many place ¶this ſame yere greate batayll march bytwene londe hūgry turkey place called septedrad innumerable turkes ſlayne bi myracle than̄e mānes honde oonly honde god ſmote theym ſaynt iohan capyſtrane preſēce prouokyd criſtē people beynge thēne aferde purſue ye turkys infynyte multytude ſlayne dyſtryed turkys ſayd yt grete nōbre armyd mē folowed thē aferde turne ayen holy angelles ſame yere pryſoners newgate londō brake theyr pryſon went vpon ſedes fought ayēſt theym cytee kepe gate longe whyle att laſte towne gate pryſon theym then̄e ſore punyſſhed enſample ¶in yere alſo grete erthquake naples ſo moche peryſſhed xl thouſande people ſanke erthe ¶alſo xxxvi yere ſaynt oſmonde ſōtyme byſſhop salyſbury canonyſed att rome pope calyſt x daye iuly tranſlated salyſbury biſſhop caūterbury many byſſhoppes ¶and auguſt ſyr pers de braſay ſeneſchal normādye capytayne depe many capytayns mē werre went thee ſee greate nauy downes nyght erly day londed sandwytche bothe bi lōde water toke towne ryfled diſpoyled toke many pryſoners lefte towne bare whyche ryche place moche good therin ladde wyth many ryche pryſoners ſame yere many place fraunce almayne flaunders holonde zeelonde chyldren gadred theym togyder greate companyes goo pylgrymage ſaynt myghels moūte normādye whiche came fro ferre coūtrees wherof people merueyled many ſuppoſed ſome wyckyd ſpyryte meued doo ſo dured longe cauſe longe waye alſo lac vytaylle wente croſſe ¶and ye haue herde certayne lordes ſlayne atte saynt albons wherfore alwaye grutchynge wrath hadde heyres ſoo ſlayne ayenſt duke yorke erles wa • wyk salyſbury wherfore kyng aduys counſeyll ſente theym vnto london whyche place duke yorke came xxvi daye ianueri four honderd men lodged hym atte baynerdes caſtell hys owne place ¶and iv daye ianuer came erle salyſbury fyue hundred men lodged therber owne place ¶and then̄e came duke excetre somerſet viiic men laye withoute temple barre ¶and erle northumberlonde lorde egremonde lorde clyfforde wyth xv hundred men lodged without towne ¶and mayer tyme geffraye boloyne kept grete watche comyns cyte rode cytee holborne fleteſtrete v thouſand men well arayed armyd kepe pea ¶and xiiii daye feuerer erle warwyke came london fro calays well beſeen worſhypfully v hundred men red iakettes broudred wyth ragged ſtaffe behynde lodged graye freres ¶and xv daye marche kynge came london quene ther accorded pea made amonge lordes ſette pea lady daye xxv daye marche yere oure lorde mcccclviii· kynge quene lordes went proceſſyon poules london anone kyng lordes departed yere grete fraye fletſtrete bytwene mē courte men ſame ſtrete whyche fayre quenes attourney ſlayne ¶howe kynges houſholde made fraye ayenſte erle warwyke iourneye bloreheth alſo ſame yere erle warwyk counſeyll weſtmynſter alle kynges houſholde meny gadred togyder haue ſlayne ſayde erle helpe god frendes recouered barge eſcapyd theyr euyll enterpryſe well coke came rennynge oute wyth ſpytes peſtels ayneh hym ſame daye rode wardes werwyk ſoone gate hym commyſſyon went ouer ſee warde calays ¶soone thys therle salyſbury comynge lōdon encoūtred bloreheth lord audley moche people ordeyned dyſtroy hym hauynge knowlege ſhold met wyth accōpanyed hys two ſones ſyr thomas ſyr iohn̄ neuell grete felyſhyp goodman ſo faught togyder erle salyſbury wanne ye felde lorde audley ſlayne many gentylmen cheſſhyre moche people hurt erles two ſones hurte goynge homewarde afterwarde taken hadde cheſtre quenes menye ¶after calixt pius pope chaſe yere mcccclvlii· callyd eneas eloquēte man poete laureate embaſſatour ye emperours tyme wrote ye coūſeyl baſyle noble treatyſe thactoryte ye ſame alſo canonyſed ſaynte katheryne senys thys pope ordeyned grete indulgēce pardonne theym wolde go werre ayēſt turke wrote pyſtle greate turke exhortynge hym become cryſten thend ordeyned paſſage ayēſt turke ankon whiche moche people drewe partyes criſtēdome whiche people ſente many home ayen cauſe ſuffyced anone dyed ſayd ankō yere lord mcccclxiii xiiii daye auguſt ¶how andrewe trollop ſouldyours calays forſoke ye duke yorke theyr mayſter therle warwyk weſte countre duke yorke erles warwyk salyſbury ſawe gouernaū ce reame ſtode mooſt quene hyr counſeyll grete prynces londe callyd counſeyl ſet parte ſoo ſayd thrugh reame tho ſayd lordes ſholde dyſtroyed openly ſhewed blorehethe yt wolde haue ſlayne erle salyſbury thenne ſauacyon theyr lyues alſo comynwele reame thought remedy thyſe thynges aſſembled togyder moche people toke felde weſt countre whiche erle warwyk came fro calays many olde souldeyours andrē trollop whoſe wyſdome ye werre truſtyd moche vpon whan thus aſſembled made theyr felde kynge ſente commyſſyons preuy ſeales vnto lordes reame come wayte hym theyr mooſt beſte defenſable araye ſo euery man came ſuche wyſe kynge ſtronger hadde more▪ peple duke yorke therles warwyk salyſbury notyd euery lorde englonde tyme durſt dyſobeye quene ſo ſhe rulyd peaſybly done abowte kynge whiche good well dyſpoſed man thenne whan kynge come place duke yorke hys felyſſhyp made theyr felde ſtrongeſt wyſe purpoſyd verely abyde haue fouȝte nyghte andrewe trollop olde ſoudyours calays wyth greate felyſhyp ſodeynly departyd duke hoſt wente ſtrayte vnto kynges felde receiued ioyouſly knewe thentent thother lordes alſo maner theyr felde duke yorke lordes ſeynge thē dyſceued toke counſeylle ſhortly ſame nyght departed frome felde leuynge behynde thē mooſt partye theyr people kepe felde tyl morowe duke yorke ſecō de ſone departyd thrugh wale towarde irlonde leuynge eldeſt ſone erle marche erles werwyk salyſbury whiche rode togyder wyth thre foure perſones ſtrayght deuenſhyre helpe ayde one denham gate ſhyp whiche coſt xi ſcore noble wyth ſame ſhyp ſayled fro then gerneſey refreſſhed theym frome then ſayled calays receyued caſtel ye poſtern̄ ye towne wyſt duke yorke toke ſhypynge walys ſayled ouer irlonde well receyued ¶how erles marche warwyk salyſbury entred calays erle warwyk wence irlonde kynge henry wyth hoſt felde knowynge ſodeyne departynge morowe foūde none felde ſayd lordes ſent haſt mē folowe purſue take thē mette thē god wolde thē kynge wēt ludlowe dyſpoyled ye caſtel towne ſēte ducheſſe yorke hyr chyldrē ducheſſe bokyngham hyr ſyſter ſhe kepte longe tyme forth kynge ordeyned duke somerſet capytayne calays thyſe lordes ſo departed afore ſayd preclamyd rebelles grete traytours duke somerſet tooke hym al ſoudyours departed fro felde made hȳ redy haſte go calays take poſſeſſyon offyce whan came founde therle warwyk therin capytayne erles marche salyſbury alſo then̄e londed scalys wēt gyues receyued fortuned ſome tho ſhyppes came ouer hym came calays hauē theyr fre wyll ſhypmē ought fauour erle warwyk thā duke somerſet whyche ſhyppes take dyuerſe mē ienyn fynkyll iohan felowe kaylles purſer whiche beheded ſoone calays came mē dayly ouer ye ſee thyſe lordes calays began wexe ſtrōger borowed moche gode staple ſyde duke somerſet beynge gynes gate people hym whiche came ſcarmyſſhed theym calays calays whiche endured many day • ucyng moche people came ouer dayly vnto thiſe lordes ¶thē tyme thaduys coūſeylle lordes att calays ſente ouer mayſter denham greate felyſhyp sandwhyche whiche tooke towne therin lorde ryuers lorde • alys ſone toke many ſhyppes hauen broughte calays wyth whiche ſhyppes many maryners ther fre wyl came calays ſerue erle warwyk erle warwyke aduys lordes tooke ſhyppes manned theym well ſaylled hymſelfe irlonde ſpeke wyth duke yorke tooke aduys ſholde entre englonde whan done hys erandes retorned ayen towardes calays broughte hym moder counteſſe salyſbury fauour ye erle warwyk thā hym departed came calays ſauf • e ¶thē kynges coūſeyll ſeynge yt thyſe lordꝭ goten thoſe ſhyppes fro sandwytche taken lorde ryuers ſone ordeyned garyſon sandwytche abyde ix brought capytayne ouer ſee ſmote hys heed yet 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page duplicate〉 daylymen came ouer theim fro partyes ¶how erle marche warwyke salyſbury entred englōd ye feld northāptō dyuerſe lordes ſlayne thys forſayd erles marche warwyke salyſbury came ouer douer moche people londed whome coūtre drewe came lōdon armyd lete lordes kynges counſell knowe theyr truth alſo theyr entente aſſembled theym tolde entended harme ye kynges perſone ſauf wolde put hym ſuche perſones aboute hym ſoo departed frome london wyth greate puyſſaunce towarde northampton kynge accompanyed many lordes made ſtronge felde withoute towne bothe partyes met fought greate batayll whyche batayll ſlayne duke bokyngham therle shreweſbury ye vycoūt beamonde lorde egremonde many knyghtes ſquyres othere alſo kynge hymſelf taken felde warde broughte london anone parlement weſtm̄ duryng whyche parlyament ye duke yorke came irlonde wyth erle rutlande rydynge wyth grete felyſhyp palays come parlyament chambre toke kynges place claymed crowne propre enherytaunce ryght caſte forth wryttynge tytele alſo ryghtfull heyre wherfore moche concluſyon yt appoynted concluded kinge henry ſholde regne kynge durynge natural lyfe moche hadde kynge ſo longe poſſeſſyd aft dethe duke yorke ſhold kynge hys heyers kynges hym forth ſholde ꝓclamed heyre apparaūt ſhold alſo protector regence englonde duryng ye kynges lyfe wyth many thyngꝭ ordeyned ſame parliment yf kynge henry durynge hys lyfe wence frome thys poyntement ony artycle concludyd ſayd paylyament ſholde depoſed duke ſholde take crowne kynge whyche thynges enacted thauctoryte ſame whiche parlyament comyn • reame beyng aſſembled comyn hons cōmynyng treatyng vpon tytle forſayd duke yorke ſodenly feldone crowne whiche henge thenne middes ſayde hous whiche frayter ye abbaye weſtm̄ whiche takē prodice tokē regne kynge henry endyd ¶and alſo crowne whiche ſtode hygheſt toure ſtyple caſtel douer fell downe ſame yere ¶how duke yorke ſlayne felde wakefelde ſeconde iourneye ſaynt albōs ye quenē prince bicauſe quene wyth prynce ſone northe abſent fro kynge obeyed ſuche thyngꝭ concluded parlement ordeyned ye duke yorke ꝓtector ſhold go north ward brynge quene ſubdue ſuche wolne obey wyth whome wente erle ſalyſbury syr thomas neuyll hys ſone moche people wakefelde cryſtmas weke ouerthrowe ſlayne lordes quenes party wyte duke yorke ſlayne erle rotlonde ſyr thomas neuyll many moo eerle salyſbury take other· iohan horowe london capytayne ruler fotmen haūſon hull whiche brought poūfret heeded heedes ſente yorke ſette vpon yates thus noble prynce ſlayne duke yorke who ſoule god haue mercy thys tyme therle marche beyng shorweſbury herynge deth fader deſyred ayde towne auenge faders dethe frothens wente walys candelmaſſe battayll martymers croſſe ayenſte therle penbroke wylſhyre erle marche vyctorye quene thoſe lordes north dyſtreſſyd ſlayne duke yorke felyſſhyp came ſouth warde grete multytude people come kynge defecte ſuche concluſyons take parlyamēt ayenſt who comyng duke northfolke ye erle warwyeke wyth moche people ordynaunce wente ſaynt albons ladde kynge henry wyth theym encoūtred gyder ſuche wyſe faught ſo duke northfolke therle werwyke wyth many ther party •• edde loſte iourneye kynge hēry takē quene prynce edwarde ſone whiche two got felde quene hyr partye beynge aboue ſēte anone lōdon whyche aſſhe weneſdaye fyrſt daye lente vytayl ¶for whiche mayre ordeyned bi thaduys aldermē ye certen carte lade wyth vytayll ſholde ſente ſaynt albons thē whā tho carte came crepell yate ye comīs cyte kept ye gate toke vytayles fro carte wolde ſuffre paſſe thēne certayn aldermē comyns apoynted goo vnto bernet ſpeke wyth ye quenes cōſeyll entreate yu northren men ſholde bee ſente home ayen theyr contree cyte london drad dyſpoyled yf come duryng treatyſe tydynges came erle warwyk met erle marche cotteſwolde comyng oute walys wyth greate menye welſſhemē bothe comynge vnto lōdon warde anone theſe tytynges knowe tratyſe broke kynge quene prynce lordes theym departed fro ſaynt albōs north ward al ther people yet departed then beheeded lorde bonuyll syr thomas kryell whiche takē iourney done ſhrewe tourſdaye ¶thenne ducheſſe yorke beyng london herynge loſſe felde ſaynt albons ſente ouerſee hyr twoo yonge ſones george rycharde whiche wente vtrech phylyp malpas trollop many knyghtes ſquers ¶thenne kynge henry kyng • beynge wyth quene prynce att yorke herynge loſſe felde ſo moche peple ſlayne ouerthrowe anone forthe departed thre wyth duke somerſet lorde roos towarde scotlande nexte daye kynge edward armye entred yorke ther proclaymyd kynge obeyed ought mayre comyns ſwore lyegemen whan taryed whyle northe north al north countree torned hym retorned ſouth warde leuynge behynde hym erle werwyk tho partyes gouerne rule countre aboute mydſomer yere lorde mcccclx fyrſte yere hys regne crowned att weſtm̄ anoynted kīge englōde hauyng poſſeſſyō al ye reame calyxtus ye thyrde pope nycholas thre yere v monethes calyxte olde mā whā choſe pope cōtynually ſeke ne myght fulfyll deſyre entēded ayēſt ye turkys deth came vpō hym choſe ye yere lord mcccclv deyed ye vi daye made ye fyguracyō alſo canonyſed ſaynt vī cēt frere precher ther grete reformacyō many monaſteryes ye worlde thoſe reformacyons made many tymes moſt none abode ye retorned ayen home ſucceſſyō tyme ye dethe worſhypfull faders· ye feſte tranſfiguracyō ordeyned calyxt ye yefte grace ye merueylous vyctory done ayēſt turke hū gary ſaynt syxtus day mcccclvii merueylous vyctory yeue ye cryſtē mē hungary ayēſt greate turke loſte many mā fledde ſhāfully drede enemyes noman folowed hym alone ye hōde god feryd ye turke hooſt ſaynt calyxte daye ſaynt iohn̄ de capryſtrano ſeen preſēt prouoked people yt aferde folow myſbeleuīge turkes fell grete vēgeaūce theym turkes ſayd yt ſo grete nō bre knyghtes folowed thē vnnethe durſte looke bacwarde therfore fledde lefte al ther treſour behynde thē angelles cauſed theym flee nota prynters bookes myghtely multyplyed maguncie thrughoute worlde began fyrſte· helde theyr craftes thys tyme myny mē begā ſubtyll craftes conaccia halowed ſaynt brandon yt hath myſe dede bodyes ben buryed bē kept erth roten mamonia wel yt waſſheth hym water ye welle ſhall waxe hore heed wel vltonia ſomeuer waſſhē therin ſhall neuer ſtynke dyde wronge ſhall ſtert wythoute wretche myſchyef yf amendes ¶r touchynge patryks purgatorye ye ſhalle vnderſtonde saynt patyrk abbote byſhoppe whyle prechyd irlonde laboured ſtudyed torne thylke wycked men lyued beeſtes oute euyll lyf drede paynes helle conferme hem good lyfe ſayde wolde torne ſome theim myghte knowe ſom grete paynes alſo bleſſe ſpake thenne ſaynt patryk prayed god almyghty therfore ouer lorde iheſu cryſte appyered ſaynt patryk toke hym ſtaffe ladde hȳ wylde place ſhewed hym rounde pytte derke wythin ſayde yf man repentaunce ſtable byleue wente pytte walkede therin daye nyghte ſholde ſee lorowes paynes euyll men ioye blyſſe good men thenne cryſte vanyſſhed oute patryks ſyght • ſaynt patryk arered buylded chyrche putte therin chanons reguler • ſe pytte hyght owayne 〈…〉 ſaynt patryks purgatory come agayne dwelled euer aft duryng life ī nedes thabbaye ludēſis yt thordre chyſtews tolde manye wōdres yt hadde ſeē patryks purgatorye ¶that place called patryks purgatorye ye chirche named reglis noo mā enioyned goo ye purgatorye coūſeylled yt ſholde come therin butte take vpō penaūce yf mā haue auowed beſtale wyll nedes goo therin ſhall fyrſt go comē ledethe hym ye chyrche wyth ꝓceſſyō ſhall fyftene dayes prayer faſtynge ¶of meruaylles ſayntes irlonde ca xxix gyraldꝰ maketh mynde yt mē nacyon bē angrye mē haſty take wretche while thei bē alyue ſo ſayntes halowes lond ben wretchefull ſayntes londes clerkes lōde bē chaſte ſayē many prayes done grete abſtynēce daye drynketh nyghte ſo afoūted myracle ye lechery regneth wyne regneth ben choſen abbayes clergye done monkes ſholde whate yt bē euyll thē bē worſte al good mē amonge theym thoughe bē fewe good ye beſte prelate coūtree bē full ſlowe correccyō treſpas beſy contemplacyn notte prechynge goddes worde therfore yt sayntes ye londe cōfeſſours noo martyr amōge thē noo wōder ye prelate londe clerkes prelate ſholde doo thē vnknowē therfore whā put ayēſte ye byſſhoppe caſſyl myghte yt ſoo many ſayntes bē irlonde neuer martyr amonge theym ſythen ye mē ben ſo ſhrewed ſo angry prelate ſo rycheles ſl • correccyons treſpas byſſhop anſwered frowardely ynoughe ſayde oure men bē ſhrewed angry ynoughe thēſelfe goddes ſeruaūtes leye neuer honde hē greate reuerence worſhyp englyſſh mē come londe cā make martyr wont vſe ye crafte ¶r byſſhop ſayd ſo bycauſe ye kynge henry ye ſecōde newe comē irlonde frenſſhly ye martyrdome ſaynt thomas caūterbury gir lōde wale scotlond bē belle ſtaues croked hedes ſuche thynges relyques greate reuerēce worſhyp soo ye mē lōde dreden ſwere vpō one thylke belle golde ſtaues thā vpō ye goſpell chyfe ſuche relyques holdē ihūs ſtaffe yt atte deuelyn yt whiche ſtaffe ſaye yt fyrſte ſaynte patryke drofe ye wormes irlōde augus de ci· dei ca vii yf mē axe howe maye dyuerſe manere beeſtes dyuerſe kynde kyndly gotē bitwene mayl female come bē ylō de no flode mē ſuppoſē ſuche beſtes ſwāme ylōdes aboute fyrſte nexte ſoo forthe el mē ſayllynge ylondes broughte wyth hē ſuche beeſtes loue hūtynge angel god almyghtes cōmaūdemēt brought ſuche beſtes ylō de aboute ye erthe brought thē ye fyrſte fulfylled tho goddes cōmaūdemēte ye cōmaun ded ye erthe brynge forth gras quicke beſtes ¶here endeth ye deſcrypcyō brytayne whiche cōteyned englōde wale scotlonde alſo bycauſe irlōde vnd ye rule englō de olde tyme hathe ſo cōtynued therfore haue ſette ye deſcrypcyō ſame aft ye ſayd brytayne whiche haue takē poly cronycon alſo enprynted one ſomtyme ſco • e mayſter ſaynt
